Compiler-Shaped Lattice Fixture

This page uses the existing compiler_structure_kind_subbed.lattice fixture, rendered through the observable runner. It is the closest current DSL description to the compiler's mode/product structure.

Locality = [ Global < Local ] Regionality = [ Global < Regional < Local ] Uniqueness = [ Aliased > Unique ] Linearity = [ Many < Once ] Portability = [ Portable < Shareable < Nonportable ] Contention = [ Contended > Shared > Uncontended ] Forkable = [ Forkable < Unforkable ] Yielding = [ Unyielding < Yielding ] Staticity = [ Dynamic > Static ] Statefulness = [ Stateless < Writing < Stateful; Stateless < Reading < Stateful ] Visibility = [ Immutable > Read > Read_write; Immutable > Write > Read_write ] Externality = [ External_ < External64 < Internal ] Nullability = [ Non_null < Maybe_null ] Separability = [ Non_float < Separable < Maybe_separable ] Pointerness = [ Non_pointer < Maybe_pointer ] Locality <= Regionality via { Global -> Global; Local -> Local; } aliases { embed = Locality_as_regionality; left1 = Regional_to_local; right1 = Regional_to_global; left2 = Local_to_regional; right2 = Global_to_regional; } Monadic = { uniqueness : Uniqueness; contention : Contention; visibility : Visibility; staticity : Staticity; } Comonadic = { linearity : Linearity; portability : Portability; forkable : Forkable; yielding : Yielding; statefulness : Statefulness; } Comonadic_with_locality = { areality : Locality; comonadic : Comonadic; } Comonadic_with_regionality = { areality : Regionality; comonadic : Comonadic; } Value = { comonadic : Comonadic_with_regionality; monadic : Monadic; } Alloc = { comonadic : Comonadic_with_locality; monadic : Monadic; } Scannable_axes = { externality : Externality; nullability : Nullability; separability : Separability; pointerness : Pointerness; } Kind_axes = { comonadic : Comonadic_with_locality; monadic : Monadic ^op; scannable : Scannable_axes; }
Compilergenerated lattice library
module Make_const_op (Base : sig
  type t
  val bottom : t
  val top : t
  val leq : t -> t -> bool
  val equal : t -> t -> bool
  val join : t -> t -> t
  val meet : t -> t -> t
  val sub : t -> t -> t
  val imply : t -> t -> t
  val pp : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
  val show : t -> string
  module Repr : sig
    val bits : int
    val mask : int
    val to_int : t -> int
    val of_int_exn : int -> t
  end
  val legacy : t
  end) = struct
  type t = Base.t
  let bottom = Base.top
  let top = Base.bottom
  let leq x y = Base.leq y x
  let equal = Base.equal
  let join = Base.meet
  let meet = Base.join
  let sub x y = Base.imply y x
  let imply x y = Base.sub y x
  let pp = Base.pp
  let show = Base.show
  module Repr = Base.Repr
  let min = bottom
  let max = top
  let le = leq
  let print = pp
  let legacy = Base.legacy
end

module Lattices_const = struct
  [@@@warning "-32-37"]
  module Locality = struct
    type t = int
    let global = 0
    let local = 1
    let bottom = 0
    let top = 1
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = x
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x land y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      zxy
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      lnot zxy land 1
    let name = function
      | 0 -> "Global"
      | 1 -> "Local"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let of_name = function
      | "Global" -> Some global
      | "Local" -> Some local
      | _ -> None
    let pp ppf = function
      | 0 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Global"
      | 1 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Local"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 1
      let mask = 1
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp
    let legacy = global
  end

  module Locality_op = struct
    include Make_const_op (Locality)
    let global = Locality.global
    let local = Locality.local
    let name = Locality.name
    let of_name = Locality.of_name
  end

  module Regionality = struct
    type t = int
    let global = 0
    let regional = 1
    let local = 3
    let[@inline] close_down_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 2) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 1) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 0
    let top = 3
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = x
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x land y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      close_down_nat zxy
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      lnot (close_up_nat zxy) land 3
    let name = function
      | 0 -> "Global"
      | 1 -> "Regional"
      | 3 -> "Local"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let of_name = function
      | "Global" -> Some global
      | "Regional" -> Some regional
      | "Local" -> Some local
      | _ -> None
    let pp ppf = function
      | 0 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Global"
      | 1 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Regional"
      | 3 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Local"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 2
      let mask = 3
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let[@inline] close_repr x =
        let x = x lor ((x land 2) lsr 1) in
        x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp
    let legacy = global
  end

  module Regionality_op = struct
    include Make_const_op (Regionality)
    let global = Regionality.global
    let regional = Regionality.regional
    let local = Regionality.local
    let name = Regionality.name
    let of_name = Regionality.of_name
  end

  module Uniqueness = struct

  module Contention = struct
    type t = int
    let contended = 0
    let shared = 1
    let uncontended = 3
    let[@inline] close_down_dual x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 2) lsr 1) in

    let[@inline] close_up_dual x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 1) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 3
    let top = 0

      let zyx = y land lnot x in
      lnot (close_up_dual zyx) land 3
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zyx = y land lnot x in
      close_down_dual zyx
    let name = function
      | 0 -> "Contended"
      | 1 -> "Shared"
      | 3 -> "Uncontended"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let of_name = function
      | "Contended" -> Some contended

    include Make_const_op (Externality)
    let external_ = Externality.external_
    let external64 = Externality.external64
    let internal = Externality.internal
    let name = Externality.name
    let of_name = Externality.of_name
  end

  module Nullability = struct
    type t = int
    let non_null = 0
    let maybe_null = 1
    let bottom = 0
    let top = 1
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = x
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x land y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      zxy
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      lnot zxy land 1
    let name = function
      | 0 -> "Non_null"
      | 1 -> "Maybe_null"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let of_name = function
      | "Non_null" -> Some non_null
      | "Maybe_null" -> Some maybe_null
      | _ -> None
    let pp ppf = function
      | 0 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Non_null"
      | 1 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Maybe_null"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 1
      let mask = 1
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp
    let legacy = top
  end

  module Nullability_op = struct
    include Make_const_op (Nullability)
    let non_null = Nullability.non_null
    let maybe_null = Nullability.maybe_null
    let name = Nullability.name
    let of_name = Nullability.of_name
  end

  module Separability = struct
    type t = int
    let non_float = 0
    let separable = 1
    let maybe_separable = 3
    let[@inline] close_down_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 2) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 1) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 0
    let top = 3
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = x
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x land y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      close_down_nat zxy
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      lnot (close_up_nat zxy) land 3
    let name = function
      | 0 -> "Non_float"
      | 1 -> "Separable"
      | 3 -> "Maybe_separable"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let of_name = function
      | "Non_float" -> Some non_float
      | "Separable" -> Some separable
      | "Maybe_separable" -> Some maybe_separable
      | _ -> None
    let pp ppf = function
      | 0 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Non_float"
      | 1 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Separable"
      | 3 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Maybe_separable"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 2
      let mask = 3
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let[@inline] close_repr x =
        let x = x lor ((x land 2) lsr 1) in
        x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp
    let legacy = top
  end

  module Separability_op = struct
    include Make_const_op (Separability)
    let non_float = Separability.non_float
    let separable = Separability.separable
    let maybe_separable = Separability.maybe_separable
    let name = Separability.name
    let of_name = Separability.of_name
  end

  module Pointerness = struct
    type t = int
    let non_pointer = 0
    let maybe_pointer = 1
    let bottom = 0
    let top = 1
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = x
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x land y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      zxy
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in

    let name = function
      | 0 -> "Non_pointer"
      | 1 -> "Maybe_pointer"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let of_name = function
      | "Non_pointer" -> Some non_pointer
      | "Maybe_pointer" -> Some maybe_pointer
      | _ -> None
    let pp ppf = function
      | 0 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Non_pointer"
      | 1 -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "Maybe_pointer"
      | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t

  module Pointerness_op = struct
    include Make_const_op (Pointerness)
    let non_pointer = Pointerness.non_pointer
    let maybe_pointer = Pointerness.maybe_pointer
    let name = Pointerness.name
    let of_name = Pointerness.of_name
  end

  module Monadic = struct
    module Field_Uniqueness = Uniqueness
    module Field_Contention = Contention
    module Field_Visibility = Visibility
    module Field_Staticity = Staticity
    type t = int
    type view = {
      uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.t;
      contention : Field_Contention.t;
      visibility : Field_Visibility.t;
      staticity : Field_Staticity.t;
    }

    module Layout = struct
      let uniqueness_shift = 0
      let uniqueness_mask = 1
      let contention_shift = 1
      let contention_mask = 6
      let visibility_shift = 3
      let visibility_mask = 24
      let staticity_shift = 5
      let staticity_mask = 32
    end
    let[@inline] make ~uniqueness ~contention ~visibility ~staticity =
      uniqueness lor (contention lsl 1) lor (visibility lsl 3) lor (staticity lsl 5)
    let[@inline] uniqueness t = (t land 1 : Field_Uniqueness.t)
    let proj_uniqueness = uniqueness
    let[@inline] with_uniqueness value t = (t land lnot Layout.uniqueness_mask) lor value
    let[@inline] contention t = ((t lsr 1) land 3 : Field_Contention.t)
    let proj_contention = contention
    let[@inline] with_contention value t = (t land lnot Layout.contention_mask) lor (value lsl 1)
    let[@inline] visibility t = ((t lsr 3) land 3 : Field_Visibility.t)
    let proj_visibility = visibility
    let[@inline] with_visibility value t = (t land lnot Layout.visibility_mask) lor (value lsl 3)
    let[@inline] staticity t = ((t lsr 5) land 1 : Field_Staticity.t)
    let proj_staticity = staticity
    let[@inline] with_staticity value t = (t land lnot Layout.staticity_mask) lor (value lsl 5)
    let[@inline] of_view view =
      make ~uniqueness:view.uniqueness ~contention:view.contention ~visibility:view.visibility ~staticity:view.staticity 
    let[@inline] view t =
      {
        uniqueness = uniqueness t;
        contention = contention t;
        visibility = visibility t;
        staticity = staticity t;
      }
    let[@inline] close_down_dual x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 4) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_dual x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 2) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 63
    let top = 0
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = y
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x land y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zyx = y land lnot x in
      lnot (close_up_dual zyx) land 63
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zyx = y land lnot x in
      close_down_dual zyx
    let[@inline] uniqueness_bot value = with_uniqueness value bottom
    let[@inline] uniqueness_top value = with_uniqueness value top
    let min_with_uniqueness = uniqueness_bot
    let max_with_uniqueness = uniqueness_top
    let[@inline] contention_bot value = with_contention value bottom
    let[@inline] contention_top value = with_contention value top
    let min_with_contention = contention_bot
    let max_with_contention = contention_top
    let[@inline] visibility_bot value = with_visibility value bottom
    let[@inline] visibility_top value = with_visibility value top
    let min_with_visibility = visibility_bot
    let max_with_visibility = visibility_top
    let[@inline] staticity_bot value = with_staticity value bottom
    let[@inline] staticity_top value = with_staticity value top
    let min_with_staticity = staticity_bot
    let max_with_staticity = staticity_top
    let pp ppf t =
      let v = view t in
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "{ ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "uniqueness = ";
      Field_Uniqueness.pp ppf v.uniqueness;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "contention = ";
      Field_Contention.pp ppf v.contention;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "visibility = ";
      Field_Visibility.pp ppf v.visibility;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "staticity = ";
      Field_Staticity.pp ppf v.staticity;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf " }"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 6
      let mask = 63
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let[@inline] close_repr x =
        let x = x lor ((x land 4) lsr 1) in
        x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp

    let split = view
    let merge = of_view

    let legacy =
      make ~uniqueness:Field_Uniqueness.legacy ~contention:Field_Contention.legacy ~visibility:Field_Visibility.legacy ~staticity:Field_Staticity.legacy 
    module Axis = struct
      type _ t =
        | Uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.t t
        | Contention : Field_Contention.t t
        | Visibility : Field_Visibility.t t
        | Staticity : Field_Staticity.t t

      type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

      let compare : type a b. a t -> b t -> (a, b) Misc.comparison =
        fun left right ->
          match left, right with
          | Uniqueness, Uniqueness -> Misc.Equal
          | Uniqueness, Contention -> Misc.Less_than
          | Uniqueness, Visibility -> Misc.Less_than
          | Uniqueness, Staticity -> Misc.Less_than
          | Contention, Contention -> Misc.Equal
          | Contention, Uniqueness -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Contention, Visibility -> Misc.Less_than
          | Contention, Staticity -> Misc.Less_than
          | Visibility, Visibility -> Misc.Equal
          | Visibility, Uniqueness -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Visibility, Contention -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Visibility, Staticity -> Misc.Less_than
          | Staticity, Staticity -> Misc.Equal
          | Staticity, Uniqueness -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Staticity, Contention -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Staticity, Visibility -> Misc.Greater_than

      let all = [
        P Uniqueness;
        P Contention;
        P Visibility;
        P Staticity;
      ]
      let print : type a. Format.formatter -> a t -> unit = fun ppf -> function
        | Uniqueness -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "uniqueness"
        | Contention -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "contention"
        | Visibility -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "visibility"
        | Staticity -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "staticity"
      let proj : type a. a t -> int -> a = fun axis t ->
        match axis with
        | Uniqueness -> uniqueness t
        | Contention -> contention t
        | Visibility -> visibility t
        | Staticity -> staticity t
      let set : type a. a t -> a -> int -> int = fun axis value t ->
        match axis with
        | Uniqueness -> with_uniqueness value t
        | Contention -> with_contention value t
        | Visibility -> with_visibility value t
        | Staticity -> with_staticity value t
      let min_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Uniqueness -> uniqueness_bot value
        | Contention -> contention_bot value
        | Visibility -> visibility_bot value
        | Staticity -> staticity_bot value
      let max_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Uniqueness -> uniqueness_top value
        | Contention -> contention_top value
        | Visibility -> visibility_top value
        | Staticity -> staticity_top value
      let _ = set
    end

    let proj = Axis.proj
    let min_with = Axis.min_with
    let max_with = Axis.max_with
  end

  module Monadic_op = struct
    module Field_Uniqueness = Uniqueness_op
    module Field_Contention = Contention_op
    module Field_Visibility = Visibility_op
    module Field_Staticity = Staticity_op
    include Make_const_op (Monadic)
    type view = Monadic.view = {
      uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.t;
      contention : Field_Contention.t;
      visibility : Field_Visibility.t;
      staticity : Field_Staticity.t;
    }

    module Layout = Monadic.Layout
    module Axis = Monadic.Axis
    let make = Monadic.make
    let view = Monadic.view
    let of_view = Monadic.of_view
    let uniqueness = Monadic.uniqueness
    let proj_uniqueness = Monadic.proj_uniqueness
    let with_uniqueness = Monadic.with_uniqueness
    let uniqueness_bot = Monadic.uniqueness_bot
    let uniqueness_top = Monadic.uniqueness_top
    let min_with_uniqueness = Monadic.min_with_uniqueness
    let max_with_uniqueness = Monadic.max_with_uniqueness
    let contention = Monadic.contention
    let proj_contention = Monadic.proj_contention
    let with_contention = Monadic.with_contention
    let contention_bot = Monadic.contention_bot
    let contention_top = Monadic.contention_top
    let min_with_contention = Monadic.min_with_contention
    let max_with_contention = Monadic.max_with_contention
    let visibility = Monadic.visibility
    let proj_visibility = Monadic.proj_visibility
    let with_visibility = Monadic.with_visibility
    let visibility_bot = Monadic.visibility_bot
    let visibility_top = Monadic.visibility_top
    let min_with_visibility = Monadic.min_with_visibility
    let max_with_visibility = Monadic.max_with_visibility
    let staticity = Monadic.staticity
    let proj_staticity = Monadic.proj_staticity
    let with_staticity = Monadic.with_staticity
    let staticity_bot = Monadic.staticity_bot
    let staticity_top = Monadic.staticity_top
    let min_with_staticity = Monadic.min_with_staticity
    let max_with_staticity = Monadic.max_with_staticity
    let split = Monadic.split
    let merge = Monadic.merge
    let proj = Monadic.proj
    let min_with = Monadic.min_with
    let max_with = Monadic.max_with
  end

  module Comonadic = struct
    module Field_Linearity = Linearity
    module Field_Portability = Portability
    module Field_Forkable = Forkable
    module Field_Yielding = Yielding
    module Field_Statefulness = Statefulness
    type t = int
    type view = {
      linearity : Field_Linearity.t;
      portability : Field_Portability.t;
      forkable : Field_Forkable.t;
      yielding : Field_Yielding.t;
      statefulness : Field_Statefulness.t;
    }

    module Layout = struct
      let linearity_shift = 0
      let linearity_mask = 1
      let portability_shift = 1
      let portability_mask = 6
      let forkable_shift = 3
      let forkable_mask = 8
      let yielding_shift = 4
      let yielding_mask = 16
      let statefulness_shift = 5
      let statefulness_mask = 96
    end
    let[@inline] make ~linearity ~portability ~forkable ~yielding ~statefulness =
      linearity lor (portability lsl 1) lor (forkable lsl 3) lor (yielding lsl 4) lor (statefulness lsl 5)
    let[@inline] linearity t = (t land 1 : Field_Linearity.t)
    let proj_linearity = linearity
    let[@inline] with_linearity value t = (t land lnot Layout.linearity_mask) lor value
    let[@inline] portability t = ((t lsr 1) land 3 : Field_Portability.t)
    let proj_portability = portability
    let[@inline] with_portability value t = (t land lnot Layout.portability_mask) lor (value lsl 1)
    let[@inline] forkable t = ((t lsr 3) land 1 : Field_Forkable.t)
    let proj_forkable = forkable
    let[@inline] with_forkable value t = (t land lnot Layout.forkable_mask) lor (value lsl 3)
    let[@inline] yielding t = ((t lsr 4) land 1 : Field_Yielding.t)
    let proj_yielding = yielding
    let[@inline] with_yielding value t = (t land lnot Layout.yielding_mask) lor (value lsl 4)
    let[@inline] statefulness t = ((t lsr 5) land 3 : Field_Statefulness.t)
    let proj_statefulness = statefulness
    let[@inline] with_statefulness value t = (t land lnot Layout.statefulness_mask) lor (value lsl 5)
    let[@inline] of_view view =
      make ~linearity:view.linearity ~portability:view.portability ~forkable:view.forkable ~yielding:view.yielding ~statefulness:view.statefulness 
    let[@inline] view t =
      {
        linearity = linearity t;
        portability = portability t;
        forkable = forkable t;
        yielding = yielding t;
        statefulness = statefulness t;
      }
    let[@inline] close_down_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 4) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 2) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 0
    let top = 127
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = x
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x land y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      close_down_nat zxy
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      lnot (close_up_nat zxy) land 127
    let[@inline] linearity_bot value = with_linearity value bottom
    let[@inline] linearity_top value = with_linearity value top
    let min_with_linearity = linearity_bot
    let max_with_linearity = linearity_top
    let[@inline] portability_bot value = with_portability value bottom
    let[@inline] portability_top value = with_portability value top
    let min_with_portability = portability_bot
    let max_with_portability = portability_top
    let[@inline] forkable_bot value = with_forkable value bottom
    let[@inline] forkable_top value = with_forkable value top
    let min_with_forkable = forkable_bot
    let max_with_forkable = forkable_top
    let[@inline] yielding_bot value = with_yielding value bottom
    let[@inline] yielding_top value = with_yielding value top
    let min_with_yielding = yielding_bot
    let max_with_yielding = yielding_top
    let[@inline] statefulness_bot value = with_statefulness value bottom
    let[@inline] statefulness_top value = with_statefulness value top
    let min_with_statefulness = statefulness_bot
    let max_with_statefulness = statefulness_top
    let pp ppf t =
      let v = view t in
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "{ ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "linearity = ";
      Field_Linearity.pp ppf v.linearity;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "portability = ";
      Field_Portability.pp ppf v.portability;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "forkable = ";
      Field_Forkable.pp ppf v.forkable;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "yielding = ";
      Field_Yielding.pp ppf v.yielding;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "statefulness = ";
      Field_Statefulness.pp ppf v.statefulness;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf " }"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 7
      let mask = 127
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let[@inline] close_repr x =
        let x = x lor ((x land 4) lsr 1) in
        x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp

    let split = view
    let merge = of_view

    let legacy =
      make ~linearity:Field_Linearity.legacy ~portability:Field_Portability.legacy ~forkable:Field_Forkable.legacy ~yielding:Field_Yielding.legacy ~statefulness:Field_Statefulness.legacy 
    module Axis = struct
      type _ t =
        | Linearity : Field_Linearity.t t
        | Portability : Field_Portability.t t
        | Forkable : Field_Forkable.t t
        | Yielding : Field_Yielding.t t
        | Statefulness : Field_Statefulness.t t

      type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

      let compare : type a b. a t -> b t -> (a, b) Misc.comparison =
        fun left right ->
          match left, right with
          | Linearity, Linearity -> Misc.Equal
          | Linearity, Portability -> Misc.Less_than
          | Linearity, Forkable -> Misc.Less_than
          | Linearity, Yielding -> Misc.Less_than
          | Linearity, Statefulness -> Misc.Less_than
          | Portability, Portability -> Misc.Equal
          | Portability, Linearity -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Portability, Forkable -> Misc.Less_than
          | Portability, Yielding -> Misc.Less_than
          | Portability, Statefulness -> Misc.Less_than
          | Forkable, Forkable -> Misc.Equal
          | Forkable, Linearity -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Forkable, Portability -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Forkable, Yielding -> Misc.Less_than
          | Forkable, Statefulness -> Misc.Less_than
          | Yielding, Yielding -> Misc.Equal
          | Yielding, Linearity -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Yielding, Portability -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Yielding, Forkable -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Yielding, Statefulness -> Misc.Less_than
          | Statefulness, Statefulness -> Misc.Equal
          | Statefulness, Linearity -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Statefulness, Portability -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Statefulness, Forkable -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Statefulness, Yielding -> Misc.Greater_than

      let all = [
        P Linearity;
        P Portability;
        P Forkable;
        P Yielding;
        P Statefulness;
      ]
      let print : type a. Format.formatter -> a t -> unit = fun ppf -> function
        | Linearity -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "linearity"
        | Portability -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "portability"
        | Forkable -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "forkable"
        | Yielding -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "yielding"
        | Statefulness -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "statefulness"
      let proj : type a. a t -> int -> a = fun axis t ->
        match axis with
        | Linearity -> linearity t
        | Portability -> portability t
        | Forkable -> forkable t
        | Yielding -> yielding t
        | Statefulness -> statefulness t
      let set : type a. a t -> a -> int -> int = fun axis value t ->
        match axis with
        | Linearity -> with_linearity value t
        | Portability -> with_portability value t
        | Forkable -> with_forkable value t
        | Yielding -> with_yielding value t
        | Statefulness -> with_statefulness value t
      let min_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Linearity -> linearity_bot value
        | Portability -> portability_bot value
        | Forkable -> forkable_bot value
        | Yielding -> yielding_bot value
        | Statefulness -> statefulness_bot value
      let max_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Linearity -> linearity_top value
        | Portability -> portability_top value
        | Forkable -> forkable_top value
        | Yielding -> yielding_top value
        | Statefulness -> statefulness_top value
      let _ = set
    end

    let proj = Axis.proj
    let min_with = Axis.min_with
    let max_with = Axis.max_with
  end

  module Comonadic_op = struct
    module Field_Linearity = Linearity_op
    module Field_Portability = Portability_op
    module Field_Forkable = Forkable_op
    module Field_Yielding = Yielding_op
    module Field_Statefulness = Statefulness_op
    include Make_const_op (Comonadic)
    type view = Comonadic.view = {
      linearity : Field_Linearity.t;
      portability : Field_Portability.t;
      forkable : Field_Forkable.t;
      yielding : Field_Yielding.t;
      statefulness : Field_Statefulness.t;
    }

    module Layout = Comonadic.Layout
    module Axis = Comonadic.Axis
    let make = Comonadic.make
    let view = Comonadic.view
    let of_view = Comonadic.of_view
    let linearity = Comonadic.linearity
    let proj_linearity = Comonadic.proj_linearity
    let with_linearity = Comonadic.with_linearity
    let linearity_bot = Comonadic.linearity_bot
    let linearity_top = Comonadic.linearity_top
    let min_with_linearity = Comonadic.min_with_linearity
    let max_with_linearity = Comonadic.max_with_linearity
    let portability = Comonadic.portability
    let proj_portability = Comonadic.proj_portability
    let with_portability = Comonadic.with_portability
    let portability_bot = Comonadic.portability_bot
    let portability_top = Comonadic.portability_top
    let min_with_portability = Comonadic.min_with_portability
    let max_with_portability = Comonadic.max_with_portability
    let forkable = Comonadic.forkable
    let proj_forkable = Comonadic.proj_forkable
    let with_forkable = Comonadic.with_forkable
    let forkable_bot = Comonadic.forkable_bot
    let forkable_top = Comonadic.forkable_top
    let min_with_forkable = Comonadic.min_with_forkable
    let max_with_forkable = Comonadic.max_with_forkable
    let yielding = Comonadic.yielding
    let proj_yielding = Comonadic.proj_yielding
    let with_yielding = Comonadic.with_yielding
    let yielding_bot = Comonadic.yielding_bot
    let yielding_top = Comonadic.yielding_top
    let min_with_yielding = Comonadic.min_with_yielding
    let max_with_yielding = Comonadic.max_with_yielding
    let statefulness = Comonadic.statefulness
    let proj_statefulness = Comonadic.proj_statefulness
    let with_statefulness = Comonadic.with_statefulness
    let statefulness_bot = Comonadic.statefulness_bot
    let statefulness_top = Comonadic.statefulness_top
    let min_with_statefulness = Comonadic.min_with_statefulness
    let max_with_statefulness = Comonadic.max_with_statefulness
    let split = Comonadic.split
    let merge = Comonadic.merge
    let proj = Comonadic.proj
    let min_with = Comonadic.min_with
    let max_with = Comonadic.max_with
  end

  module Comonadic_with_locality = struct
    module Field_Areality = Locality
    module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic
    type t = int
    type view = {
      areality : Field_Areality.t;
      comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t;
    }

    module Layout = struct
      let areality_shift = 0
      let areality_mask = 1
      let comonadic_shift = 1
      let comonadic_mask = 254
    end
    let[@inline] make ~areality ~comonadic =
      areality lor (comonadic lsl 1)
    let[@inline] areality t = (t land 1 : Field_Areality.t)
    let proj_areality = areality
    let[@inline] with_areality value t = (t land lnot Layout.areality_mask) lor value
    let[@inline] comonadic t = ((t lsr 1) land 127 : Field_Comonadic.t)
    let proj_comonadic = comonadic
    let[@inline] with_comonadic value t = (t land lnot Layout.comonadic_mask) lor (value lsl 1)
    let[@inline] of_view view =
      make ~areality:view.areality ~comonadic:view.comonadic 
    let[@inline] view t =
      {
        areality = areality t;
        comonadic = comonadic t;
      }
    let[@inline] close_down_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 8) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 4) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 0
    let top = 255
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = x
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x land y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      close_down_nat zxy
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      lnot (close_up_nat zxy) land 255
    let[@inline] areality_bot value = with_areality value bottom
    let[@inline] areality_top value = with_areality value top
    let min_with_areality = areality_bot
    let max_with_areality = areality_top
    let[@inline] comonadic_bot value = with_comonadic value bottom
    let[@inline] comonadic_top value = with_comonadic value top
    let min_with_comonadic = comonadic_bot
    let max_with_comonadic = comonadic_top
    let pp ppf t =
      let v = view t in
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "{ ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "areality = ";
      Field_Areality.pp ppf v.areality;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic = ";
      Field_Comonadic.pp ppf v.comonadic;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf " }"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 8
      let mask = 255
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let[@inline] close_repr x =
        let x = x lor ((x land 8) lsr 1) in
        x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp

    let split = view
    let merge = of_view

    let legacy =
      make ~areality:Field_Areality.legacy ~comonadic:Field_Comonadic.legacy 
    module Axis = struct
      type _ t =
        | Areality : Field_Areality.t t
        | Comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t t

      type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

      let compare : type a b. a t -> b t -> (a, b) Misc.comparison =
        fun left right ->
          match left, right with
          | Areality, Areality -> Misc.Equal
          | Areality, Comonadic -> Misc.Less_than
          | Comonadic, Comonadic -> Misc.Equal
          | Comonadic, Areality -> Misc.Greater_than

      let all = [
        P Areality;
        P Comonadic;
      ]
      let print : type a. Format.formatter -> a t -> unit = fun ppf -> function
        | Areality -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "areality"
        | Comonadic -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic"
      let proj : type a. a t -> int -> a = fun axis t ->
        match axis with
        | Areality -> areality t
        | Comonadic -> comonadic t
      let set : type a. a t -> a -> int -> int = fun axis value t ->
        match axis with
        | Areality -> with_areality value t
        | Comonadic -> with_comonadic value t
      let min_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Areality -> areality_bot value
        | Comonadic -> comonadic_bot value
      let max_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Areality -> areality_top value
        | Comonadic -> comonadic_top value
      let _ = set
    end

    let proj = Axis.proj
    let min_with = Axis.min_with
    let max_with = Axis.max_with
  end

  module Comonadic_with_locality_op = struct
    module Field_Areality = Locality_op
    module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_op
    include Make_const_op (Comonadic_with_locality)
    type view = Comonadic_with_locality.view = {

    module Layout = Comonadic_with_locality.Layout

    let make = Comonadic_with_locality.make

    let areality = Comonadic_with_locality.areality
    let proj_areality = Comonadic_with_locality.proj_areality
    let with_areality = Comonadic_with_locality.with_areality
    let areality_bot = Comonadic_with_locality.areality_bot
    let areality_top = Comonadic_with_locality.areality_top
    let min_with_areality = Comonadic_with_locality.min_with_areality
    let max_with_areality = Comonadic_with_locality.max_with_areality
    let comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.comonadic
    let proj_comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.proj_comonadic
    let with_comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.with_comonadic
    let comonadic_bot = Comonadic_with_locality.comonadic_bot
    let comonadic_top = Comonadic_with_locality.comonadic_top
    let min_with_comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.min_with_comonadic
    let max_with_comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.max_with_comonadic
    let split = Comonadic_with_locality.split
    let merge = Comonadic_with_locality.merge

    let min_with = Comonadic_with_locality.min_with
    let max_with = Comonadic_with_locality.max_with
  end

  module Comonadic_with_regionality = struct
    module Field_Areality = Regionality
    module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic
    type t = int
    type view = {
      areality : Field_Areality.t;
      comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t;
    }

    module Layout = struct
      let areality_shift = 0
      let areality_mask = 3
      let comonadic_shift = 2
      let comonadic_mask = 508
    end
    let[@inline] make ~areality ~comonadic =
      areality lor (comonadic lsl 2)
    let[@inline] areality t = (t land 3 : Field_Areality.t)
    let proj_areality = areality
    let[@inline] with_areality value t = (t land lnot Layout.areality_mask) lor value
    let[@inline] comonadic t = ((t lsr 2) land 127 : Field_Comonadic.t)
    let proj_comonadic = comonadic
    let[@inline] with_comonadic value t = (t land lnot Layout.comonadic_mask) lor (value lsl 2)
    let[@inline] of_view view =
      make ~areality:view.areality ~comonadic:view.comonadic 
    let[@inline] view t =
      {
        areality = areality t;
        comonadic = comonadic t;
      }
    let[@inline] close_down_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 18) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 9) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 0
    let top = 511
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = x
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x land y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      close_down_nat zxy
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      lnot (close_up_nat zxy) land 511
    let[@inline] areality_bot value = with_areality value bottom
    let[@inline] areality_top value = with_areality value top
    let min_with_areality = areality_bot
    let max_with_areality = areality_top
    let[@inline] comonadic_bot value = with_comonadic value bottom
    let[@inline] comonadic_top value = with_comonadic value top
    let min_with_comonadic = comonadic_bot
    let max_with_comonadic = comonadic_top
    let pp ppf t =
      let v = view t in
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "{ ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "areality = ";
      Field_Areality.pp ppf v.areality;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic = ";
      Field_Comonadic.pp ppf v.comonadic;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf " }"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 9
      let mask = 511
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let[@inline] close_repr x =
        let x = x lor ((x land 18) lsr 1) in
        x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp

    let split = view
    let merge = of_view

    let legacy =
      make ~areality:Field_Areality.legacy ~comonadic:Field_Comonadic.legacy 
    module Axis = struct
      type _ t =
        | Areality : Field_Areality.t t
        | Comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t t

      type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

      let compare : type a b. a t -> b t -> (a, b) Misc.comparison =
        fun left right ->
          match left, right with
          | Areality, Areality -> Misc.Equal
          | Areality, Comonadic -> Misc.Less_than
          | Comonadic, Comonadic -> Misc.Equal
          | Comonadic, Areality -> Misc.Greater_than

      let all = [
        P Areality;
        P Comonadic;
      ]
      let print : type a. Format.formatter -> a t -> unit = fun ppf -> function
        | Areality -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "areality"
        | Comonadic -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic"
      let proj : type a. a t -> int -> a = fun axis t ->
        match axis with
        | Areality -> areality t
        | Comonadic -> comonadic t
      let set : type a. a t -> a -> int -> int = fun axis value t ->
        match axis with
        | Areality -> with_areality value t
        | Comonadic -> with_comonadic value t
      let min_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Areality -> areality_bot value
        | Comonadic -> comonadic_bot value
      let max_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Areality -> areality_top value
        | Comonadic -> comonadic_top value
      let _ = set
    end

    let proj = Axis.proj
    let min_with = Axis.min_with
    let max_with = Axis.max_with
  end

  module Comonadic_with_regionality_op = struct

  module Value = struct
    module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality
    module Field_Monadic = Monadic
    type t = int
    type view = {
      comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t;
      monadic : Field_Monadic.t;
    }

    module Layout = struct
      let comonadic_shift = 0
      let comonadic_mask = 511
      let monadic_shift = 9
      let monadic_mask = 32256
    end
    let[@inline] make ~comonadic ~monadic =
      comonadic lor (monadic lsl 9)
    let[@inline] comonadic t = (t land 511 : Field_Comonadic.t)
    let proj_comonadic = comonadic
    let[@inline] with_comonadic value t = (t land lnot Layout.comonadic_mask) lor value
    let[@inline] monadic t = ((t lsr 9) land 63 : Field_Monadic.t)
    let proj_monadic = monadic
    let[@inline] with_monadic value t = (t land lnot Layout.monadic_mask) lor (value lsl 9)
    let[@inline] of_view view =
      make ~comonadic:view.comonadic ~monadic:view.monadic 
    let[@inline] view t =
      {
        comonadic = comonadic t;
        monadic = monadic t;
      }
    let[@inline] close_down_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 2066) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 1033) lsl 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_down_dual x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 2066) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_dual x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 1033) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 32256
    let top = 511
    let[@inline] leq x y =
      (((x land lnot y) land 511) = 0)
      && (((y land lnot x) land 32256) = 0)
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y =
      let o = x lor y in
      let a = x land y in
      (o land 511) lor (a land 32256)
    let[@inline] meet x y =
      let o = x lor y in
      let a = x land y in
      (a land 511) lor (o land 32256)
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      let zyx = y land lnot x in
      ((close_down_nat zxy) land 511)
      lor ((lnot (close_up_dual zyx)) land 32256)
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      let zyx = y land lnot x in
      ((lnot (close_up_nat zxy)) land 511)
      lor ((close_down_dual zyx) land 32256)
    let[@inline] comonadic_bot value = with_comonadic value bottom
    let[@inline] comonadic_top value = with_comonadic value top
    let min_with_comonadic = comonadic_bot
    let max_with_comonadic = comonadic_top
    let[@inline] monadic_bot value = with_monadic value bottom
    let[@inline] monadic_top value = with_monadic value top
    let min_with_monadic = monadic_bot
    let max_with_monadic = monadic_top
    let pp ppf t =
      let v = view t in
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "{ ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic = ";
      Field_Comonadic.pp ppf v.comonadic;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "monadic = ";
      Field_Monadic.pp ppf v.monadic;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf " }"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 15
      let mask = 32767
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let[@inline] close_repr x =
        let x = x lor ((x land 2066) lsr 1) in
        x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp

    let split = view
    let merge = of_view

    let legacy =
      make ~comonadic:Field_Comonadic.legacy ~monadic:Field_Monadic.legacy 
    module Axis = struct
      type _ t =
        | Comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t t
        | Monadic : Field_Monadic.t t

      type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

      let compare : type a b. a t -> b t -> (a, b) Misc.comparison =
        fun left right ->
          match left, right with
          | Comonadic, Comonadic -> Misc.Equal
          | Comonadic, Monadic -> Misc.Less_than
          | Monadic, Monadic -> Misc.Equal
          | Monadic, Comonadic -> Misc.Greater_than

      let all = [
        P Comonadic;
        P Monadic;
      ]
      let print : type a. Format.formatter -> a t -> unit = fun ppf -> function
        | Comonadic -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic"
        | Monadic -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "monadic"
      let proj : type a. a t -> int -> a = fun axis t ->
        match axis with
        | Comonadic -> comonadic t
        | Monadic -> monadic t
      let set : type a. a t -> a -> int -> int = fun axis value t ->
        match axis with
        | Comonadic -> with_comonadic value t
        | Monadic -> with_monadic value t
      let min_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Comonadic -> comonadic_bot value
        | Monadic -> monadic_bot value
      let max_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Comonadic -> comonadic_top value
        | Monadic -> monadic_top value
      let _ = set
    end

    let proj = Axis.proj
    let min_with = Axis.min_with
    let max_with = Axis.max_with
  end

  module Value_op = struct
    module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality_op
    module Field_Monadic = Monadic_op
    include Make_const_op (Value)
    type view = Value.view = {
      comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t;
      monadic : Field_Monadic.t;

    module Layout = Value.Layout

    let make = Value.make
    let view = Value.view
    let of_view = Value.of_view
    let comonadic = Value.comonadic
    let proj_comonadic = Value.proj_comonadic
    let with_comonadic = Value.with_comonadic
    let comonadic_bot = Value.comonadic_bot
    let comonadic_top = Value.comonadic_top
    let min_with_comonadic = Value.min_with_comonadic
    let max_with_comonadic = Value.max_with_comonadic
    let monadic = Value.monadic
    let proj_monadic = Value.proj_monadic
    let with_monadic = Value.with_monadic
    let monadic_bot = Value.monadic_bot
    let monadic_top = Value.monadic_top
    let min_with_monadic = Value.min_with_monadic
    let max_with_monadic = Value.max_with_monadic
    let split = Value.split
    let merge = Value.merge
    let proj = Value.proj
    let min_with = Value.min_with
    let max_with = Value.max_with
  end

  module Alloc = struct
    module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality
    module Field_Monadic = Monadic
    type t = int
    type view = {
      comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t;
      monadic : Field_Monadic.t;
    }

    module Layout = struct
      let comonadic_shift = 0
      let comonadic_mask = 255
      let monadic_shift = 8
      let monadic_mask = 16128
    end
    let[@inline] make ~comonadic ~monadic =
      comonadic lor (monadic lsl 8)
    let[@inline] comonadic t = (t land 255 : Field_Comonadic.t)
    let proj_comonadic = comonadic
    let[@inline] with_comonadic value t = (t land lnot Layout.comonadic_mask) lor value
    let[@inline] monadic t = ((t lsr 8) land 63 : Field_Monadic.t)
    let proj_monadic = monadic
    let[@inline] with_monadic value t = (t land lnot Layout.monadic_mask) lor (value lsl 8)
    let[@inline] of_view view =
      make ~comonadic:view.comonadic ~monadic:view.monadic 
    let[@inline] view t =
      {
        comonadic = comonadic t;
        monadic = monadic t;
      }
    let[@inline] close_down_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 1032) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 516) lsl 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_down_dual x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 1032) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_dual x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 516) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 16128
    let top = 255
    let[@inline] leq x y =
      (((x land lnot y) land 255) = 0)
      && (((y land lnot x) land 16128) = 0)
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y =
      let o = x lor y in
      let a = x land y in
      (o land 255) lor (a land 16128)
    let[@inline] meet x y =
      let o = x lor y in
      let a = x land y in
      (a land 255) lor (o land 16128)
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      let zyx = y land lnot x in
      ((close_down_nat zxy) land 255)
      lor ((lnot (close_up_dual zyx)) land 16128)
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      let zyx = y land lnot x in
      ((lnot (close_up_nat zxy)) land 255)
      lor ((close_down_dual zyx) land 16128)
    let[@inline] comonadic_bot value = with_comonadic value bottom
    let[@inline] comonadic_top value = with_comonadic value top
    let min_with_comonadic = comonadic_bot
    let max_with_comonadic = comonadic_top
    let[@inline] monadic_bot value = with_monadic value bottom
    let[@inline] monadic_top value = with_monadic value top
    let min_with_monadic = monadic_bot
    let max_with_monadic = monadic_top
    let pp ppf t =
      let v = view t in
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "{ ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic = ";
      Field_Comonadic.pp ppf v.comonadic;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "monadic = ";
      Field_Monadic.pp ppf v.monadic;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf " }"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 14
      let mask = 16383
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let[@inline] close_repr x =
        let x = x lor ((x land 1032) lsr 1) in
        x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp

    let split = view
    let merge = of_view

    let legacy =
      make ~comonadic:Field_Comonadic.legacy ~monadic:Field_Monadic.legacy 
    module Axis = struct
      type _ t =
        | Comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t t
        | Monadic : Field_Monadic.t t

      type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

      let compare : type a b. a t -> b t -> (a, b) Misc.comparison =
        fun left right ->
          match left, right with
          | Comonadic, Comonadic -> Misc.Equal
          | Comonadic, Monadic -> Misc.Less_than
          | Monadic, Monadic -> Misc.Equal
          | Monadic, Comonadic -> Misc.Greater_than

      let all = [
        P Comonadic;
        P Monadic;
      ]
      let print : type a. Format.formatter -> a t -> unit = fun ppf -> function
        | Comonadic -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic"
        | Monadic -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "monadic"
      let proj : type a. a t -> int -> a = fun axis t ->
        match axis with
        | Comonadic -> comonadic t
        | Monadic -> monadic t
      let set : type a. a t -> a -> int -> int = fun axis value t ->
        match axis with
        | Comonadic -> with_comonadic value t
        | Monadic -> with_monadic value t
      let min_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Comonadic -> comonadic_bot value
        | Monadic -> monadic_bot value
      let max_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Comonadic -> comonadic_top value
        | Monadic -> monadic_top value
      let _ = set
    end

    let proj = Axis.proj
    let min_with = Axis.min_with
    let max_with = Axis.max_with
  end

  module Alloc_op = struct

    module Field_Monadic = Monadic_op

  module Scannable_axes = struct
    module Field_Externality = Externality
    module Field_Nullability = Nullability
    module Field_Separability = Separability
    module Field_Pointerness = Pointerness
    type t = int
    type view = {
      externality : Field_Externality.t;
      nullability : Field_Nullability.t;
      separability : Field_Separability.t;
      pointerness : Field_Pointerness.t;
    }

    module Layout = struct
      let externality_shift = 0
      let externality_mask = 3
      let nullability_shift = 2
      let nullability_mask = 4
      let separability_shift = 3
      let separability_mask = 24
      let pointerness_shift = 5
      let pointerness_mask = 32
    end
    let[@inline] make ~externality ~nullability ~separability ~pointerness =
      externality lor (nullability lsl 2) lor (separability lsl 3) lor (pointerness lsl 5)
    let[@inline] externality t = (t land 3 : Field_Externality.t)
    let proj_externality = externality
    let[@inline] with_externality value t = (t land lnot Layout.externality_mask) lor value
    let[@inline] nullability t = ((t lsr 2) land 1 : Field_Nullability.t)
    let proj_nullability = nullability
    let[@inline] with_nullability value t = (t land lnot Layout.nullability_mask) lor (value lsl 2)
    let[@inline] separability t = ((t lsr 3) land 3 : Field_Separability.t)
    let proj_separability = separability
    let[@inline] with_separability value t = (t land lnot Layout.separability_mask) lor (value lsl 3)
    let[@inline] pointerness t = ((t lsr 5) land 1 : Field_Pointerness.t)
    let proj_pointerness = pointerness
    let[@inline] with_pointerness value t = (t land lnot Layout.pointerness_mask) lor (value lsl 5)
    let[@inline] of_view view =
      make ~externality:view.externality ~nullability:view.nullability ~separability:view.separability ~pointerness:view.pointerness 
    let[@inline] view t =
      {
        externality = externality t;
        nullability = nullability t;
        separability = separability t;
        pointerness = pointerness t;
      }
    let[@inline] close_down_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 18) lsr 1) in
      x
    let[@inline] close_up_nat x =
      let x = x lor ((x land 9) lsl 1) in
      x
    let bottom = 0
    let top = 63
    let[@inline] leq x y = (x land y) = x
    let[@inline] equal (x : t) (y : t) = x = y
    let[@inline] join x y = x lor y
    let[@inline] meet x y = x land y
    let[@inline] sub x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      close_down_nat zxy
    let[@inline] imply x y =
      let zxy = x land lnot y in
      lnot (close_up_nat zxy) land 63
    let[@inline] externality_bot value = with_externality value bottom
    let[@inline] externality_top value = with_externality value top
    let min_with_externality = externality_bot
    let max_with_externality = externality_top
    let[@inline] nullability_bot value = with_nullability value bottom
    let[@inline] nullability_top value = with_nullability value top
    let min_with_nullability = nullability_bot
    let max_with_nullability = nullability_top
    let[@inline] separability_bot value = with_separability value bottom
    let[@inline] separability_top value = with_separability value top
    let min_with_separability = separability_bot
    let max_with_separability = separability_top
    let[@inline] pointerness_bot value = with_pointerness value bottom
    let[@inline] pointerness_top value = with_pointerness value top
    let min_with_pointerness = pointerness_bot
    let max_with_pointerness = pointerness_top
    let pp ppf t =
      let v = view t in
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "{ ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "externality = ";
      Field_Externality.pp ppf v.externality;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "nullability = ";
      Field_Nullability.pp ppf v.nullability;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "separability = ";
      Field_Separability.pp ppf v.separability;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "pointerness = ";
      Field_Pointerness.pp ppf v.pointerness;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf " }"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 6
      let mask = 63
      let to_int (x : t) = x
      let[@inline] close_repr x =
        let x = x lor ((x land 18) lsr 1) in
        x
      let of_int_exn x =
        if x land lnot mask <> 0 then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x
    end

    let min = bottom
    let max = top
    let le = leq
    let print = pp

    let split = view
    let merge = of_view

    let legacy =
      make ~externality:Field_Externality.legacy ~nullability:Field_Nullability.legacy ~separability:Field_Separability.legacy ~pointerness:Field_Pointerness.legacy 
    module Axis = struct
      type _ t =
        | Externality : Field_Externality.t t
        | Nullability : Field_Nullability.t t
        | Separability : Field_Separability.t t
        | Pointerness : Field_Pointerness.t t

      type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

      let compare : type a b. a t -> b t -> (a, b) Misc.comparison =
        fun left right ->
          match left, right with
          | Externality, Externality -> Misc.Equal
          | Externality, Nullability -> Misc.Less_than
          | Externality, Separability -> Misc.Less_than
          | Externality, Pointerness -> Misc.Less_than
          | Nullability, Nullability -> Misc.Equal
          | Nullability, Externality -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Nullability, Separability -> Misc.Less_than
          | Nullability, Pointerness -> Misc.Less_than
          | Separability, Separability -> Misc.Equal
          | Separability, Externality -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Separability, Nullability -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Separability, Pointerness -> Misc.Less_than
          | Pointerness, Pointerness -> Misc.Equal
          | Pointerness, Externality -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Pointerness, Nullability -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Pointerness, Separability -> Misc.Greater_than

      let all = [
        P Externality;
        P Nullability;
        P Separability;
        P Pointerness;
      ]
      let print : type a. Format.formatter -> a t -> unit = fun ppf -> function
        | Externality -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "externality"
        | Nullability -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "nullability"
        | Separability -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "separability"
        | Pointerness -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "pointerness"
      let proj : type a. a t -> int -> a = fun axis t ->
        match axis with
        | Externality -> externality t
        | Nullability -> nullability t
        | Separability -> separability t
        | Pointerness -> pointerness t
      let set : type a. a t -> a -> int -> int = fun axis value t ->
        match axis with
        | Externality -> with_externality value t
        | Nullability -> with_nullability value t
        | Separability -> with_separability value t
        | Pointerness -> with_pointerness value t
      let min_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Externality -> externality_bot value
        | Nullability -> nullability_bot value
        | Separability -> separability_bot value
        | Pointerness -> pointerness_bot value
      let max_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Externality -> externality_top value
        | Nullability -> nullability_top value
        | Separability -> separability_top value
        | Pointerness -> pointerness_top value
      let _ = set
    end

    let proj = Axis.proj
    let min_with = Axis.min_with
    let max_with = Axis.max_with
  end

  module Kind_axes = struct
    module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality
    module Field_Monadic = Monadic_op
    module Field_Scannable = Scannable_axes
    type t = int
    type view = {
      comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t;

    module Layout = struct
      let comonadic_shift = 0
      let comonadic_mask = 255
      let monadic_shift = 8
      let monadic_mask = 16128
      let scannable_shift = 14
      let scannable_mask = 1032192
    end
    let[@inline] make ~comonadic ~monadic ~scannable =
      comonadic lor (monadic lsl 8) lor (scannable lsl 14)

    let proj_comonadic = comonadic

    let max_with_monadic = monadic_top

    let[@inline] scannable_top value = with_scannable value top
    let min_with_scannable = scannable_bot
    let max_with_scannable = scannable_top
    let pp ppf t =
      let v = view t in
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "{ ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic = ";
      Field_Comonadic.pp ppf v.comonadic;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "monadic = ";
      Field_Monadic.pp ppf v.monadic;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "; ";
      Format.pp_print_string ppf "scannable = ";
      Field_Scannable.pp ppf v.scannable;
      Format.pp_print_string ppf " }"
    let show t = Format.asprintf "%a" pp t
    module Repr = struct
      let bits = 20
      let mask = 1048575

        x
      let of_int_exn x =

        if close_repr x <> x then invalid_arg "invalid representation";
        x

    let min = bottom

    let legacy =

    module Axis = struct
      type _ t =
        | Comonadic : Field_Comonadic.t t
        | Monadic : Field_Monadic.t t
        | Scannable : Field_Scannable.t t

      type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

      let compare : type a b. a t -> b t -> (a, b) Misc.comparison =
        fun left right ->
          match left, right with
          | Comonadic, Comonadic -> Misc.Equal
          | Comonadic, Monadic -> Misc.Less_than
          | Comonadic, Scannable -> Misc.Less_than
          | Monadic, Monadic -> Misc.Equal
          | Monadic, Comonadic -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Monadic, Scannable -> Misc.Less_than
          | Scannable, Scannable -> Misc.Equal
          | Scannable, Comonadic -> Misc.Greater_than
          | Scannable, Monadic -> Misc.Greater_than

      let all = [
        P Comonadic;
        P Monadic;
        P Scannable;
      ]
      let print : type a. Format.formatter -> a t -> unit = fun ppf -> function
        | Comonadic -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "comonadic"

        | Scannable -> Format.pp_print_string ppf "scannable"
      let proj : type a. a t -> int -> a = fun axis t ->

        | Comonadic -> comonadic t
        | Monadic -> monadic t

        | Scannable -> scannable_bot value
      let max_with : type a. a t -> a -> int = fun axis value ->
        match axis with
        | Comonadic -> comonadic_top value
        | Monadic -> monadic_top value
        | Scannable -> scannable_top value
      let _ = set
    end

    let proj = Axis.proj
    let min_with = Axis.min_with
    let max_with = Axis.max_with
  end

    let split = Kind_axes.split
    let merge = Kind_axes.merge
    let proj = Kind_axes.proj
    let min_with = Kind_axes.min_with
    let max_with = Kind_axes.max_with
  end

  type _ obj =
    | Obj_Locality : Locality.t obj
    | Obj_Locality_op : Locality_op.t obj
    | Obj_Regionality : Regionality.t obj
    | Obj_Regionality_op : Regionality_op.t obj
