      | Obj_Yielding -> Yielding.sub x y
      | Obj_Yielding_op -> Yielding_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Staticity -> Staticity.sub x y
      | Obj_Staticity_op -> Staticity_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Statefulness -> Statefulness.sub x y
      | Obj_Statefulness_op -> Statefulness_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Visibility -> Visibility.sub x y
      | Obj_Visibility_op -> Visibility_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Externality -> Externality.sub x y
      | Obj_Externality_op -> Externality_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Nullability -> Nullability.sub x y
      | Obj_Nullability_op -> Nullability_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Separability -> Separability.sub x y
      | Obj_Separability_op -> Separability_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Pointerness -> Pointerness.sub x y
      | Obj_Pointerness_op -> Pointerness_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Monadic -> Monadic.sub x y
      | Obj_Monadic_op -> Monadic_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Comonadic -> Comonadic.sub x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_op -> Comonadic_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality -> Comonadic_with_locality.sub x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op -> Comonadic_with_locality_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality -> Comonadic_with_regionality.sub x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality_op -> Comonadic_with_regionality_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Value -> Value.sub x y
      | Obj_Value_op -> Value_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Alloc -> Alloc.sub x y
      | Obj_Alloc_op -> Alloc_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Scannable_axes -> Scannable_axes.sub x y
      | Obj_Scannable_axes_op -> Scannable_axes_op.sub x y
      | Obj_Kind_axes -> Kind_axes.sub x y
      | Obj_Kind_axes_op -> Kind_axes_op.sub x y

  let imply : type a. a obj -> a -> a -> a = fun obj x y ->
      match obj with
      | Obj_Locality -> Locality.imply x y
      | Obj_Locality_op -> Locality_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Regionality -> Regionality.imply x y
      | Obj_Regionality_op -> Regionality_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Uniqueness -> Uniqueness.imply x y
      | Obj_Uniqueness_op -> Uniqueness_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Linearity -> Linearity.imply x y
      | Obj_Linearity_op -> Linearity_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Portability -> Portability.imply x y
      | Obj_Portability_op -> Portability_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Contention -> Contention.imply x y
      | Obj_Contention_op -> Contention_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Forkable -> Forkable.imply x y
      | Obj_Forkable_op -> Forkable_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Yielding -> Yielding.imply x y
      | Obj_Yielding_op -> Yielding_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Staticity -> Staticity.imply x y
      | Obj_Staticity_op -> Staticity_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Statefulness -> Statefulness.imply x y
      | Obj_Statefulness_op -> Statefulness_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Visibility -> Visibility.imply x y
      | Obj_Visibility_op -> Visibility_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Externality -> Externality.imply x y
      | Obj_Externality_op -> Externality_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Nullability -> Nullability.imply x y
      | Obj_Nullability_op -> Nullability_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Separability -> Separability.imply x y
      | Obj_Separability_op -> Separability_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Pointerness -> Pointerness.imply x y
      | Obj_Pointerness_op -> Pointerness_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Monadic -> Monadic.imply x y
      | Obj_Monadic_op -> Monadic_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Comonadic -> Comonadic.imply x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_op -> Comonadic_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality -> Comonadic_with_locality.imply x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op -> Comonadic_with_locality_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality -> Comonadic_with_regionality.imply x y
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality_op -> Comonadic_with_regionality_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Value -> Value.imply x y
      | Obj_Value_op -> Value_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Alloc -> Alloc.imply x y
      | Obj_Alloc_op -> Alloc_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Scannable_axes -> Scannable_axes.imply x y
      | Obj_Scannable_axes_op -> Scannable_axes_op.imply x y
      | Obj_Kind_axes -> Kind_axes.imply x y
      | Obj_Kind_axes_op -> Kind_axes_op.imply x y

  let print : type a. a obj -> Format_doc.formatter -> a -> unit = fun obj ppf x ->
      match obj with
      | Obj_Locality -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Locality.show x)
      | Obj_Locality_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Locality_op.show x)
      | Obj_Regionality -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Regionality.show x)
      | Obj_Regionality_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Regionality_op.show x)
      | Obj_Uniqueness -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Uniqueness.show x)
      | Obj_Uniqueness_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Uniqueness_op.show x)
      | Obj_Linearity -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Linearity.show x)
      | Obj_Linearity_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Linearity_op.show x)
      | Obj_Portability -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Portability.show x)
      | Obj_Portability_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Portability_op.show x)
      | Obj_Contention -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Contention.show x)
      | Obj_Contention_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Contention_op.show x)
      | Obj_Forkable -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Forkable.show x)
      | Obj_Forkable_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Forkable_op.show x)
      | Obj_Yielding -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Yielding.show x)
      | Obj_Yielding_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Yielding_op.show x)
      | Obj_Staticity -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Staticity.show x)
      | Obj_Staticity_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Staticity_op.show x)
      | Obj_Statefulness -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Statefulness.show x)
      | Obj_Statefulness_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Statefulness_op.show x)
      | Obj_Visibility -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Visibility.show x)
      | Obj_Visibility_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Visibility_op.show x)
      | Obj_Externality -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Externality.show x)
      | Obj_Externality_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Externality_op.show x)
      | Obj_Nullability -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Nullability.show x)
      | Obj_Nullability_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Nullability_op.show x)
      | Obj_Separability -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Separability.show x)
      | Obj_Separability_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Separability_op.show x)
      | Obj_Pointerness -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Pointerness.show x)
      | Obj_Pointerness_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Pointerness_op.show x)
      | Obj_Monadic -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Monadic.show x)
      | Obj_Monadic_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Monadic_op.show x)
      | Obj_Comonadic -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Comonadic.show x)
      | Obj_Comonadic_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Comonadic_op.show x)
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Comonadic_with_locality.show x)
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Comonadic_with_locality_op.show x)
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Comonadic_with_regionality.show x)
      | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Comonadic_with_regionality_op.show x)
      | Obj_Value -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Value.show x)
      | Obj_Value_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Value_op.show x)
      | Obj_Alloc -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Alloc.show x)
      | Obj_Alloc_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Alloc_op.show x)
      | Obj_Scannable_axes -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Scannable_axes.show x)
      | Obj_Scannable_axes_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Scannable_axes_op.show x)
      | Obj_Kind_axes -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Kind_axes.show x)
      | Obj_Kind_axes_op -> Format_doc.pp_print_string ppf (Kind_axes_op.show x)

  let _ = legacy, sub, imply

  let equal_obj : type a b. a obj -> b obj -> (a, b) Misc.eq option =
   fun obj1 obj2 ->
    match obj1, obj2 with
    | Obj_Locality, Obj_Locality -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Locality_op, Obj_Locality_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Regionality, Obj_Regionality -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Regionality_op, Obj_Regionality_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Uniqueness, Obj_Uniqueness -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Uniqueness_op, Obj_Uniqueness_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Linearity, Obj_Linearity -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Linearity_op, Obj_Linearity_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Portability, Obj_Portability -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Portability_op, Obj_Portability_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Contention, Obj_Contention -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Contention_op, Obj_Contention_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Forkable, Obj_Forkable -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Forkable_op, Obj_Forkable_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Yielding, Obj_Yielding -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Yielding_op, Obj_Yielding_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Staticity, Obj_Staticity -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Staticity_op, Obj_Staticity_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Statefulness, Obj_Statefulness -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Statefulness_op, Obj_Statefulness_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Visibility, Obj_Visibility -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Visibility_op, Obj_Visibility_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Externality, Obj_Externality -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Externality_op, Obj_Externality_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Nullability, Obj_Nullability -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Nullability_op, Obj_Nullability_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Separability, Obj_Separability -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Separability_op, Obj_Separability_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Pointerness, Obj_Pointerness -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Pointerness_op, Obj_Pointerness_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Monadic, Obj_Monadic -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Monadic_op, Obj_Monadic_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Comonadic, Obj_Comonadic -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Comonadic_op, Obj_Comonadic_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality, Obj_Comonadic_with_locality -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op, Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality, Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality_op, Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Value, Obj_Value -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Value_op, Obj_Value_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Alloc, Obj_Alloc -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Alloc_op, Obj_Alloc_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Scannable_axes, Obj_Scannable_axes -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Scannable_axes_op, Obj_Scannable_axes_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Kind_axes, Obj_Kind_axes -> Some Misc.Refl
    | Obj_Kind_axes_op, Obj_Kind_axes_op -> Some Misc.Refl
    | _ -> None

  let compare_obj : type a b. a obj -> b obj -> (a, b) Misc.comparison =
   fun obj1 obj2 ->
    match equal_obj obj1 obj2 with
    | Some Misc.Refl -> Misc.Equal
    | None ->
      if obj_index obj1 < obj_index obj2 then Misc.Less_than else Misc.Greater_than

  let print_obj : type a. Format_doc.formatter -> a obj -> unit =
   fun ppf -> function
    | Obj_Locality -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Locality"
    | Obj_Locality_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Locality_op"
    | Obj_Regionality -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Regionality"
    | Obj_Regionality_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Regionality_op"
    | Obj_Uniqueness -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Uniqueness"
    | Obj_Uniqueness_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Uniqueness_op"
    | Obj_Linearity -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Linearity"
    | Obj_Linearity_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Linearity_op"
    | Obj_Portability -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Portability"
    | Obj_Portability_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Portability_op"
    | Obj_Contention -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Contention"
    | Obj_Contention_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Contention_op"
    | Obj_Forkable -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Forkable"
    | Obj_Forkable_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Forkable_op"
    | Obj_Yielding -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Yielding"
    | Obj_Yielding_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Yielding_op"
    | Obj_Staticity -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Staticity"
    | Obj_Staticity_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Staticity_op"
    | Obj_Statefulness -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Statefulness"
    | Obj_Statefulness_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Statefulness_op"
    | Obj_Visibility -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Visibility"
    | Obj_Visibility_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Visibility_op"
    | Obj_Externality -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Externality"
    | Obj_Externality_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Externality_op"
    | Obj_Nullability -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Nullability"
    | Obj_Nullability_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Nullability_op"
    | Obj_Separability -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Separability"
    | Obj_Separability_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Separability_op"
    | Obj_Pointerness -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Pointerness"
    | Obj_Pointerness_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Pointerness_op"
    | Obj_Monadic -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Monadic"
    | Obj_Monadic_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Monadic_op"
    | Obj_Comonadic -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Comonadic"
    | Obj_Comonadic_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Comonadic_op"
    | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Comonadic_with_locality"
    | Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Comonadic_with_locality_op"
    | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Comonadic_with_regionality"
    | Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Comonadic_with_regionality_op"
    | Obj_Value -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Value"
    | Obj_Value_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Value_op"
    | Obj_Alloc -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Alloc"
    | Obj_Alloc_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Alloc_op"
    | Obj_Scannable_axes -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Scannable_axes"
    | Obj_Scannable_axes_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Scannable_axes_op"
    | Obj_Kind_axes -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Kind_axes"
    | Obj_Kind_axes_op -> Format_doc.fprintf ppf "Kind_axes_op"

end

module Lattices_univ = struct
  [@@@warning "-32-37"]
  include Lattices_const
  open Allowance
  open Misc
  module Fmt = Format_doc

  type ('a, 'b, 'd) morph =
    | Id : ('a, 'a, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness : (Uniqueness.t, Monadic.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Monadic_Uniqueness : (Uniqueness.t, Monadic.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Monadic_Uniqueness : (Uniqueness.t, Monadic.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Monadic_Contention : (Contention.t, Monadic.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Monadic_Contention : (Contention.t, Monadic.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Monadic_Contention : (Contention.t, Monadic.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Monadic_Visibility : (Visibility.t, Monadic.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Monadic_Visibility : (Visibility.t, Monadic.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Monadic_Visibility : (Visibility.t, Monadic.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Monadic_Staticity : (Staticity.t, Monadic.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Monadic_Staticity : (Staticity.t, Monadic.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Monadic_Staticity : (Staticity.t, Monadic.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Uniqueness : (Uniqueness_op.t, Monadic_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness : (Uniqueness_op.t, Monadic_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness : (Uniqueness_op.t, Monadic_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Contention : (Contention_op.t, Monadic_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Contention : (Contention_op.t, Monadic_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Contention : (Contention_op.t, Monadic_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Visibility : (Visibility_op.t, Monadic_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Visibility : (Visibility_op.t, Monadic_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Visibility : (Visibility_op.t, Monadic_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Staticity : (Staticity_op.t, Monadic_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Staticity : (Staticity_op.t, Monadic_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Staticity : (Staticity_op.t, Monadic_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_Linearity : (Linearity.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Linearity : (Linearity.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Linearity : (Linearity.t, Comonadic.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_Portability : (Portability.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Portability : (Portability.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Portability : (Portability.t, Comonadic.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_Forkable : (Forkable.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Forkable : (Forkable.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Forkable : (Forkable.t, Comonadic.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_Yielding : (Yielding.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Yielding : (Yielding.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Yielding : (Yielding.t, Comonadic.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_Statefulness : (Statefulness.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Statefulness : (Statefulness.t, Comonadic.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Statefulness : (Statefulness.t, Comonadic.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Linearity : (Linearity_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_op_Linearity : (Linearity_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_op_Linearity : (Linearity_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Portability : (Portability_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_op_Portability : (Portability_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_op_Portability : (Portability_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Forkable : (Forkable_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_op_Forkable : (Forkable_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_op_Forkable : (Forkable_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Yielding : (Yielding_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_op_Yielding : (Yielding_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_op_Yielding : (Yielding_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Statefulness : (Statefulness_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_op_Statefulness : (Statefulness_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_op_Statefulness : (Statefulness_op.t, Comonadic_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_Areality : (Locality.t, Comonadic_with_locality.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Areality : (Locality.t, Comonadic_with_locality.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Areality : (Locality.t, Comonadic_with_locality.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_Comonadic : (Comonadic.t, Comonadic_with_locality.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Comonadic : (Comonadic.t, Comonadic_with_locality.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Comonadic : (Comonadic.t, Comonadic_with_locality.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Areality : (Locality_op.t, Comonadic_with_locality_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph

    | Proj_Kind_axes_op_Scannable : (Scannable_axes_op.t, Kind_axes_op.t, 'l * 'r) morph
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable : (Scannable_axes_op.t, Kind_axes_op.t, 'l * disallowed) morph
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable : (Scannable_axes_op.t, Kind_axes_op.t, disallowed * 'r) morph
    | Compose :
        ('b, 'c, 'l * 'r) morph * ('a, 'b, 'l * 'r) morph
        -> ('a, 'c, 'l * 'r) morph
    constraint 'd = _ * _
  [@@ocaml.warning "-62"]

  include Magic_allow_disallow (struct
    type ('a, 'b, 'd) sided = ('a, 'b, 'd) morph constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

    let disallow_right : type a b l r.
        (a, b, l * r) sided -> (a, b, l * disallowed) sided = Obj.magic
    let disallow_left : type a b l r.
        (a, b, l * r) sided -> (a, b, disallowed * r) sided = Obj.magic
    let allow_right : type a b l r.
        (a, b, l * allowed) sided -> (a, b, l * r) sided = Obj.magic
    let allow_left : type a b l r.
        (a, b, allowed * r) sided -> (a, b, l * r) sided = Obj.magic
  end)

  let rec src : type a b l r. b obj -> (a, b, l * r) morph -> a obj =
   fun dst -> function
    | Id -> dst
    | Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Obj_Monadic
    | Min_with_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Obj_Uniqueness
    | Max_with_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Obj_Uniqueness

    | Max_with_Monadic_Visibility -> Obj_Visibility

    | Proj_Comonadic_Linearity -> Obj_Comonadic
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Linearity -> Obj_Linearity
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Linearity -> Obj_Linearity
    | Proj_Comonadic_Portability -> Obj_Comonadic
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Portability -> Obj_Portability
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Portability -> Obj_Portability
    | Proj_Comonadic_Forkable -> Obj_Comonadic
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Forkable -> Obj_Forkable

    | Proj_Comonadic_Yielding -> Obj_Comonadic

    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_Separability -> Obj_Separability
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_Pointerness -> Obj_Scannable_axes

    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_Pointerness -> Obj_Pointerness
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Externality -> Obj_Scannable_axes_op
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Externality -> Obj_Externality_op

    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability -> Obj_Nullability_op
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability -> Obj_Nullability_op
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Separability -> Obj_Scannable_axes_op
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability -> Obj_Separability_op
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability -> Obj_Separability_op
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness -> Obj_Scannable_axes_op
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness -> Obj_Pointerness_op
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness -> Obj_Pointerness_op
    | Proj_Kind_axes_Comonadic -> Obj_Kind_axes
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic -> Obj_Comonadic_with_locality
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic -> Obj_Comonadic_with_locality
    | Proj_Kind_axes_Monadic -> Obj_Kind_axes
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_Monadic -> Obj_Monadic_op
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_Monadic -> Obj_Monadic_op
    | Proj_Kind_axes_Scannable -> Obj_Kind_axes
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_Scannable -> Obj_Scannable_axes

    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic -> Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op
    | Proj_Kind_axes_op_Monadic -> Obj_Kind_axes_op
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic -> Obj_Monadic
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic -> Obj_Monadic
    | Proj_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> Obj_Kind_axes_op
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> Obj_Scannable_axes_op
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> Obj_Scannable_axes_op
    | Compose (f, g) -> src (src dst f) g

  let id = Id

  let maybe_compose : type a b c l r.
      c obj -> (b, c, l * r) morph -> (a, b, l * r) morph -> (a, c, l * r) morph =
   fun _dst f g ->
    match f, g with
    | Id, g -> g
    | f, Id -> f
    | _ -> Compose (f, g)

  let compose = maybe_compose

  let rec left_adjoint : type a b l.
      b obj -> (a, b, l * allowed) morph -> (b, a, left_only) morph =
   fun dst -> function
    | Id -> Id
    | Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Min_with_Monadic_Uniqueness
    | Max_with_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness
    | Proj_Monadic_Contention -> Min_with_Monadic_Contention
    | Max_with_Monadic_Contention -> Proj_Monadic_Contention
    | Proj_Monadic_Visibility -> Min_with_Monadic_Visibility
    | Max_with_Monadic_Visibility -> Proj_Monadic_Visibility
    | Proj_Monadic_Staticity -> Min_with_Monadic_Staticity
    | Max_with_Monadic_Staticity -> Proj_Monadic_Staticity
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Uniqueness -> Min_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness -> Proj_Monadic_op_Uniqueness
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Contention -> Min_with_Monadic_op_Contention
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Contention -> Proj_Monadic_op_Contention
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Visibility -> Min_with_Monadic_op_Visibility
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Visibility -> Proj_Monadic_op_Visibility
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Staticity -> Min_with_Monadic_op_Staticity
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Staticity -> Proj_Monadic_op_Staticity
    | Proj_Comonadic_Linearity -> Min_with_Comonadic_Linearity
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Linearity -> Proj_Comonadic_Linearity
    | Proj_Comonadic_Portability -> Min_with_Comonadic_Portability
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Portability -> Proj_Comonadic_Portability
    | Proj_Comonadic_Forkable -> Min_with_Comonadic_Forkable
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Forkable -> Proj_Comonadic_Forkable
    | Proj_Comonadic_Yielding -> Min_with_Comonadic_Yielding
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Yielding -> Proj_Comonadic_Yielding
    | Proj_Comonadic_Statefulness -> Min_with_Comonadic_Statefulness
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Statefulness -> Proj_Comonadic_Statefulness
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Linearity -> Min_with_Comonadic_op_Linearity
    | Max_with_Comonadic_op_Linearity -> Proj_Comonadic_op_Linearity
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Portability -> Min_with_Comonadic_op_Portability

    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> Proj_Kind_axes_op_Scannable
    | Compose (f, g) ->
      Compose (left_adjoint (src dst f) g, left_adjoint dst f)

  let rec right_adjoint : type a b r.
      b obj -> (a, b, allowed * r) morph -> (b, a, right_only) morph =
   fun dst -> function
    | Id -> Id
    | Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Max_with_Monadic_Uniqueness
    | Min_with_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness
    | Proj_Monadic_Contention -> Max_with_Monadic_Contention
    | Min_with_Monadic_Contention -> Proj_Monadic_Contention

    | Min_with_Monadic_Visibility -> Proj_Monadic_Visibility
    | Proj_Monadic_Staticity -> Max_with_Monadic_Staticity
    | Min_with_Monadic_Staticity -> Proj_Monadic_Staticity
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Uniqueness -> Max_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness -> Proj_Monadic_op_Uniqueness
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Contention -> Max_with_Monadic_op_Contention
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Contention -> Proj_Monadic_op_Contention
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Visibility -> Max_with_Monadic_op_Visibility
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Visibility -> Proj_Monadic_op_Visibility
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Staticity -> Max_with_Monadic_op_Staticity
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Staticity -> Proj_Monadic_op_Staticity
    | Proj_Comonadic_Linearity -> Max_with_Comonadic_Linearity
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Linearity -> Proj_Comonadic_Linearity

    | Min_with_Comonadic_Yielding -> Proj_Comonadic_Yielding
    | Proj_Comonadic_Statefulness -> Max_with_Comonadic_Statefulness
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Statefulness -> Proj_Comonadic_Statefulness
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Linearity -> Max_with_Comonadic_op_Linearity
    | Min_with_Comonadic_op_Linearity -> Proj_Comonadic_op_Linearity
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Portability -> Max_with_Comonadic_op_Portability

    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic -> Proj_Kind_axes_op_Monadic

    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> Proj_Kind_axes_op_Scannable
    | Compose (f, g) ->
      Compose (right_adjoint (src dst f) g, right_adjoint dst f)

  let rec apply : type a b l r. b obj -> (a, b, l * r) morph -> a -> b =
   fun dst morph x ->
    match morph with
    | Id -> x
    | Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Monadic.Axis.proj Monadic.Axis.Uniqueness x
    | Min_with_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Monadic.Axis.min_with Monadic.Axis.Uniqueness x
    | Max_with_Monadic_Uniqueness -> Monadic.Axis.max_with Monadic.Axis.Uniqueness x
    | Proj_Monadic_Contention -> Monadic.Axis.proj Monadic.Axis.Contention x
    | Min_with_Monadic_Contention -> Monadic.Axis.min_with Monadic.Axis.Contention x
    | Max_with_Monadic_Contention -> Monadic.Axis.max_with Monadic.Axis.Contention x
    | Proj_Monadic_Visibility -> Monadic.Axis.proj Monadic.Axis.Visibility x
    | Min_with_Monadic_Visibility -> Monadic.Axis.min_with Monadic.Axis.Visibility x
    | Max_with_Monadic_Visibility -> Monadic.Axis.max_with Monadic.Axis.Visibility x
    | Proj_Monadic_Staticity -> Monadic.Axis.proj Monadic.Axis.Staticity x
    | Min_with_Monadic_Staticity -> Monadic.Axis.min_with Monadic.Axis.Staticity x
    | Max_with_Monadic_Staticity -> Monadic.Axis.max_with Monadic.Axis.Staticity x
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Uniqueness -> Monadic_op.Axis.proj Monadic_op.Axis.Uniqueness x
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness -> Monadic_op.Axis.min_with Monadic_op.Axis.Uniqueness x
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness -> Monadic_op.Axis.max_with Monadic_op.Axis.Uniqueness x
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Contention -> Monadic_op.Axis.proj Monadic_op.Axis.Contention x
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Contention -> Monadic_op.Axis.min_with Monadic_op.Axis.Contention x
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Contention -> Monadic_op.Axis.max_with Monadic_op.Axis.Contention x
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Visibility -> Monadic_op.Axis.proj Monadic_op.Axis.Visibility x
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Visibility -> Monadic_op.Axis.min_with Monadic_op.Axis.Visibility x
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Visibility -> Monadic_op.Axis.max_with Monadic_op.Axis.Visibility x
    | Proj_Monadic_op_Staticity -> Monadic_op.Axis.proj Monadic_op.Axis.Staticity x
    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Staticity -> Monadic_op.Axis.min_with Monadic_op.Axis.Staticity x
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Staticity -> Monadic_op.Axis.max_with Monadic_op.Axis.Staticity x
    | Proj_Comonadic_Linearity -> Comonadic.Axis.proj Comonadic.Axis.Linearity x
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Linearity -> Comonadic.Axis.min_with Comonadic.Axis.Linearity x
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Linearity -> Comonadic.Axis.max_with Comonadic.Axis.Linearity x
    | Proj_Comonadic_Portability -> Comonadic.Axis.proj Comonadic.Axis.Portability x
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Portability -> Comonadic.Axis.min_with Comonadic.Axis.Portability x
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Portability -> Comonadic.Axis.max_with Comonadic.Axis.Portability x
    | Proj_Comonadic_Forkable -> Comonadic.Axis.proj Comonadic.Axis.Forkable x
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Forkable -> Comonadic.Axis.min_with Comonadic.Axis.Forkable x
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Forkable -> Comonadic.Axis.max_with Comonadic.Axis.Forkable x
    | Proj_Comonadic_Yielding -> Comonadic.Axis.proj Comonadic.Axis.Yielding x
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Yielding -> Comonadic.Axis.min_with Comonadic.Axis.Yielding x
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Yielding -> Comonadic.Axis.max_with Comonadic.Axis.Yielding x
    | Proj_Comonadic_Statefulness -> Comonadic.Axis.proj Comonadic.Axis.Statefulness x
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Statefulness -> Comonadic.Axis.min_with Comonadic.Axis.Statefulness x
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Statefulness -> Comonadic.Axis.max_with Comonadic.Axis.Statefulness x
    | Proj_Comonadic_op_Linearity -> Comonadic_op.Axis.proj Comonadic_op.Axis.Linearity x

    | Min_with_Comonadic_op_Portability -> Comonadic_op.Axis.min_with Comonadic_op.Axis.Portability x
    | Max_with_Comonadic_op_Portability -> Comonadic_op.Axis.max_with Comonadic_op.Axis.Portability x

    | Min_with_Comonadic_op_Forkable -> Comonadic_op.Axis.min_with Comonadic_op.Axis.Forkable x

    | Min_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_op_Comonadic -> Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Axis.min_with Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Max_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_op_Comonadic -> Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Axis.max_with Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Proj_Value_Comonadic -> Value.Axis.proj Value.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Min_with_Value_Comonadic -> Value.Axis.min_with Value.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Max_with_Value_Comonadic -> Value.Axis.max_with Value.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Proj_Value_Monadic -> Value.Axis.proj Value.Axis.Monadic x
    | Min_with_Value_Monadic -> Value.Axis.min_with Value.Axis.Monadic x
    | Max_with_Value_Monadic -> Value.Axis.max_with Value.Axis.Monadic x
    | Proj_Value_op_Comonadic -> Value_op.Axis.proj Value_op.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Min_with_Value_op_Comonadic -> Value_op.Axis.min_with Value_op.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Max_with_Value_op_Comonadic -> Value_op.Axis.max_with Value_op.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Proj_Value_op_Monadic -> Value_op.Axis.proj Value_op.Axis.Monadic x
    | Min_with_Value_op_Monadic -> Value_op.Axis.min_with Value_op.Axis.Monadic x
    | Max_with_Value_op_Monadic -> Value_op.Axis.max_with Value_op.Axis.Monadic x
    | Proj_Alloc_Comonadic -> Alloc.Axis.proj Alloc.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Min_with_Alloc_Comonadic -> Alloc.Axis.min_with Alloc.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Max_with_Alloc_Comonadic -> Alloc.Axis.max_with Alloc.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Proj_Alloc_Monadic -> Alloc.Axis.proj Alloc.Axis.Monadic x
    | Min_with_Alloc_Monadic -> Alloc.Axis.min_with Alloc.Axis.Monadic x
    | Max_with_Alloc_Monadic -> Alloc.Axis.max_with Alloc.Axis.Monadic x
    | Proj_Alloc_op_Comonadic -> Alloc_op.Axis.proj Alloc_op.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Min_with_Alloc_op_Comonadic -> Alloc_op.Axis.min_with Alloc_op.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Max_with_Alloc_op_Comonadic -> Alloc_op.Axis.max_with Alloc_op.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Proj_Alloc_op_Monadic -> Alloc_op.Axis.proj Alloc_op.Axis.Monadic x
    | Min_with_Alloc_op_Monadic -> Alloc_op.Axis.min_with Alloc_op.Axis.Monadic x
    | Max_with_Alloc_op_Monadic -> Alloc_op.Axis.max_with Alloc_op.Axis.Monadic x
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_Externality -> Scannable_axes.Axis.proj Scannable_axes.Axis.Externality x
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_Externality -> Scannable_axes.Axis.min_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Externality x
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_Externality -> Scannable_axes.Axis.max_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Externality x
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_Nullability -> Scannable_axes.Axis.proj Scannable_axes.Axis.Nullability x
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_Nullability -> Scannable_axes.Axis.min_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Nullability x

    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_Separability -> Scannable_axes.Axis.min_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Separability x
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_Separability -> Scannable_axes.Axis.max_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Separability x
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_Pointerness -> Scannable_axes.Axis.proj Scannable_axes.Axis.Pointerness x
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_Pointerness -> Scannable_axes.Axis.min_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Pointerness x
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_Pointerness -> Scannable_axes.Axis.max_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Pointerness x

    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability -> Scannable_axes_op.Axis.min_with Scannable_axes_op.Axis.Nullability x
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability -> Scannable_axes_op.Axis.max_with Scannable_axes_op.Axis.Nullability x
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Separability -> Scannable_axes_op.Axis.proj Scannable_axes_op.Axis.Separability x
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability -> Scannable_axes_op.Axis.min_with Scannable_axes_op.Axis.Separability x
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability -> Scannable_axes_op.Axis.max_with Scannable_axes_op.Axis.Separability x
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness -> Scannable_axes_op.Axis.proj Scannable_axes_op.Axis.Pointerness x

    | Proj_Kind_axes_Comonadic -> Kind_axes.Axis.proj Kind_axes.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic -> Kind_axes.Axis.min_with Kind_axes.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic -> Kind_axes.Axis.max_with Kind_axes.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Proj_Kind_axes_Monadic -> Kind_axes.Axis.proj Kind_axes.Axis.Monadic x
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_Monadic -> Kind_axes.Axis.min_with Kind_axes.Axis.Monadic x
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_Monadic -> Kind_axes.Axis.max_with Kind_axes.Axis.Monadic x
    | Proj_Kind_axes_Scannable -> Kind_axes.Axis.proj Kind_axes.Axis.Scannable x
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_Scannable -> Kind_axes.Axis.min_with Kind_axes.Axis.Scannable x
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_Scannable -> Kind_axes.Axis.max_with Kind_axes.Axis.Scannable x
    | Proj_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic -> Kind_axes_op.Axis.proj Kind_axes_op.Axis.Comonadic x

    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic -> Kind_axes_op.Axis.max_with Kind_axes_op.Axis.Comonadic x
    | Proj_Kind_axes_op_Monadic -> Kind_axes_op.Axis.proj Kind_axes_op.Axis.Monadic x
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic -> Kind_axes_op.Axis.min_with Kind_axes_op.Axis.Monadic x

    | Proj_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> Kind_axes_op.Axis.proj Kind_axes_op.Axis.Scannable x
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> Kind_axes_op.Axis.min_with Kind_axes_op.Axis.Scannable x
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> Kind_axes_op.Axis.max_with Kind_axes_op.Axis.Scannable x
    | Compose (f, g) -> apply dst f (apply (src dst f) g x)

  let rec morph_key : type a b l r. (a, b, l * r) morph -> string = function
    | Id -> "Id"
    | Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness -> "Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness"

    | Min_with_Monadic_op_Staticity -> "Min_with_Monadic_op_Staticity"
    | Max_with_Monadic_op_Staticity -> "Max_with_Monadic_op_Staticity"
    | Proj_Comonadic_Linearity -> "Proj_Comonadic_Linearity"
    | Min_with_Comonadic_Linearity -> "Min_with_Comonadic_Linearity"
    | Max_with_Comonadic_Linearity -> "Max_with_Comonadic_Linearity"

    | Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Comonadic -> "Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Comonadic"
    | Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Areality -> "Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Areality"
    | Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Areality -> "Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Areality"

    | Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Comonadic -> "Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Comonadic"
    | Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Comonadic -> "Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Comonadic"
    | Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Comonadic -> "Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Comonadic"
    | Proj_Comonadic_with_regionality_Areality -> "Proj_Comonadic_with_regionality_Areality"

    | Min_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_Comonadic -> "Min_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_Comonadic"

    | Proj_Comonadic_with_regionality_op_Areality -> "Proj_Comonadic_with_regionality_op_Areality"

    | Min_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_op_Comonadic -> "Min_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_op_Comonadic"
    | Max_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_op_Comonadic -> "Max_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_op_Comonadic"
    | Proj_Value_Comonadic -> "Proj_Value_Comonadic"

    | Proj_Value_op_Comonadic -> "Proj_Value_op_Comonadic"

    | Proj_Alloc_op_Comonadic -> "Proj_Alloc_op_Comonadic"

    | Proj_Scannable_axes_Pointerness -> "Proj_Scannable_axes_Pointerness"
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_Pointerness -> "Min_with_Scannable_axes_Pointerness"
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_Pointerness -> "Max_with_Scannable_axes_Pointerness"
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Externality -> "Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Externality"
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Externality -> "Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Externality"
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Externality -> "Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Externality"
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability -> "Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability"
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability -> "Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability"
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability -> "Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability"
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Separability -> "Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Separability"
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability -> "Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability"
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability -> "Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability"
    | Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness -> "Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness"
    | Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness -> "Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness"
    | Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness -> "Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness"
    | Proj_Kind_axes_Comonadic -> "Proj_Kind_axes_Comonadic"
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic -> "Min_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic"
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic -> "Max_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic"
    | Proj_Kind_axes_Monadic -> "Proj_Kind_axes_Monadic"
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_Monadic -> "Min_with_Kind_axes_Monadic"
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_Monadic -> "Max_with_Kind_axes_Monadic"
    | Proj_Kind_axes_Scannable -> "Proj_Kind_axes_Scannable"
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_Scannable -> "Min_with_Kind_axes_Scannable"
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_Scannable -> "Max_with_Kind_axes_Scannable"
    | Proj_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic -> "Proj_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic"
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic -> "Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic"
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic -> "Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic"
    | Proj_Kind_axes_op_Monadic -> "Proj_Kind_axes_op_Monadic"
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic -> "Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic"
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic -> "Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic"
    | Proj_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> "Proj_Kind_axes_op_Scannable"
    | Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> "Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable"
    | Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable -> "Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable"
    | Compose (f, g) -> "Compose(" ^ morph_key f ^ "," ^ morph_key g ^ ")"

  let equal_morph : type a0 a1 b l0 r0 l1 r1.
      b obj ->
      (a0, b, l0 * r0) morph ->
      (a1, b, l1 * r1) morph ->
      (a0, a1) Misc.eq option =
   fun _dst m1 m2 ->
    if String.equal (morph_key m1) (morph_key m2)
    then Some (Obj.magic Misc.Refl)
    else None

  let compare_morph : type a0 a1 b l0 r0 l1 r1.
      b obj ->
      (a0, b, l0 * r0) morph ->
      (a1, b, l1 * r1) morph ->
      (a0, a1) Misc.comparison =
   fun _dst m1 m2 ->
    if String.equal (morph_key m1) (morph_key m2)
    then Obj.magic Equal
    else if String.compare (morph_key m1) (morph_key m2) < 0
    then Less_than
    else Greater_than

  let print_morph : type a b l r. b obj -> Fmt.formatter -> (a, b, l * r) morph -> unit =
   fun _dst ppf morph -> Fmt.fprintf ppf "%s" (morph_key morph)

end

module Solver_support = Solver_runtime.Make (Lattices_univ)

module Make_solver_core
    (Const_desc : sig
      type t
      module Repr : sig
        val to_int : t -> int
      end
      val legacy : t
    end)
    (Obj_desc : sig
      val obj : int Solver_support.obj
    end) =
struct
  include Solver_support.Positive_gen (Obj_desc)

  let of_const_value c = of_const (Const_desc.Repr.to_int c)
  let legacy = of_const_value Const_desc.legacy
  let show ?verbose t = Format_doc.asprintf "%a" (print ?verbose) t
end

module Make_solver_module
    (Const_desc : sig
      type t
      val pp : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
      module Repr : sig
        val to_int : t -> int
        val of_int_exn : int -> t
      end
      val legacy : t
    end)
    (Obj_desc : sig
      val obj : int Solver_support.obj
    end) =
struct
  include Make_solver_core (struct
    type t = Const_desc.t
    module Repr = struct
      let to_int = Const_desc.Repr.to_int
    end
    let legacy = Const_desc.legacy
  end) (Obj_desc)

  type simple_error = {
    left : Const_desc.t;
    right : Const_desc.t;
  }

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    {
      left = Const_desc.Repr.of_int_exn left;
      right = Const_desc.Repr.of_int_exn right;
    }

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_error ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" Const_desc.pp left Const_desc.pp right

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)
end

module Locality = struct
  module Const = Lattices_const.Locality
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_module (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Locality
  end)
  let global = of_const_value Const.global
  let local = of_const_value Const.local
end

module Locality_op = struct
  module Const = Lattices_const.Locality_op
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_module (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Locality_op
  end)
  let global = of_const_value Const.global
  let local = of_const_value Const.local
end

module Locality_in_Regionality = struct
  let embed = function
    | 0 -> Regionality.Const.global
    | 1 -> Regionality.Const.local
    | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
  let left1 = function
    | 0 -> Locality.Const.global
    | 1 -> Locality.Const.local
    | 3 -> Locality.Const.local
    | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
  let left2 = function
    | 0 -> Regionality.Const.global
    | 1 -> Regionality.Const.regional
    | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
  let right1 = function
    | 0 -> Locality.Const.global
    | 1 -> Locality.Const.global
    | 3 -> Locality.Const.local
    | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
  let right2 = function
    | 0 -> Regionality.Const.regional
    | 1 -> Regionality.Const.local
    | _ -> invalid_arg "invalid lattice element"
  let locality_as_regionality = embed
  let regional_to_local = left1
  let regional_to_global = right1
  let local_to_regional = left2
  let global_to_regional = right2
end

module Monadic = struct
  module Field_Uniqueness = Uniqueness
  module Field_Contention = Contention
  module Field_Visibility = Visibility
  module Field_Staticity = Staticity
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Monadic.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Monadic
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Uniqueness.Const.le left_view.uniqueness right_view.uniqueness) then
    Error (Axis.Uniqueness, { left = left_view.uniqueness; right = right_view.uniqueness })
  else if not (Field_Contention.Const.le left_view.contention right_view.contention) then
    Error (Axis.Contention, { left = left_view.contention; right = right_view.contention })
  else if not (Field_Visibility.Const.le left_view.visibility right_view.visibility) then
    Error (Axis.Visibility, { left = left_view.visibility; right = right_view.visibility })
  else if not (Field_Staticity.Const.le left_view.staticity right_view.staticity) then
    Error (Axis.Staticity, { left = left_view.staticity; right = right_view.staticity })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Uniqueness, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Uniqueness
        (print_axerror Field_Uniqueness.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Contention, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Contention
        (print_axerror Field_Contention.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Visibility, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Visibility
        (print_axerror Field_Visibility.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Staticity, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Staticity
        (print_axerror Field_Staticity.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Uniqueness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Uniqueness
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Monadic_Uniqueness
        m
    | Axis.Contention ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Contention
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Monadic_Contention
        m
    | Axis.Visibility ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Visibility
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Monadic_Visibility
        m
    | Axis.Staticity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Staticity
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Monadic_Staticity
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Uniqueness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Monadic_Uniqueness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Contention ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Monadic_Contention
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Visibility ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Monadic_Visibility
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Staticity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Monadic_Staticity
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Uniqueness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Monadic_Uniqueness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Contention ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Monadic_Contention
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Visibility ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Monadic_Visibility
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Staticity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Monadic_Staticity
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_uniqueness m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Uniqueness m)
  let min_with_uniqueness m = min_with Axis.Uniqueness (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_uniqueness m = max_with Axis.Uniqueness (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_contention m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Contention m)
  let min_with_contention m = min_with Axis.Contention (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_contention m = max_with Axis.Contention (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_visibility m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Visibility m)
  let min_with_visibility m = min_with Axis.Visibility (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_visibility m = max_with Axis.Visibility (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_staticity m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Staticity m)
  let min_with_staticity m = min_with Axis.Staticity (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_staticity m = max_with Axis.Staticity (Obj.magic m)

end

module Monadic_op = struct
  module Field_Uniqueness = Uniqueness_op
  module Field_Contention = Contention_op
  module Field_Visibility = Visibility_op
  module Field_Staticity = Staticity_op
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Monadic_op.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Monadic_op
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Uniqueness.Const.le left_view.uniqueness right_view.uniqueness) then
    Error (Axis.Uniqueness, { left = left_view.uniqueness; right = right_view.uniqueness })
  else if not (Field_Contention.Const.le left_view.contention right_view.contention) then
    Error (Axis.Contention, { left = left_view.contention; right = right_view.contention })
  else if not (Field_Visibility.Const.le left_view.visibility right_view.visibility) then
    Error (Axis.Visibility, { left = left_view.visibility; right = right_view.visibility })
  else if not (Field_Staticity.Const.le left_view.staticity right_view.staticity) then
    Error (Axis.Staticity, { left = left_view.staticity; right = right_view.staticity })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Uniqueness, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Uniqueness
        (print_axerror Field_Uniqueness.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Contention, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Contention
        (print_axerror Field_Contention.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Visibility, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Visibility
        (print_axerror Field_Visibility.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Staticity, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Staticity
        (print_axerror Field_Staticity.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Uniqueness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Uniqueness_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Monadic_op_Uniqueness
        m
    | Axis.Contention ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Contention_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Monadic_op_Contention
        m
    | Axis.Visibility ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Visibility_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Monadic_op_Visibility
        m
    | Axis.Staticity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Staticity_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Monadic_op_Staticity
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Uniqueness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Contention ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Monadic_op_Contention
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Visibility ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Monadic_op_Visibility
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Staticity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Monadic_op_Staticity
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Uniqueness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Monadic_op_Uniqueness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Contention ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Monadic_op_Contention
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Visibility ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Monadic_op_Visibility
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Staticity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Monadic_op_Staticity
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_uniqueness m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Uniqueness m)
  let min_with_uniqueness m = min_with Axis.Uniqueness (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_uniqueness m = max_with Axis.Uniqueness (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_contention m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Contention m)
  let min_with_contention m = min_with Axis.Contention (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_contention m = max_with Axis.Contention (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_visibility m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Visibility m)
  let min_with_visibility m = min_with Axis.Visibility (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_visibility m = max_with Axis.Visibility (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_staticity m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Staticity m)
  let min_with_staticity m = min_with Axis.Staticity (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_staticity m = max_with Axis.Staticity (Obj.magic m)

end

module Comonadic = struct
  module Field_Linearity = Linearity
  module Field_Portability = Portability
  module Field_Forkable = Forkable
  module Field_Yielding = Yielding
  module Field_Statefulness = Statefulness
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Comonadic.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Comonadic
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Linearity.Const.le left_view.linearity right_view.linearity) then
    Error (Axis.Linearity, { left = left_view.linearity; right = right_view.linearity })
  else if not (Field_Portability.Const.le left_view.portability right_view.portability) then
    Error (Axis.Portability, { left = left_view.portability; right = right_view.portability })
  else if not (Field_Forkable.Const.le left_view.forkable right_view.forkable) then
    Error (Axis.Forkable, { left = left_view.forkable; right = right_view.forkable })
  else if not (Field_Yielding.Const.le left_view.yielding right_view.yielding) then
    Error (Axis.Yielding, { left = left_view.yielding; right = right_view.yielding })
  else if not (Field_Statefulness.Const.le left_view.statefulness right_view.statefulness) then
    Error (Axis.Statefulness, { left = left_view.statefulness; right = right_view.statefulness })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Linearity, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Linearity
        (print_axerror Field_Linearity.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Portability, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Portability
        (print_axerror Field_Portability.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Forkable, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Forkable
        (print_axerror Field_Forkable.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Yielding, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Yielding
        (print_axerror Field_Yielding.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Statefulness, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Statefulness
        (print_axerror Field_Statefulness.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Linearity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Linearity
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_Linearity
        m
    | Axis.Portability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Portability
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_Portability
        m
    | Axis.Forkable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Forkable
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_Forkable
        m
    | Axis.Yielding ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Yielding
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_Yielding
        m
    | Axis.Statefulness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Statefulness
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_Statefulness
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Linearity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_Linearity
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Portability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_Portability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Forkable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_Forkable
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Yielding ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_Yielding
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Statefulness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_Statefulness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Linearity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_Linearity
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Portability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_Portability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Forkable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_Forkable
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Yielding ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_Yielding
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Statefulness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_Statefulness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_linearity m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Linearity m)
  let min_with_linearity m = min_with Axis.Linearity (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_linearity m = max_with Axis.Linearity (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_portability m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Portability m)
  let min_with_portability m = min_with Axis.Portability (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_portability m = max_with Axis.Portability (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_forkable m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Forkable m)
  let min_with_forkable m = min_with Axis.Forkable (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_forkable m = max_with Axis.Forkable (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_yielding m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Yielding m)
  let min_with_yielding m = min_with Axis.Yielding (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_yielding m = max_with Axis.Yielding (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_statefulness m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Statefulness m)
  let min_with_statefulness m = min_with Axis.Statefulness (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_statefulness m = max_with Axis.Statefulness (Obj.magic m)

end

module Comonadic_op = struct
  module Field_Linearity = Linearity_op
  module Field_Portability = Portability_op
  module Field_Forkable = Forkable_op
  module Field_Yielding = Yielding_op
  module Field_Statefulness = Statefulness_op
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Comonadic_op.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Comonadic_op
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in

    let right_view = Const.view right in

    Error (Axis.Linearity, { left = left_view.linearity; right = right_view.linearity })
  else if not (Field_Portability.Const.le left_view.portability right_view.portability) then
    Error (Axis.Portability, { left = left_view.portability; right = right_view.portability })
  else if not (Field_Forkable.Const.le left_view.forkable right_view.forkable) then
    Error (Axis.Forkable, { left = left_view.forkable; right = right_view.forkable })
  else if not (Field_Yielding.Const.le left_view.yielding right_view.yielding) then
    Error (Axis.Yielding, { left = left_view.yielding; right = right_view.yielding })
  else if not (Field_Statefulness.Const.le left_view.statefulness right_view.statefulness) then
    Error (Axis.Statefulness, { left = left_view.statefulness; right = right_view.statefulness })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =

        Axis.print

    | Axis.Portability, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Portability
        (print_axerror Field_Portability.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Forkable, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Forkable
        (print_axerror Field_Forkable.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Yielding, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Yielding
        (print_axerror Field_Yielding.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Statefulness, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Statefulness
        (print_axerror Field_Statefulness.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Linearity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Linearity_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_op_Linearity
        m
    | Axis.Portability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Portability_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_op_Portability
        m
    | Axis.Forkable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Forkable_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_op_Forkable
        m
    | Axis.Yielding ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Yielding_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_op_Yielding
        m
    | Axis.Statefulness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Statefulness_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_op_Statefulness
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Linearity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_op_Linearity
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Portability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_op_Portability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Forkable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_op_Forkable
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Yielding ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_op_Yielding
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Statefulness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_op_Statefulness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Linearity ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_op_Linearity
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Portability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_op_Portability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Forkable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_op_Forkable
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Yielding ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_op_Yielding
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Statefulness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_op_Statefulness
