  let proj_linearity m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Linearity m)
  let min_with_linearity m = min_with Axis.Linearity (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_linearity m = max_with Axis.Linearity (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_portability m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Portability m)
  let min_with_portability m = min_with Axis.Portability (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_portability m = max_with Axis.Portability (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_forkable m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Forkable m)
  let min_with_forkable m = min_with Axis.Forkable (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_forkable m = max_with Axis.Forkable (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_yielding m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Yielding m)
  let min_with_yielding m = min_with Axis.Yielding (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_yielding m = max_with Axis.Yielding (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_statefulness m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Statefulness m)
  let min_with_statefulness m = min_with Axis.Statefulness (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_statefulness m = max_with Axis.Statefulness (Obj.magic m)

end

module Comonadic_with_locality = struct
  module Field_Areality = Locality
  module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Comonadic_with_locality.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Comonadic_with_locality
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Areality.Const.le left_view.areality right_view.areality) then
    Error (Axis.Areality, { left = left_view.areality; right = right_view.areality })
  else if not (Field_Comonadic.Const.le left_view.comonadic right_view.comonadic) then
    Error (Axis.Comonadic, { left = left_view.comonadic; right = right_view.comonadic })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Areality, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Areality
        (print_axerror Field_Areality.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Comonadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Comonadic
        (print_axerror Field_Comonadic.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Areality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Locality
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_Areality
        m
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_Comonadic
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Areality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Areality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Areality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Areality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_areality m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Areality m)
  let min_with_areality m = min_with Axis.Areality (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_areality m = max_with Axis.Areality (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_comonadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Comonadic m)
  let min_with_comonadic m = min_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_comonadic m = max_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)

end

module Comonadic_with_locality_op = struct
  module Field_Areality = Locality_op
  module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_op
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Comonadic_with_locality_op.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Comonadic_with_locality_op
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Areality.Const.le left_view.areality right_view.areality) then
    Error (Axis.Areality, { left = left_view.areality; right = right_view.areality })
  else if not (Field_Comonadic.Const.le left_view.comonadic right_view.comonadic) then
    Error (Axis.Comonadic, { left = left_view.comonadic; right = right_view.comonadic })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Areality, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Areality
        (print_axerror Field_Areality.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Comonadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Comonadic
        (print_axerror Field_Comonadic.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Areality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Locality_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Areality
        m
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Comonadic
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Areality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Areality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Areality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Areality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_with_locality_op_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_areality m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Areality m)
  let min_with_areality m = min_with Axis.Areality (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_areality m = max_with Axis.Areality (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_comonadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Comonadic m)
  let min_with_comonadic m = min_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_comonadic m = max_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)

end

module Comonadic_with_regionality = struct
  module Field_Areality = Regionality
  module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Comonadic_with_regionality.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Comonadic_with_regionality
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in

    Error (Axis.Areality, { left = left_view.areality; right = right_view.areality })
  else if not (Field_Comonadic.Const.le left_view.comonadic right_view.comonadic) then
    Error (Axis.Comonadic, { left = left_view.comonadic; right = right_view.comonadic })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Areality, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Areality
        (print_axerror Field_Areality.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Comonadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Comonadic
        (print_axerror Field_Comonadic.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Areality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Regionality
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_with_regionality_Areality
        m
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Comonadic_with_regionality_Comonadic
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Areality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_Areality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Areality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_Areality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Comonadic_with_regionality_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_areality m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Areality m)
  let min_with_areality m = min_with Axis.Areality (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_areality m = max_with Axis.Areality (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_comonadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Comonadic m)
  let min_with_comonadic m = min_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_comonadic m = max_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)

end

module Comonadic_with_regionality_op = struct

module Value = struct
  module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality
  module Field_Monadic = Monadic
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Value.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Value
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Value
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Comonadic.Const.le left_view.comonadic right_view.comonadic) then
    Error (Axis.Comonadic, { left = left_view.comonadic; right = right_view.comonadic })
  else if not (Field_Monadic.Const.le left_view.monadic right_view.monadic) then
    Error (Axis.Monadic, { left = left_view.monadic; right = right_view.monadic })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Comonadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Comonadic
        (print_axerror Field_Comonadic.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Monadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Monadic
        (print_axerror Field_Monadic.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Value_Comonadic
        m
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Value_Monadic
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Value
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Value_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Value
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Value_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Value
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Value_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Value
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Value_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_comonadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Comonadic m)
  let min_with_comonadic m = min_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_comonadic m = max_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_monadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Monadic m)
  let min_with_monadic m = min_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_monadic m = max_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)

end

module Value_op = struct
  module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality_op
  module Field_Monadic = Monadic_op
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Value_op.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Value_op
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Value_op
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in

    let right_view = Const.view right in

  else if not (Field_Monadic.Const.le left_view.monadic right_view.monadic) then
    Error (Axis.Monadic, { left = left_view.monadic; right = right_view.monadic })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Comonadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Comonadic
        (print_axerror Field_Comonadic.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Monadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Monadic
        (print_axerror Field_Monadic.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_regionality_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Value_op_Comonadic
        m
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Value_op_Monadic
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Value_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Value_op_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Value_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Value_op_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Value_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Value_op_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Value_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Value_op_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_comonadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Comonadic m)
  let min_with_comonadic m = min_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_comonadic m = max_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_monadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Monadic m)
  let min_with_monadic m = min_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_monadic m = max_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)

end

module Alloc = struct
  module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality
  module Field_Monadic = Monadic
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Alloc.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Alloc
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Alloc
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Comonadic.Const.le left_view.comonadic right_view.comonadic) then
    Error (Axis.Comonadic, { left = left_view.comonadic; right = right_view.comonadic })
  else if not (Field_Monadic.Const.le left_view.monadic right_view.monadic) then
    Error (Axis.Monadic, { left = left_view.monadic; right = right_view.monadic })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Comonadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Comonadic
        (print_axerror Field_Comonadic.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Monadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Monadic
        (print_axerror Field_Monadic.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Alloc_Comonadic
        m
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Alloc_Monadic
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Alloc
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Alloc_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Alloc
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Alloc_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Alloc
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Alloc_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Alloc
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Alloc_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_comonadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Comonadic m)
  let min_with_comonadic m = min_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_comonadic m = max_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_monadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Monadic m)
  let min_with_monadic m = min_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_monadic m = max_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)

end

module Scannable_axes = struct
  module Field_Externality = Externality
  module Field_Nullability = Nullability
  module Field_Separability = Separability
  module Field_Pointerness = Pointerness
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Scannable_axes.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Scannable_axes
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Externality.Const.le left_view.externality right_view.externality) then
    Error (Axis.Externality, { left = left_view.externality; right = right_view.externality })
  else if not (Field_Nullability.Const.le left_view.nullability right_view.nullability) then
    Error (Axis.Nullability, { left = left_view.nullability; right = right_view.nullability })
  else if not (Field_Separability.Const.le left_view.separability right_view.separability) then
    Error (Axis.Separability, { left = left_view.separability; right = right_view.separability })
  else if not (Field_Pointerness.Const.le left_view.pointerness right_view.pointerness) then
    Error (Axis.Pointerness, { left = left_view.pointerness; right = right_view.pointerness })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Externality, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Externality
        (print_axerror Field_Externality.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Nullability, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Nullability
        (print_axerror Field_Nullability.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Separability, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Separability
        (print_axerror Field_Separability.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Pointerness, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Pointerness
        (print_axerror Field_Pointerness.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Externality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Externality
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Scannable_axes_Externality
        m
    | Axis.Nullability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Nullability
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Scannable_axes_Nullability
        m
    | Axis.Separability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Separability
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Scannable_axes_Separability
        m
    | Axis.Pointerness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Pointerness
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Scannable_axes_Pointerness
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Externality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Scannable_axes_Externality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Nullability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Scannable_axes_Nullability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Separability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Scannable_axes_Separability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Pointerness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Scannable_axes_Pointerness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Externality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Scannable_axes_Externality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Nullability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Scannable_axes_Nullability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Separability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Scannable_axes_Separability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Pointerness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Scannable_axes_Pointerness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_externality m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Externality m)
  let min_with_externality m = min_with Axis.Externality (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_externality m = max_with Axis.Externality (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_nullability m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Nullability m)
  let min_with_nullability m = min_with Axis.Nullability (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_nullability m = max_with Axis.Nullability (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_separability m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Separability m)
  let min_with_separability m = min_with Axis.Separability (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_separability m = max_with Axis.Separability (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_pointerness m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Pointerness m)
  let min_with_pointerness m = min_with Axis.Pointerness (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_pointerness m = max_with Axis.Pointerness (Obj.magic m)

end

        Lattices_univ.Obj_Nullability_op

      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Separability_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Separability
        m
    | Axis.Pointerness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Pointerness_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Externality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Externality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Nullability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Separability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Pointerness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Externality ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Externality
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Nullability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Nullability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Separability ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Separability
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Pointerness ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Scannable_axes_op_Pointerness
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_externality m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Externality m)
  let min_with_externality m = min_with Axis.Externality (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_externality m = max_with Axis.Externality (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_nullability m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Nullability m)
  let min_with_nullability m = min_with Axis.Nullability (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_nullability m = max_with Axis.Nullability (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_separability m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Separability m)
  let min_with_separability m = min_with Axis.Separability (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_separability m = max_with Axis.Separability (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_pointerness m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Pointerness m)
  let min_with_pointerness m = min_with Axis.Pointerness (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_pointerness m = max_with Axis.Pointerness (Obj.magic m)

end

module Kind_axes = struct
  module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality
  module Field_Monadic = Monadic_op
  module Field_Scannable = Scannable_axes
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Kind_axes.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Kind_axes
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Comonadic.Const.le left_view.comonadic right_view.comonadic) then
    Error (Axis.Comonadic, { left = left_view.comonadic; right = right_view.comonadic })
  else if not (Field_Monadic.Const.le left_view.monadic right_view.monadic) then
    Error (Axis.Monadic, { left = left_view.monadic; right = right_view.monadic })
  else if not (Field_Scannable.Const.le left_view.scannable right_view.scannable) then
    Error (Axis.Scannable, { left = left_view.scannable; right = right_view.scannable })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Comonadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Comonadic
        (print_axerror Field_Comonadic.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Monadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Monadic
        (print_axerror Field_Monadic.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Scannable, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Scannable
        (print_axerror Field_Scannable.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Kind_axes_Comonadic
        m
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Kind_axes_Monadic
        m
    | Axis.Scannable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Kind_axes_Scannable
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Kind_axes_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Scannable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Kind_axes_Scannable
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Kind_axes_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Kind_axes_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Scannable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Kind_axes_Scannable
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_comonadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Comonadic m)
  let min_with_comonadic m = min_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_comonadic m = max_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_monadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Monadic m)
  let min_with_monadic m = min_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_monadic m = max_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_scannable m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Scannable m)
  let min_with_scannable m = min_with Axis.Scannable (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_scannable m = max_with Axis.Scannable (Obj.magic m)

end

module Kind_axes_op = struct
  module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op
  module Field_Monadic = Monadic
  module Field_Scannable = Scannable_axes_op
  module Axis = Lattices_const.Kind_axes_op.Axis
  module Const = Lattices_const.Kind_axes_op
  type const = Const.t

  include Make_solver_core (Const) (struct
    let obj = Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes_op
  end)

  type 'a simple_axerror = {
    left : 'a;
    right : 'a;
  }

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  let error_of_raw ({ left; right; _ } : int Solver_support.Raw.error_raw) =
    let left = Const.Repr.of_int_exn left in
    let right = Const.Repr.of_int_exn right in
    let left_view = Const.view left in
    let right_view = Const.view right in
  if not (Field_Comonadic.Const.le left_view.comonadic right_view.comonadic) then
    Error (Axis.Comonadic, { left = left_view.comonadic; right = right_view.comonadic })
  else if not (Field_Monadic.Const.le left_view.monadic right_view.monadic) then
    Error (Axis.Monadic, { left = left_view.monadic; right = right_view.monadic })
  else if not (Field_Scannable.Const.le left_view.scannable right_view.scannable) then
    Error (Axis.Scannable, { left = left_view.scannable; right = right_view.scannable })
  else
    invalid_arg "product error_of_raw: no failing axis"

  let to_simple_error error = error

  let print_axerror pp ppf { left; right } =
    Format.fprintf ppf "%a <= %a does not hold" pp left pp right

  let print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit =
   fun ppf (Error (axis, error)) ->
    match axis, error with
    | Axis.Comonadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Comonadic
        (print_axerror Field_Comonadic.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Monadic, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Monadic
        (print_axerror Field_Monadic.Const.pp)
        error
    | Axis.Scannable, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "%a: %a"
        Axis.print
        Axis.Scannable
        (print_axerror Field_Scannable.Const.pp)
        error

  let print_equate_error ppf = function
    | Left_le_right, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Left_le_right: %a" print_error error
    | Right_le_left, error ->
      Format.fprintf ppf "Right_le_left: %a" print_error error

  let submode a b = Result.map_error error_of_raw (submode_raw a b)

  let submode_exn a b =
    match submode a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_error error)

  let equate a b =
    Result.map_error
      (fun (forward, error) ->
        ((if forward then Left_le_right else Right_le_left), error_of_raw error))
      (equate_raw a b)

  let equate_exn a b =
    match equate a b with
    | Ok () -> ()
    | Error error -> invalid_arg (Format.asprintf "%a" print_equate_error error)

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode = (int, 'd) Solver_support.Raw.mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  let proj : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (l * r) t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Comonadic_with_locality_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic
        m
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Monadic
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Kind_axes_op_Monadic
        m
    | Axis.Scannable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Scannable_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Proj_Kind_axes_op_Scannable
        m
  let min_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (l * Allowance.disallowed) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
    | Axis.Scannable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Min_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_right m)
  let max_with : type a l r. a Axis.t -> (a, l * r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * r) t =
   fun axis m ->
    match axis with
    | Axis.Comonadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Comonadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Monadic ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Monadic
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
    | Axis.Scannable ->
      Solver_support.Raw.apply
        Lattices_univ.Obj_Kind_axes_op
        Lattices_univ.Max_with_Kind_axes_op_Scannable
        (Solver_support.Raw.disallow_left m)
  let proj_comonadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Comonadic m)
  let min_with_comonadic m = min_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_comonadic m = max_with Axis.Comonadic (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_monadic m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Monadic m)
  let min_with_monadic m = min_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_monadic m = max_with Axis.Monadic (Obj.magic m)
  let proj_scannable m = Obj.magic (proj Axis.Scannable m)
  let min_with_scannable m = min_with Axis.Scannable (Obj.magic m)
  let max_with_scannable m = max_with Axis.Scannable (Obj.magic m)

end

let locality_as_regionality = Locality_in_Regionality.locality_as_regionality
let regional_to_local = Locality_in_Regionality.regional_to_local
let regional_to_global = Locality_in_Regionality.regional_to_global
let local_to_regional = Locality_in_Regionality.local_to_regional
let global_to_regional = Locality_in_Regionality.global_to_regional


module Locality : sig
  module Const : sig
    type t = private int

    val global : t
    val local : t

    val bottom : t
    val top : t

    val leq : t -> t -> bool
    val equal : t -> t -> bool
    val join : t -> t -> t
    val meet : t -> t -> t
    val sub : t -> t -> t
    val imply : t -> t -> t

    val name : t -> string
    val of_name : string -> t option
    val pp : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val show : t -> string

    module Repr : sig
      val bits : int
      val mask : int
      val to_int : t -> int
      val of_int_exn : int -> t
    end

    val min : t
    val max : t
    val le : t -> t -> bool
    val print : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val legacy : t
  end
  type const = Const.t

  type 'd t constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  type l = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.disallowed) t
  type r = (Allowance.disallowed * Allowance.allowed) t
  type lr = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.allowed) t

  type simple_error = {
    left : const;
    right : const;
  }

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  val min : lr
  val max : lr
  val legacy : lr

  val of_const : const -> ('l * 'r) t
  val to_const_exn : lr -> const

  val newvar : unit -> ('l * 'r) t
  val newvar_above : l -> ('l * 'r) t * bool
  val newvar_below : r -> ('l * 'r) t * bool

  val to_simple_error : error -> simple_error
  val print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit
  val print_equate_error : Format.formatter -> equate_error -> unit

  val submode : l -> r -> (unit, error) result
  val submode_exn : l -> r -> unit
  val equate : lr -> lr -> (unit, equate_error) result
  val equate_exn : lr -> lr -> unit

  val join : l list -> l
  val meet : r list -> r

  val print : ?verbose:bool -> Format_doc.formatter -> ('l * 'r) t -> unit
  val show : ?verbose:bool -> ('l * 'r) t -> string

  val zap_to_floor : l -> const
  val zap_to_ceil : r -> const

  val global : lr
  val local : lr

end

module Locality_op : sig
  module Const : sig
    type t = Locality.Const.t

    val global : t
    val local : t

    val bottom : t
    val top : t

    val leq : t -> t -> bool
    val equal : t -> t -> bool
    val join : t -> t -> t
    val meet : t -> t -> t
    val sub : t -> t -> t
    val imply : t -> t -> t

    val name : t -> string

    val pp : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val show : t -> string

    module Repr : sig
      val bits : int
      val mask : int

      val of_int_exn : int -> t
    end

    val min : t

  end
  type const = Const.t

  type 'd t constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  type simple_error = {
    left : const;
    right : const;

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right

  val min : lr

  val legacy : lr

  val of_const : const -> ('l * 'r) t

  val newvar : unit -> ('l * 'r) t

  val to_simple_error : error -> simple_error

  val print_equate_error : Format.formatter -> equate_error -> unit

  val submode : l -> r -> (unit, error) result
  val submode_exn : l -> r -> unit
  val equate : lr -> lr -> (unit, equate_error) result
  val equate_exn : lr -> lr -> unit

  val meet : r list -> r

  val print : ?verbose:bool -> Format_doc.formatter -> ('l * 'r) t -> unit
  val show : ?verbose:bool -> ('l * 'r) t -> string

  val zap_to_floor : l -> const
  val zap_to_ceil : r -> const

  val global : lr
  val local : lr

end

module Regionality_op : sig
  module Const : sig
    type t = Regionality.Const.t

    val global : t

    val bottom : t
    val top : t

    val leq : t -> t -> bool

    val meet : t -> t -> t
    val sub : t -> t -> t
    val imply : t -> t -> t

    val name : t -> string
    val of_name : string -> t option
    val pp : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val show : t -> string

    module Repr : sig
      val bits : int
      val mask : int
      val to_int : t -> int
      val of_int_exn : int -> t
    end

    val min : t
    val max : t
    val le : t -> t -> bool
    val print : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val legacy : t
  end
  type const = Const.t

  type 'd t constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  type l = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.disallowed) t
  type r = (Allowance.disallowed * Allowance.allowed) t
  type lr = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.allowed) t

    left : const;
    right : const;
  }

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  val min : lr
  val max : lr

  val of_const : const -> ('l * 'r) t
  val to_const_exn : lr -> const

  val newvar_below : r -> ('l * 'r) t * bool

  val equate_exn : lr -> lr -> unit

  val meet : r list -> r

  val show : ?verbose:bool -> ('l * 'r) t -> string

  val zap_to_ceil : r -> const

  val print_equate_error : Format.formatter -> equate_error -> unit

  val equate : lr -> lr -> (unit, equate_error) result
  val equate_exn : lr -> lr -> unit

  val join : l list -> l
  val meet : r list -> r

  val print : ?verbose:bool -> Format_doc.formatter -> ('l * 'r) t -> unit
  val show : ?verbose:bool -> ('l * 'r) t -> string

  val zap_to_floor : l -> const
  val zap_to_ceil : r -> const

  val forkable : lr
  val unforkable : lr

end

    val non_null : t
    val maybe_null : t

    val bottom : t
    val top : t

    val leq : t -> t -> bool
    val equal : t -> t -> bool
    val join : t -> t -> t
    val meet : t -> t -> t
    val sub : t -> t -> t
    val imply : t -> t -> t

    val name : t -> string
    val of_name : string -> t option
    val pp : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val show : t -> string

    module Repr : sig
      val bits : int
      val mask : int
      val to_int : t -> int
      val of_int_exn : int -> t
    end

    val min : t
    val max : t
    val le : t -> t -> bool
    val print : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val legacy : t
  end
  type const = Const.t

  type 'd t constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  type l = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.disallowed) t
  type r = (Allowance.disallowed * Allowance.allowed) t
  type lr = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.allowed) t

  type simple_error = {
    left : const;
    right : const;
  }

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  val min : lr
  val max : lr
  val legacy : lr

  val of_const : const -> ('l * 'r) t
  val to_const_exn : lr -> const

  val newvar : unit -> ('l * 'r) t
  val newvar_above : l -> ('l * 'r) t * bool
  val newvar_below : r -> ('l * 'r) t * bool

  val to_simple_error : error -> simple_error
  val print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit
  val print_equate_error : Format.formatter -> equate_error -> unit

  val submode : l -> r -> (unit, error) result
  val submode_exn : l -> r -> unit
  val equate : lr -> lr -> (unit, equate_error) result
  val equate_exn : lr -> lr -> unit

  val join : l list -> l
  val meet : r list -> r

  val print : ?verbose:bool -> Format_doc.formatter -> ('l * 'r) t -> unit
  val show : ?verbose:bool -> ('l * 'r) t -> string

  val zap_to_floor : l -> const
  val zap_to_ceil : r -> const

  val non_null : lr
  val maybe_null : lr

end

module Monadic : sig
  module Field_Uniqueness = Uniqueness
  module Field_Contention = Contention
  module Field_Visibility = Visibility
  module Field_Staticity = Staticity

  module Axis : sig
    type _ t =
      | Uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t t
      | Contention : Field_Contention.Const.t t
      | Visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t t
      | Staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t t

    type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

    val compare : 'a t -> 'b t -> ('a, 'b) Misc.comparison

    val all : packed list
    val print : Format.formatter -> 'a t -> unit
  end

  module Const : sig
    type t = private int

    type view = {
      uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t;
      contention : Field_Contention.Const.t;
      visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t;
      staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t;
    }

    val make : uniqueness:Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> contention:Field_Contention.Const.t -> visibility:Field_Visibility.Const.t -> staticity:Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t
    val view : t -> view
    val of_view : view -> t

    val uniqueness : t -> Field_Uniqueness.Const.t
    val proj_uniqueness : t -> Field_Uniqueness.Const.t
    val with_uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t -> t
    val uniqueness_bot : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t
    val uniqueness_top : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t
    val contention : t -> Field_Contention.Const.t
    val proj_contention : t -> Field_Contention.Const.t
    val with_contention : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t -> t
    val contention_bot : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t
    val contention_top : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_contention : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_contention : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t
    val visibility : t -> Field_Visibility.Const.t
    val proj_visibility : t -> Field_Visibility.Const.t
    val with_visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t -> t
    val visibility_bot : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t
    val visibility_top : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t
    val staticity : t -> Field_Staticity.Const.t
    val proj_staticity : t -> Field_Staticity.Const.t
    val with_staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t -> t
    val staticity_bot : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t
    val staticity_top : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t

    val bottom : t
    val top : t

    val leq : t -> t -> bool
    val equal : t -> t -> bool
    val join : t -> t -> t
    val meet : t -> t -> t
    val sub : t -> t -> t
    val imply : t -> t -> t

    val pp : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val show : t -> string

    module Layout : sig
      val uniqueness_shift : int
      val uniqueness_mask : int
      val contention_shift : int
      val contention_mask : int
      val visibility_shift : int
      val visibility_mask : int
      val staticity_shift : int
      val staticity_mask : int
    end

    module Repr : sig
      val bits : int
      val mask : int
      val to_int : t -> int
      val of_int_exn : int -> t
    end

    val min : t
    val max : t
    val le : t -> t -> bool
    val print : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val legacy : t

    val split : t -> view
    val merge : view -> t

    val proj : 'a Axis.t -> t -> 'a
    val min_with : 'a Axis.t -> 'a -> t
    val max_with : 'a Axis.t -> 'a -> t
  end
  type const = Const.t

  type 'd t constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  type l = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.disallowed) t
  type r = (Allowance.disallowed * Allowance.allowed) t
  type lr = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.allowed) t

  type 'a simple_axerror

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  val min : lr
  val max : lr
  val legacy : lr

  val of_const : const -> ('l * 'r) t
  val to_const_exn : lr -> const

  val newvar : unit -> ('l * 'r) t
  val newvar_above : l -> ('l * 'r) t * bool
  val newvar_below : r -> ('l * 'r) t * bool

  val to_simple_error : error -> simple_error
  val print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit
  val print_equate_error : Format.formatter -> equate_error -> unit

  val submode : l -> r -> (unit, error) result
  val submode_exn : l -> r -> unit
  val equate : lr -> lr -> (unit, equate_error) result
  val equate_exn : lr -> lr -> unit

  val join : l list -> l
  val meet : r list -> r

  val print : ?verbose:bool -> Format_doc.formatter -> ('l * 'r) t -> unit
  val show : ?verbose:bool -> ('l * 'r) t -> string

  val zap_to_floor : l -> const
  val zap_to_ceil : r -> const

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  val proj : 'a Axis.t -> ('l * 'r) t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode
  val min_with : 'a Axis.t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with : 'a Axis.t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_uniqueness : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Uniqueness.t
  val min_with_uniqueness : ('l * 'r) Field_Uniqueness.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_uniqueness : ('l * 'r) Field_Uniqueness.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_contention : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Contention.t
  val min_with_contention : ('l * 'r) Field_Contention.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_contention : ('l * 'r) Field_Contention.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_visibility : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Visibility.t
  val min_with_visibility : ('l * 'r) Field_Visibility.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_visibility : ('l * 'r) Field_Visibility.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_staticity : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Staticity.t
  val min_with_staticity : ('l * 'r) Field_Staticity.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_staticity : ('l * 'r) Field_Staticity.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t

end

module Monadic_op : sig
  module Field_Uniqueness = Uniqueness_op
  module Field_Contention = Contention_op
  module Field_Visibility = Visibility_op
  module Field_Staticity = Staticity_op

  module Axis : sig
    type _ t =
      | Uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t t
      | Contention : Field_Contention.Const.t t
      | Visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t t
      | Staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t t

    type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

    val compare : 'a t -> 'b t -> ('a, 'b) Misc.comparison

    val all : packed list

  end

  module Const : sig
    type t = Monadic.Const.t

    type view = {
      uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t;
      contention : Field_Contention.Const.t;
      visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t;
      staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t;

    val make : uniqueness:Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> contention:Field_Contention.Const.t -> visibility:Field_Visibility.Const.t -> staticity:Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t
    val view : t -> view

    val uniqueness : t -> Field_Uniqueness.Const.t
    val proj_uniqueness : t -> Field_Uniqueness.Const.t
    val with_uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t -> t
    val uniqueness_bot : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t
    val uniqueness_top : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_uniqueness : Field_Uniqueness.Const.t -> t
    val contention : t -> Field_Contention.Const.t
    val proj_contention : t -> Field_Contention.Const.t
    val with_contention : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t -> t
    val contention_bot : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t
    val contention_top : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_contention : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_contention : Field_Contention.Const.t -> t
    val visibility : t -> Field_Visibility.Const.t
    val proj_visibility : t -> Field_Visibility.Const.t
    val with_visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t -> t
    val visibility_bot : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t
    val visibility_top : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_visibility : Field_Visibility.Const.t -> t
    val staticity : t -> Field_Staticity.Const.t
    val proj_staticity : t -> Field_Staticity.Const.t
    val with_staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t -> t
    val staticity_bot : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t
    val staticity_top : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_staticity : Field_Staticity.Const.t -> t

    val bottom : t
    val top : t

    val leq : t -> t -> bool
    val equal : t -> t -> bool
    val join : t -> t -> t
    val meet : t -> t -> t
    val sub : t -> t -> t
    val imply : t -> t -> t

    val pp : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val show : t -> string

    module Layout : sig
      val uniqueness_shift : int
      val uniqueness_mask : int
      val contention_shift : int
      val contention_mask : int
      val visibility_shift : int
      val visibility_mask : int
      val staticity_shift : int
      val staticity_mask : int
    end

    module Repr : sig
      val bits : int
      val mask : int
      val to_int : t -> int
      val of_int_exn : int -> t
    end

    val min : t
    val max : t
    val le : t -> t -> bool
    val print : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val legacy : t

    val split : t -> view
    val merge : view -> t

    val proj : 'a Axis.t -> t -> 'a
    val min_with : 'a Axis.t -> 'a -> t
    val max_with : 'a Axis.t -> 'a -> t
  end
  type const = Const.t

  type 'd t constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  type l = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.disallowed) t
  type r = (Allowance.disallowed * Allowance.allowed) t
  type lr = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.allowed) t

  type 'a simple_axerror

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  val min : lr
  val max : lr
  val legacy : lr

  val of_const : const -> ('l * 'r) t
  val to_const_exn : lr -> const

  val newvar : unit -> ('l * 'r) t
  val newvar_above : l -> ('l * 'r) t * bool
  val newvar_below : r -> ('l * 'r) t * bool

  val to_simple_error : error -> simple_error
  val print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit
  val print_equate_error : Format.formatter -> equate_error -> unit

  val submode : l -> r -> (unit, error) result
  val submode_exn : l -> r -> unit
  val equate : lr -> lr -> (unit, equate_error) result
  val equate_exn : lr -> lr -> unit

  val join : l list -> l
  val meet : r list -> r

  val print : ?verbose:bool -> Format_doc.formatter -> ('l * 'r) t -> unit
  val show : ?verbose:bool -> ('l * 'r) t -> string

  val zap_to_floor : l -> const
  val zap_to_ceil : r -> const

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  val proj : 'a Axis.t -> ('l * 'r) t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode
  val min_with : 'a Axis.t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with : 'a Axis.t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_uniqueness : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Uniqueness.t
  val min_with_uniqueness : ('l * 'r) Field_Uniqueness.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_uniqueness : ('l * 'r) Field_Uniqueness.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_contention : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Contention.t
  val min_with_contention : ('l * 'r) Field_Contention.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_contention : ('l * 'r) Field_Contention.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_visibility : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Visibility.t
  val min_with_visibility : ('l * 'r) Field_Visibility.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_visibility : ('l * 'r) Field_Visibility.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_staticity : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Staticity.t
  val min_with_staticity : ('l * 'r) Field_Staticity.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_staticity : ('l * 'r) Field_Staticity.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t

end

module Comonadic : sig
  module Field_Linearity = Linearity
  module Field_Portability = Portability
  module Field_Forkable = Forkable
  module Field_Yielding = Yielding
  module Field_Statefulness = Statefulness

  module Axis : sig
    type _ t =
      | Linearity : Field_Linearity.Const.t t
      | Portability : Field_Portability.Const.t t
      | Forkable : Field_Forkable.Const.t t
      | Yielding : Field_Yielding.Const.t t
      | Statefulness : Field_Statefulness.Const.t t

    type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

    val compare : 'a t -> 'b t -> ('a, 'b) Misc.comparison

    val all : packed list
    val print : Format.formatter -> 'a t -> unit
  end

  module Const : sig
    type t = private int

    type view = {
      linearity : Field_Linearity.Const.t;
      portability : Field_Portability.Const.t;
      forkable : Field_Forkable.Const.t;
      yielding : Field_Yielding.Const.t;
      statefulness : Field_Statefulness.Const.t;
    }

    val make : linearity:Field_Linearity.Const.t -> portability:Field_Portability.Const.t -> forkable:Field_Forkable.Const.t -> yielding:Field_Yielding.Const.t -> statefulness:Field_Statefulness.Const.t -> t
    val view : t -> view
    val of_view : view -> t

    val linearity : t -> Field_Linearity.Const.t
    val proj_linearity : t -> Field_Linearity.Const.t
    val with_linearity : Field_Linearity.Const.t -> t -> t
    val linearity_bot : Field_Linearity.Const.t -> t
    val linearity_top : Field_Linearity.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_linearity : Field_Linearity.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_linearity : Field_Linearity.Const.t -> t
    val portability : t -> Field_Portability.Const.t
    val proj_portability : t -> Field_Portability.Const.t
    val with_portability : Field_Portability.Const.t -> t -> t
    val portability_bot : Field_Portability.Const.t -> t
    val portability_top : Field_Portability.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_portability : Field_Portability.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_portability : Field_Portability.Const.t -> t
    val forkable : t -> Field_Forkable.Const.t
    val proj_forkable : t -> Field_Forkable.Const.t
    val with_forkable : Field_Forkable.Const.t -> t -> t
    val forkable_bot : Field_Forkable.Const.t -> t
    val forkable_top : Field_Forkable.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_forkable : Field_Forkable.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_forkable : Field_Forkable.Const.t -> t
    val yielding : t -> Field_Yielding.Const.t
    val proj_yielding : t -> Field_Yielding.Const.t
    val with_yielding : Field_Yielding.Const.t -> t -> t
    val yielding_bot : Field_Yielding.Const.t -> t
    val yielding_top : Field_Yielding.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_yielding : Field_Yielding.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_yielding : Field_Yielding.Const.t -> t
    val statefulness : t -> Field_Statefulness.Const.t
    val proj_statefulness : t -> Field_Statefulness.Const.t
    val with_statefulness : Field_Statefulness.Const.t -> t -> t
    val statefulness_bot : Field_Statefulness.Const.t -> t
    val statefulness_top : Field_Statefulness.Const.t -> t
    val min_with_statefulness : Field_Statefulness.Const.t -> t
    val max_with_statefulness : Field_Statefulness.Const.t -> t

    val bottom : t
    val top : t

    val leq : t -> t -> bool
    val equal : t -> t -> bool
    val join : t -> t -> t
    val meet : t -> t -> t
    val sub : t -> t -> t
    val imply : t -> t -> t

    val pp : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val show : t -> string

    module Layout : sig
      val linearity_shift : int
      val linearity_mask : int
      val portability_shift : int
      val portability_mask : int
      val forkable_shift : int
      val forkable_mask : int
      val yielding_shift : int
      val yielding_mask : int
      val statefulness_shift : int
      val statefulness_mask : int
    end

    module Repr : sig
      val bits : int
      val mask : int
      val to_int : t -> int
      val of_int_exn : int -> t
    end

    val min : t
    val max : t
    val le : t -> t -> bool
    val print : Format.formatter -> t -> unit
    val legacy : t

    val split : t -> view
    val merge : view -> t

    val proj : 'a Axis.t -> t -> 'a
    val min_with : 'a Axis.t -> 'a -> t
    val max_with : 'a Axis.t -> 'a -> t
  end
  type const = Const.t

  type 'd t constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  type l = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.disallowed) t
  type r = (Allowance.disallowed * Allowance.allowed) t
  type lr = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.allowed) t

  type 'a simple_axerror

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  val min : lr
  val max : lr
  val legacy : lr

  val of_const : const -> ('l * 'r) t
  val to_const_exn : lr -> const

  val newvar : unit -> ('l * 'r) t
  val newvar_above : l -> ('l * 'r) t * bool
  val newvar_below : r -> ('l * 'r) t * bool

  val to_simple_error : error -> simple_error
  val print_error : Format.formatter -> error -> unit
  val print_equate_error : Format.formatter -> equate_error -> unit

  val submode : l -> r -> (unit, error) result
  val submode_exn : l -> r -> unit
  val equate : lr -> lr -> (unit, equate_error) result
  val equate_exn : lr -> lr -> unit

  val join : l list -> l
  val meet : r list -> r

  val print : ?verbose:bool -> Format_doc.formatter -> ('l * 'r) t -> unit
  val show : ?verbose:bool -> ('l * 'r) t -> string

  val zap_to_floor : l -> const
  val zap_to_ceil : r -> const

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  val proj : 'a Axis.t -> ('l * 'r) t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode
  val min_with : 'a Axis.t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with : 'a Axis.t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_linearity : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Linearity.t
  val min_with_linearity : ('l * 'r) Field_Linearity.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_linearity : ('l * 'r) Field_Linearity.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_portability : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Portability.t
  val min_with_portability : ('l * 'r) Field_Portability.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_portability : ('l * 'r) Field_Portability.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_forkable : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Forkable.t
  val min_with_forkable : ('l * 'r) Field_Forkable.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_forkable : ('l * 'r) Field_Forkable.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_yielding : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Yielding.t
  val min_with_yielding : ('l * 'r) Field_Yielding.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_yielding : ('l * 'r) Field_Yielding.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_statefulness : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Statefulness.t
  val min_with_statefulness : ('l * 'r) Field_Statefulness.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_statefulness : ('l * 'r) Field_Statefulness.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t

end

module Comonadic_with_locality : sig
  module Field_Areality = Locality
  module Field_Comonadic = Comonadic

  module Axis : sig
    type _ t =
      | Areality : Field_Areality.Const.t t
      | Comonadic : Field_Comonadic.Const.t t

    type packed = P : 'a t -> packed

    val compare : 'a t -> 'b t -> ('a, 'b) Misc.comparison

    val all : packed list
    val print : Format.formatter -> 'a t -> unit
  end

  module Const : sig
    type t = private int

    type view = {
      areality : Field_Areality.Const.t;
      comonadic : Field_Comonadic.Const.t;
    }

    val make : areality:Field_Areality.Const.t -> comonadic:Field_Comonadic.Const.t -> t
    val view : t -> view
    val of_view : view -> t

    val areality : t -> Field_Areality.Const.t

    val max_with_areality : Field_Areality.Const.t -> t

    val max_with_comonadic : Field_Comonadic.Const.t -> t

    val bottom : t
    val top : t

    val equal : t -> t -> bool

    end

    module Repr : sig
      val bits : int

      val of_int_exn : int -> t

    val min : t

    val merge : view -> t

    val proj : 'a Axis.t -> t -> 'a
    val min_with : 'a Axis.t -> 'a -> t
    val max_with : 'a Axis.t -> 'a -> t
  end
  type const = Const.t

  type 'd t constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  type l = (Allowance.allowed * Allowance.disallowed) t
  type r = (Allowance.disallowed * Allowance.allowed) t

  type 'a simple_axerror

  type simple_error = Error : 'a Axis.t * 'a simple_axerror -> simple_error

  type error = simple_error

  type equate_step =
    | Left_le_right
    | Right_le_left

  type equate_error = equate_step * error

  val min : lr
  val max : lr

  val of_const : const -> ('l * 'r) t
  val to_const_exn : lr -> const

  val newvar : unit -> ('l * 'r) t

  val newvar_below : r -> ('l * 'r) t * bool

  val show : ?verbose:bool -> ('l * 'r) t -> string

  val zap_to_floor : l -> const
  val zap_to_ceil : r -> const

  type ('a, 'd) axis_mode constraint 'd = 'l * 'r

  val proj : 'a Axis.t -> ('l * 'r) t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode

  val max_with : 'a Axis.t -> ('a, 'l * 'r) axis_mode -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_areality : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Areality.t
  val min_with_areality : ('l * 'r) Field_Areality.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_areality : ('l * 'r) Field_Areality.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t
  val proj_comonadic : ('l * 'r) t -> ('l * 'r) Field_Comonadic.t
  val min_with_comonadic : ('l * 'r) Field_Comonadic.t -> ('l * Allowance.disallowed) t
  val max_with_comonadic : ('l * 'r) Field_Comonadic.t -> (Allowance.disallowed * 'r) t

end
