  check_duality ~name:"Pointerness" ~values:values_pointerness ~bottom:Pointerness.Const.bottom ~top:Pointerness.Const.top ~join:Pointerness.Const.join ~meet:Pointerness.Const.meet ~sub:Pointerness.Const.sub ~imply:Pointerness.Const.imply ~op_bottom:Pointerness_op.Const.bottom ~op_top:Pointerness_op.Const.top ~op_join:Pointerness_op.Const.join ~op_meet:Pointerness_op.Const.meet ~op_sub:Pointerness_op.Const.sub ~op_imply:Pointerness_op.Const.imply ~show:Pointerness.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Pointerness" ~values:values_pointerness ~bottom:Pointerness.Const.bottom ~top:Pointerness.Const.top ~leq:Pointerness.Const.leq ~equal:Pointerness.Const.equal ~solver_min:Pointerness.min ~solver_max:Pointerness.max ~of_const:Pointerness.of_const ~to_const_exn:Pointerness.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Pointerness.newvar_above (Pointerness.of_const value) in Pointerness.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Pointerness.newvar_below (Pointerness.of_const value) in Pointerness.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Pointerness.submode (Pointerness.of_const x) (Pointerness.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Pointerness.equate (Pointerness.of_const x) (Pointerness.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Pointerness.newvar () in Pointerness.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Pointerness.newvar () in Pointerness.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Pointerness.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Pointerness_op" ~values:values_pointerness_op ~bottom:Pointerness_op.Const.bottom ~top:Pointerness_op.Const.top ~leq:Pointerness_op.Const.leq ~equal:Pointerness_op.Const.equal ~solver_min:Pointerness_op.min ~solver_max:Pointerness_op.max ~of_const:Pointerness_op.of_const ~to_const_exn:Pointerness_op.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Pointerness_op.newvar_above (Pointerness_op.of_const value) in Pointerness_op.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Pointerness_op.newvar_below (Pointerness_op.of_const value) in Pointerness_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Pointerness_op.submode (Pointerness_op.of_const x) (Pointerness_op.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Pointerness_op.equate (Pointerness_op.of_const x) (Pointerness_op.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Pointerness_op.newvar () in Pointerness_op.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Pointerness_op.newvar () in Pointerness_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Pointerness_op.Const.show;
  ()

let () =
  iter2 values_locality values_locality (fun x y ->
    let ex = Locality_in_Regionality.embed x in
    let ey = Locality_in_Regionality.embed y in
    check_valid ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.embed(x)" ~to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Regionality.Const.show ex;
    check_valid ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.embed(y)" ~to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Regionality.Const.show ey;
    ensure ((not (Locality.Const.leq x y)) || Regionality.Const.leq ex ey) "Locality_in_Regionality: order preservation failed";
    ensure ((not (Regionality.Const.leq ex ey)) || Locality.Const.leq x y) "Locality_in_Regionality: order reflection failed");
  check_adjunction ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.left1/embed" ~a_values:values_regionality ~b_values:values_locality ~leq_a:Regionality.Const.leq ~leq_b:Locality.Const.leq ~f:Locality_in_Regionality.left1 ~g:Locality_in_Regionality.embed ~show_f:Locality.Const.show ~show_g:Regionality.Const.show ~f_to_int:Locality.Const.Repr.to_int ~f_of_int_exn:Locality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~g_to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~g_of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn;
  check_adjunction ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.left2/left1" ~a_values:values_locality ~b_values:values_regionality ~leq_a:Locality.Const.leq ~leq_b:Regionality.Const.leq ~f:Locality_in_Regionality.left2 ~g:Locality_in_Regionality.left1 ~show_f:Regionality.Const.show ~show_g:Locality.Const.show ~f_to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~f_of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~g_to_int:Locality.Const.Repr.to_int ~g_of_int_exn:Locality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn;
  check_adjunction ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.embed/right1" ~a_values:values_locality ~b_values:values_regionality ~leq_a:Locality.Const.leq ~leq_b:Regionality.Const.leq ~f:Locality_in_Regionality.embed ~g:Locality_in_Regionality.right1 ~show_f:Regionality.Const.show ~show_g:Locality.Const.show ~f_to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~f_of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~g_to_int:Locality.Const.Repr.to_int ~g_of_int_exn:Locality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn;
  check_adjunction ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.right1/right2" ~a_values:values_regionality ~b_values:values_locality ~leq_a:Regionality.Const.leq ~leq_b:Locality.Const.leq ~f:Locality_in_Regionality.right1 ~g:Locality_in_Regionality.right2 ~show_f:Locality.Const.show ~show_g:Regionality.Const.show ~f_to_int:Locality.Const.Repr.to_int ~f_of_int_exn:Locality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~g_to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~g_of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.locality_as_regionality" ~values:values_locality ~f:Locality_in_Regionality.locality_as_regionality ~g:Locality_in_Regionality.embed ~to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.regional_to_local" ~values:values_regionality ~f:Locality_in_Regionality.regional_to_local ~g:Locality_in_Regionality.left1 ~to_int:Locality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Locality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Locality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.regional_to_global" ~values:values_regionality ~f:Locality_in_Regionality.regional_to_global ~g:Locality_in_Regionality.right1 ~to_int:Locality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Locality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Locality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.local_to_regional" ~values:values_locality ~f:Locality_in_Regionality.local_to_regional ~g:Locality_in_Regionality.left2 ~to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Locality_in_Regionality.global_to_regional" ~values:values_locality ~f:Locality_in_Regionality.global_to_regional ~g:Locality_in_Regionality.right2 ~to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Regionality.Const.show;
  ()

let () =
  check_repr ~name:"Monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~mask:Monadic.Const.Repr.mask ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~bottom:Monadic.Const.bottom ~top:Monadic.Const.top ~leq:Monadic.Const.leq ~join:Monadic.Const.join ~meet:Monadic.Const.meet ~sub:Monadic.Const.sub ~imply:Monadic.Const.imply ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Monadic_op" ~values:values_monadic_op ~bottom:Monadic_op.Const.bottom ~top:Monadic_op.Const.top ~leq:Monadic_op.Const.leq ~join:Monadic_op.Const.join ~meet:Monadic_op.Const.meet ~sub:Monadic_op.Const.sub ~imply:Monadic_op.Const.imply ~to_int:Monadic_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic_op.Const.show;
  check_duality ~name:"Monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~bottom:Monadic.Const.bottom ~top:Monadic.Const.top ~join:Monadic.Const.join ~meet:Monadic.Const.meet ~sub:Monadic.Const.sub ~imply:Monadic.Const.imply ~op_bottom:Monadic_op.Const.bottom ~op_top:Monadic_op.Const.top ~op_join:Monadic_op.Const.join ~op_meet:Monadic_op.Const.meet ~op_sub:Monadic_op.Const.sub ~op_imply:Monadic_op.Const.imply ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Monadic.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness.Const.bottom;
      contention = Contention.Const.bottom;
      visibility = Visibility.Const.bottom;
      staticity = Staticity.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Monadic.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness.Const.top;
      contention = Contention.Const.top;
      visibility = Visibility.Const.top;
      staticity = Staticity.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Monadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic.Const.view y in
    Uniqueness.Const.leq xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness
    && Contention.Const.leq xv.contention yv.contention
    && Visibility.Const.leq xv.visibility yv.visibility
    && Staticity.Const.leq xv.staticity yv.staticity
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Monadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic.Const.view y in
    Monadic.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness.Const.join xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness;
      contention = Contention.Const.join xv.contention yv.contention;
      visibility = Visibility.Const.join xv.visibility yv.visibility;
      staticity = Staticity.Const.join xv.staticity yv.staticity;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Monadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic.Const.view y in
    Monadic.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness.Const.meet xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness;
      contention = Contention.Const.meet xv.contention yv.contention;
      visibility = Visibility.Const.meet xv.visibility yv.visibility;
      staticity = Staticity.Const.meet xv.staticity yv.staticity;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Monadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic.Const.view y in
    Monadic.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness.Const.sub xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness;
      contention = Contention.Const.sub xv.contention yv.contention;
      visibility = Visibility.Const.sub xv.visibility yv.visibility;
      staticity = Staticity.Const.sub xv.staticity yv.staticity;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Monadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic.Const.view y in
    Monadic.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness.Const.imply xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness;
      contention = Contention.Const.imply xv.contention yv.contention;
      visibility = Visibility.Const.imply xv.visibility yv.visibility;
      staticity = Staticity.Const.imply xv.staticity yv.staticity;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~bottom:Monadic.Const.bottom ~top:Monadic.Const.top ~leq:Monadic.Const.leq ~join:Monadic.Const.join ~meet:Monadic.Const.meet ~sub:Monadic.Const.sub ~imply:Monadic.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~bottom:Monadic.Const.bottom ~top:Monadic.Const.top ~leq:Monadic.Const.leq ~equal:Monadic.Const.equal ~solver_min:Monadic.min ~solver_max:Monadic.max ~of_const:Monadic.of_const ~to_const_exn:Monadic.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Monadic.newvar_above (Monadic.of_const value) in Monadic.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Monadic.newvar_below (Monadic.of_const value) in Monadic.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Monadic.submode (Monadic.of_const x) (Monadic.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Monadic.equate (Monadic.of_const x) (Monadic.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Monadic.newvar () in Monadic.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Monadic.newvar () in Monadic.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Monadic.Solver.uniqueness" ~product_values:values_monadic ~field_values:values_uniqueness ~product_of_const:Monadic.of_const ~field_of_const:Uniqueness.of_const ~field_to_const:Uniqueness.to_const_exn ~proj:Monadic.proj_uniqueness ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Monadic.zap_to_floor (Monadic.min_with_uniqueness x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Monadic.zap_to_ceil (Monadic.max_with_uniqueness x)) ~newvar:Monadic.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Uniqueness.equate x (Uniqueness.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Monadic.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Monadic.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Monadic.Const.uniqueness ~field_bot:Monadic.Const.uniqueness_bot ~field_top:Monadic.Const.uniqueness_top ~product_show:Monadic.Const.show ~field_show:Uniqueness.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Monadic.Solver.contention" ~product_values:values_monadic ~field_values:values_contention ~product_of_const:Monadic.of_const ~field_of_const:Contention.of_const ~field_to_const:Contention.to_const_exn ~proj:Monadic.proj_contention ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Monadic.zap_to_floor (Monadic.min_with_contention x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Monadic.zap_to_ceil (Monadic.max_with_contention x)) ~newvar:Monadic.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Contention.equate x (Contention.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Monadic.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Monadic.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Monadic.Const.contention ~field_bot:Monadic.Const.contention_bot ~field_top:Monadic.Const.contention_top ~product_show:Monadic.Const.show ~field_show:Contention.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Monadic.Solver.visibility" ~product_values:values_monadic ~field_values:values_visibility ~product_of_const:Monadic.of_const ~field_of_const:Visibility.of_const ~field_to_const:Visibility.to_const_exn ~proj:Monadic.proj_visibility ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Monadic.zap_to_floor (Monadic.min_with_visibility x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Monadic.zap_to_ceil (Monadic.max_with_visibility x)) ~newvar:Monadic.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Visibility.equate x (Visibility.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Monadic.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Monadic.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Monadic.Const.visibility ~field_bot:Monadic.Const.visibility_bot ~field_top:Monadic.Const.visibility_top ~product_show:Monadic.Const.show ~field_show:Visibility.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Monadic.Solver.staticity" ~product_values:values_monadic ~field_values:values_staticity ~product_of_const:Monadic.of_const ~field_of_const:Staticity.of_const ~field_to_const:Staticity.to_const_exn ~proj:Monadic.proj_staticity ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Monadic.zap_to_floor (Monadic.min_with_staticity x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Monadic.zap_to_ceil (Monadic.max_with_staticity x)) ~newvar:Monadic.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Staticity.equate x (Staticity.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Monadic.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Monadic.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Monadic.Const.staticity ~field_bot:Monadic.Const.staticity_bot ~field_top:Monadic.Const.staticity_top ~product_show:Monadic.Const.show ~field_show:Staticity.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Monadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness_op.Const.bottom;
      contention = Contention_op.Const.bottom;
      visibility = Visibility_op.Const.bottom;
      staticity = Staticity_op.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Monadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness_op.Const.top;
      contention = Contention_op.Const.top;
      visibility = Visibility_op.Const.top;
      staticity = Staticity_op.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Monadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic_op.Const.view y in
    Uniqueness_op.Const.leq xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness
    && Contention_op.Const.leq xv.contention yv.contention
    && Visibility_op.Const.leq xv.visibility yv.visibility
    && Staticity_op.Const.leq xv.staticity yv.staticity
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Monadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic_op.Const.view y in
    Monadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness_op.Const.join xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness;
      contention = Contention_op.Const.join xv.contention yv.contention;
      visibility = Visibility_op.Const.join xv.visibility yv.visibility;
      staticity = Staticity_op.Const.join xv.staticity yv.staticity;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Monadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic_op.Const.view y in
    Monadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness_op.Const.meet xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness;
      contention = Contention_op.Const.meet xv.contention yv.contention;
      visibility = Visibility_op.Const.meet xv.visibility yv.visibility;
      staticity = Staticity_op.Const.meet xv.staticity yv.staticity;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Monadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic_op.Const.view y in
    Monadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness_op.Const.sub xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness;
      contention = Contention_op.Const.sub xv.contention yv.contention;
      visibility = Visibility_op.Const.sub xv.visibility yv.visibility;
      staticity = Staticity_op.Const.sub xv.staticity yv.staticity;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Monadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Monadic_op.Const.view y in
    Monadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      uniqueness = Uniqueness_op.Const.imply xv.uniqueness yv.uniqueness;
      contention = Contention_op.Const.imply xv.contention yv.contention;
      visibility = Visibility_op.Const.imply xv.visibility yv.visibility;
      staticity = Staticity_op.Const.imply xv.staticity yv.staticity;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Monadic_op" ~values:values_monadic_op ~bottom:Monadic_op.Const.bottom ~top:Monadic_op.Const.top ~leq:Monadic_op.Const.leq ~join:Monadic_op.Const.join ~meet:Monadic_op.Const.meet ~sub:Monadic_op.Const.sub ~imply:Monadic_op.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Monadic_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic_op.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Monadic_op" ~values:values_monadic_op ~bottom:Monadic_op.Const.bottom ~top:Monadic_op.Const.top ~leq:Monadic_op.Const.leq ~equal:Monadic_op.Const.equal ~solver_min:Monadic_op.min ~solver_max:Monadic_op.max ~of_const:Monadic_op.of_const ~to_const_exn:Monadic_op.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Monadic_op.newvar_above (Monadic_op.of_const value) in Monadic_op.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Monadic_op.newvar_below (Monadic_op.of_const value) in Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Monadic_op.submode (Monadic_op.of_const x) (Monadic_op.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Monadic_op.equate (Monadic_op.of_const x) (Monadic_op.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Monadic_op.newvar () in Monadic_op.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Monadic_op.newvar () in Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Monadic_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Monadic_op.Solver.uniqueness" ~product_values:values_monadic_op ~field_values:values_uniqueness_op ~product_of_const:Monadic_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Uniqueness_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Uniqueness_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Monadic_op.proj_uniqueness ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Monadic_op.zap_to_floor (Monadic_op.min_with_uniqueness x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Monadic_op.max_with_uniqueness x)) ~newvar:Monadic_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Uniqueness_op.equate x (Uniqueness_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Monadic_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Monadic_op.Const.uniqueness ~field_bot:Monadic_op.Const.uniqueness_bot ~field_top:Monadic_op.Const.uniqueness_top ~product_show:Monadic_op.Const.show ~field_show:Uniqueness_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Monadic_op.Solver.contention" ~product_values:values_monadic_op ~field_values:values_contention_op ~product_of_const:Monadic_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Contention_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Contention_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Monadic_op.proj_contention ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Monadic_op.zap_to_floor (Monadic_op.min_with_contention x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Monadic_op.max_with_contention x)) ~newvar:Monadic_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Contention_op.equate x (Contention_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Monadic_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Monadic_op.Const.contention ~field_bot:Monadic_op.Const.contention_bot ~field_top:Monadic_op.Const.contention_top ~product_show:Monadic_op.Const.show ~field_show:Contention_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Monadic_op.Solver.visibility" ~product_values:values_monadic_op ~field_values:values_visibility_op ~product_of_const:Monadic_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Visibility_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Visibility_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Monadic_op.proj_visibility ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Monadic_op.zap_to_floor (Monadic_op.min_with_visibility x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Monadic_op.max_with_visibility x)) ~newvar:Monadic_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Visibility_op.equate x (Visibility_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Monadic_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Monadic_op.Const.visibility ~field_bot:Monadic_op.Const.visibility_bot ~field_top:Monadic_op.Const.visibility_top ~product_show:Monadic_op.Const.show ~field_show:Visibility_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Monadic_op.Solver.staticity" ~product_values:values_monadic_op ~field_values:values_staticity_op ~product_of_const:Monadic_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Staticity_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Staticity_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Monadic_op.proj_staticity ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Monadic_op.zap_to_floor (Monadic_op.min_with_staticity x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Monadic_op.max_with_staticity x)) ~newvar:Monadic_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Staticity_op.equate x (Staticity_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Monadic_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Monadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Monadic_op.Const.staticity ~field_bot:Monadic_op.Const.staticity_bot ~field_top:Monadic_op.Const.staticity_top ~product_show:Monadic_op.Const.show ~field_show:Staticity_op.Const.show;
  check_product_roundtrip ~name:"Monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~view:Monadic.Const.view ~of_view:Monadic.Const.of_view ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  iter1 values_monadic (fun value ->
    let made = Monadic.Const.make ~uniqueness:(Monadic.Const.uniqueness value) ~contention:(Monadic.Const.contention value) ~visibility:(Monadic.Const.visibility value) ~staticity:(Monadic.Const.staticity value) in
    check_valid ~name:"Monadic" ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show made;
    ensure (made = value) "Monadic: make/projection roundtrip failed");
  check_field_projection ~name:"Monadic.uniqueness" ~product_values:values_monadic ~field_values:values_uniqueness ~product_leq:Monadic.Const.leq ~field_leq:Uniqueness.Const.leq ~field:Monadic.Const.uniqueness ~with_field:Monadic.Const.with_uniqueness ~field_bot:Monadic.Const.uniqueness_bot ~field_top:Monadic.Const.uniqueness_top ~product_to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Monadic.Const.show ~field_to_int:Uniqueness.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Uniqueness.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Uniqueness.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.proj_uniqueness" ~values:values_monadic ~f:Monadic.Const.proj_uniqueness ~g:Monadic.Const.uniqueness ~to_int:Uniqueness.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Uniqueness.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Uniqueness.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.min_with_uniqueness" ~values:values_uniqueness ~f:Monadic.Const.min_with_uniqueness ~g:Monadic.Const.uniqueness_bot ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.max_with_uniqueness" ~values:values_uniqueness ~f:Monadic.Const.max_with_uniqueness ~g:Monadic.Const.uniqueness_top ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.proj.uniqueness" ~values:values_monadic ~f:(Monadic.Const.proj Monadic.Axis.Uniqueness) ~g:Monadic.Const.uniqueness ~to_int:Uniqueness.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Uniqueness.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Uniqueness.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.min_with.uniqueness" ~values:values_uniqueness ~f:(Monadic.Const.min_with Monadic.Axis.Uniqueness) ~g:Monadic.Const.uniqueness_bot ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.max_with.uniqueness" ~values:values_uniqueness ~f:(Monadic.Const.max_with Monadic.Axis.Uniqueness) ~g:Monadic.Const.uniqueness_top ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Monadic.contention" ~product_values:values_monadic ~field_values:values_contention ~product_leq:Monadic.Const.leq ~field_leq:Contention.Const.leq ~field:Monadic.Const.contention ~with_field:Monadic.Const.with_contention ~field_bot:Monadic.Const.contention_bot ~field_top:Monadic.Const.contention_top ~product_to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Monadic.Const.show ~field_to_int:Contention.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Contention.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Contention.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.proj_contention" ~values:values_monadic ~f:Monadic.Const.proj_contention ~g:Monadic.Const.contention ~to_int:Contention.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Contention.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Contention.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.min_with_contention" ~values:values_contention ~f:Monadic.Const.min_with_contention ~g:Monadic.Const.contention_bot ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.max_with_contention" ~values:values_contention ~f:Monadic.Const.max_with_contention ~g:Monadic.Const.contention_top ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.proj.contention" ~values:values_monadic ~f:(Monadic.Const.proj Monadic.Axis.Contention) ~g:Monadic.Const.contention ~to_int:Contention.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Contention.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Contention.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.min_with.contention" ~values:values_contention ~f:(Monadic.Const.min_with Monadic.Axis.Contention) ~g:Monadic.Const.contention_bot ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.max_with.contention" ~values:values_contention ~f:(Monadic.Const.max_with Monadic.Axis.Contention) ~g:Monadic.Const.contention_top ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Monadic.visibility" ~product_values:values_monadic ~field_values:values_visibility ~product_leq:Monadic.Const.leq ~field_leq:Visibility.Const.leq ~field:Monadic.Const.visibility ~with_field:Monadic.Const.with_visibility ~field_bot:Monadic.Const.visibility_bot ~field_top:Monadic.Const.visibility_top ~product_to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Monadic.Const.show ~field_to_int:Visibility.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Visibility.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Visibility.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.proj_visibility" ~values:values_monadic ~f:Monadic.Const.proj_visibility ~g:Monadic.Const.visibility ~to_int:Visibility.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Visibility.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Visibility.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.min_with_visibility" ~values:values_visibility ~f:Monadic.Const.min_with_visibility ~g:Monadic.Const.visibility_bot ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.max_with_visibility" ~values:values_visibility ~f:Monadic.Const.max_with_visibility ~g:Monadic.Const.visibility_top ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.proj.visibility" ~values:values_monadic ~f:(Monadic.Const.proj Monadic.Axis.Visibility) ~g:Monadic.Const.visibility ~to_int:Visibility.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Visibility.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Visibility.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.min_with.visibility" ~values:values_visibility ~f:(Monadic.Const.min_with Monadic.Axis.Visibility) ~g:Monadic.Const.visibility_bot ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.max_with.visibility" ~values:values_visibility ~f:(Monadic.Const.max_with Monadic.Axis.Visibility) ~g:Monadic.Const.visibility_top ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Monadic.staticity" ~product_values:values_monadic ~field_values:values_staticity ~product_leq:Monadic.Const.leq ~field_leq:Staticity.Const.leq ~field:Monadic.Const.staticity ~with_field:Monadic.Const.with_staticity ~field_bot:Monadic.Const.staticity_bot ~field_top:Monadic.Const.staticity_top ~product_to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Monadic.Const.show ~field_to_int:Staticity.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Staticity.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Staticity.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.proj_staticity" ~values:values_monadic ~f:Monadic.Const.proj_staticity ~g:Monadic.Const.staticity ~to_int:Staticity.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Staticity.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Staticity.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.min_with_staticity" ~values:values_staticity ~f:Monadic.Const.min_with_staticity ~g:Monadic.Const.staticity_bot ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.max_with_staticity" ~values:values_staticity ~f:Monadic.Const.max_with_staticity ~g:Monadic.Const.staticity_top ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.proj.staticity" ~values:values_monadic ~f:(Monadic.Const.proj Monadic.Axis.Staticity) ~g:Monadic.Const.staticity ~to_int:Staticity.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Staticity.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Staticity.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.min_with.staticity" ~values:values_staticity ~f:(Monadic.Const.min_with Monadic.Axis.Staticity) ~g:Monadic.Const.staticity_bot ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Monadic.Const.max_with.staticity" ~values:values_staticity ~f:(Monadic.Const.max_with Monadic.Axis.Staticity) ~g:Monadic.Const.staticity_top ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  ()

let () =
  check_repr ~name:"Comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~mask:Comonadic.Const.Repr.mask ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~bottom:Comonadic.Const.bottom ~top:Comonadic.Const.top ~leq:Comonadic.Const.leq ~join:Comonadic.Const.join ~meet:Comonadic.Const.meet ~sub:Comonadic.Const.sub ~imply:Comonadic.Const.imply ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Comonadic_op" ~values:values_comonadic_op ~bottom:Comonadic_op.Const.bottom ~top:Comonadic_op.Const.top ~leq:Comonadic_op.Const.leq ~join:Comonadic_op.Const.join ~meet:Comonadic_op.Const.meet ~sub:Comonadic_op.Const.sub ~imply:Comonadic_op.Const.imply ~to_int:Comonadic_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_op.Const.show;
  check_duality ~name:"Comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~bottom:Comonadic.Const.bottom ~top:Comonadic.Const.top ~join:Comonadic.Const.join ~meet:Comonadic.Const.meet ~sub:Comonadic.Const.sub ~imply:Comonadic.Const.imply ~op_bottom:Comonadic_op.Const.bottom ~op_top:Comonadic_op.Const.top ~op_join:Comonadic_op.Const.join ~op_meet:Comonadic_op.Const.meet ~op_sub:Comonadic_op.Const.sub ~op_imply:Comonadic_op.Const.imply ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Comonadic.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity.Const.bottom;
      portability = Portability.Const.bottom;
      forkable = Forkable.Const.bottom;
      yielding = Yielding.Const.bottom;
      statefulness = Statefulness.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Comonadic.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity.Const.top;
      portability = Portability.Const.top;
      forkable = Forkable.Const.top;
      yielding = Yielding.Const.top;
      statefulness = Statefulness.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Comonadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic.Const.view y in
    Linearity.Const.leq xv.linearity yv.linearity
    && Portability.Const.leq xv.portability yv.portability
    && Forkable.Const.leq xv.forkable yv.forkable
    && Yielding.Const.leq xv.yielding yv.yielding
    && Statefulness.Const.leq xv.statefulness yv.statefulness
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Comonadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic.Const.view y in
    Comonadic.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity.Const.join xv.linearity yv.linearity;
      portability = Portability.Const.join xv.portability yv.portability;
      forkable = Forkable.Const.join xv.forkable yv.forkable;
      yielding = Yielding.Const.join xv.yielding yv.yielding;
      statefulness = Statefulness.Const.join xv.statefulness yv.statefulness;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Comonadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic.Const.view y in
    Comonadic.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity.Const.meet xv.linearity yv.linearity;
      portability = Portability.Const.meet xv.portability yv.portability;
      forkable = Forkable.Const.meet xv.forkable yv.forkable;
      yielding = Yielding.Const.meet xv.yielding yv.yielding;
      statefulness = Statefulness.Const.meet xv.statefulness yv.statefulness;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Comonadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic.Const.view y in
    Comonadic.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity.Const.sub xv.linearity yv.linearity;
      portability = Portability.Const.sub xv.portability yv.portability;
      forkable = Forkable.Const.sub xv.forkable yv.forkable;
      yielding = Yielding.Const.sub xv.yielding yv.yielding;
      statefulness = Statefulness.Const.sub xv.statefulness yv.statefulness;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Comonadic.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic.Const.view y in
    Comonadic.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity.Const.imply xv.linearity yv.linearity;
      portability = Portability.Const.imply xv.portability yv.portability;
      forkable = Forkable.Const.imply xv.forkable yv.forkable;
      yielding = Yielding.Const.imply xv.yielding yv.yielding;
      statefulness = Statefulness.Const.imply xv.statefulness yv.statefulness;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~bottom:Comonadic.Const.bottom ~top:Comonadic.Const.top ~leq:Comonadic.Const.leq ~join:Comonadic.Const.join ~meet:Comonadic.Const.meet ~sub:Comonadic.Const.sub ~imply:Comonadic.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~bottom:Comonadic.Const.bottom ~top:Comonadic.Const.top ~leq:Comonadic.Const.leq ~equal:Comonadic.Const.equal ~solver_min:Comonadic.min ~solver_max:Comonadic.max ~of_const:Comonadic.of_const ~to_const_exn:Comonadic.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Comonadic.newvar_above (Comonadic.of_const value) in Comonadic.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Comonadic.newvar_below (Comonadic.of_const value) in Comonadic.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic.submode (Comonadic.of_const x) (Comonadic.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic.equate (Comonadic.of_const x) (Comonadic.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Comonadic.newvar () in Comonadic.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Comonadic.newvar () in Comonadic.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic.Solver.linearity" ~product_values:values_comonadic ~field_values:values_linearity ~product_of_const:Comonadic.of_const ~field_of_const:Linearity.of_const ~field_to_const:Linearity.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic.proj_linearity ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Comonadic.min_with_linearity x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic.max_with_linearity x)) ~newvar:Comonadic.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Linearity.equate x (Linearity.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic.Const.linearity ~field_bot:Comonadic.Const.linearity_bot ~field_top:Comonadic.Const.linearity_top ~product_show:Comonadic.Const.show ~field_show:Linearity.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic.Solver.portability" ~product_values:values_comonadic ~field_values:values_portability ~product_of_const:Comonadic.of_const ~field_of_const:Portability.of_const ~field_to_const:Portability.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic.proj_portability ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Comonadic.min_with_portability x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic.max_with_portability x)) ~newvar:Comonadic.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Portability.equate x (Portability.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic.Const.portability ~field_bot:Comonadic.Const.portability_bot ~field_top:Comonadic.Const.portability_top ~product_show:Comonadic.Const.show ~field_show:Portability.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic.Solver.forkable" ~product_values:values_comonadic ~field_values:values_forkable ~product_of_const:Comonadic.of_const ~field_of_const:Forkable.of_const ~field_to_const:Forkable.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic.proj_forkable ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Comonadic.min_with_forkable x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic.max_with_forkable x)) ~newvar:Comonadic.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Forkable.equate x (Forkable.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic.Const.forkable ~field_bot:Comonadic.Const.forkable_bot ~field_top:Comonadic.Const.forkable_top ~product_show:Comonadic.Const.show ~field_show:Forkable.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic.Solver.yielding" ~product_values:values_comonadic ~field_values:values_yielding ~product_of_const:Comonadic.of_const ~field_of_const:Yielding.of_const ~field_to_const:Yielding.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic.proj_yielding ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Comonadic.min_with_yielding x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic.max_with_yielding x)) ~newvar:Comonadic.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Yielding.equate x (Yielding.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic.Const.yielding ~field_bot:Comonadic.Const.yielding_bot ~field_top:Comonadic.Const.yielding_top ~product_show:Comonadic.Const.show ~field_show:Yielding.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic.Solver.statefulness" ~product_values:values_comonadic ~field_values:values_statefulness ~product_of_const:Comonadic.of_const ~field_of_const:Statefulness.of_const ~field_to_const:Statefulness.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic.proj_statefulness ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Comonadic.min_with_statefulness x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic.max_with_statefulness x)) ~newvar:Comonadic.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Statefulness.equate x (Statefulness.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic.Const.statefulness ~field_bot:Comonadic.Const.statefulness_bot ~field_top:Comonadic.Const.statefulness_top ~product_show:Comonadic.Const.show ~field_show:Statefulness.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Comonadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity_op.Const.bottom;
      portability = Portability_op.Const.bottom;
      forkable = Forkable_op.Const.bottom;
      yielding = Yielding_op.Const.bottom;
      statefulness = Statefulness_op.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Comonadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity_op.Const.top;
      portability = Portability_op.Const.top;
      forkable = Forkable_op.Const.top;
      yielding = Yielding_op.Const.top;
      statefulness = Statefulness_op.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Comonadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic_op.Const.view y in
    Linearity_op.Const.leq xv.linearity yv.linearity
    && Portability_op.Const.leq xv.portability yv.portability
    && Forkable_op.Const.leq xv.forkable yv.forkable
    && Yielding_op.Const.leq xv.yielding yv.yielding
    && Statefulness_op.Const.leq xv.statefulness yv.statefulness
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Comonadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic_op.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity_op.Const.join xv.linearity yv.linearity;
      portability = Portability_op.Const.join xv.portability yv.portability;
      forkable = Forkable_op.Const.join xv.forkable yv.forkable;
      yielding = Yielding_op.Const.join xv.yielding yv.yielding;
      statefulness = Statefulness_op.Const.join xv.statefulness yv.statefulness;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Comonadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic_op.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity_op.Const.meet xv.linearity yv.linearity;
      portability = Portability_op.Const.meet xv.portability yv.portability;
      forkable = Forkable_op.Const.meet xv.forkable yv.forkable;
      yielding = Yielding_op.Const.meet xv.yielding yv.yielding;
      statefulness = Statefulness_op.Const.meet xv.statefulness yv.statefulness;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Comonadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic_op.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity_op.Const.sub xv.linearity yv.linearity;
      portability = Portability_op.Const.sub xv.portability yv.portability;
      forkable = Forkable_op.Const.sub xv.forkable yv.forkable;
      yielding = Yielding_op.Const.sub xv.yielding yv.yielding;
      statefulness = Statefulness_op.Const.sub xv.statefulness yv.statefulness;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Comonadic_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Comonadic_op.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_op.Const.of_view
    {
      linearity = Linearity_op.Const.imply xv.linearity yv.linearity;
      portability = Portability_op.Const.imply xv.portability yv.portability;
      forkable = Forkable_op.Const.imply xv.forkable yv.forkable;
      yielding = Yielding_op.Const.imply xv.yielding yv.yielding;
      statefulness = Statefulness_op.Const.imply xv.statefulness yv.statefulness;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Comonadic_op" ~values:values_comonadic_op ~bottom:Comonadic_op.Const.bottom ~top:Comonadic_op.Const.top ~leq:Comonadic_op.Const.leq ~join:Comonadic_op.Const.join ~meet:Comonadic_op.Const.meet ~sub:Comonadic_op.Const.sub ~imply:Comonadic_op.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Comonadic_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_op.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Comonadic_op" ~values:values_comonadic_op ~bottom:Comonadic_op.Const.bottom ~top:Comonadic_op.Const.top ~leq:Comonadic_op.Const.leq ~equal:Comonadic_op.Const.equal ~solver_min:Comonadic_op.min ~solver_max:Comonadic_op.max ~of_const:Comonadic_op.of_const ~to_const_exn:Comonadic_op.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Comonadic_op.newvar_above (Comonadic_op.of_const value) in Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Comonadic_op.newvar_below (Comonadic_op.of_const value) in Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic_op.submode (Comonadic_op.of_const x) (Comonadic_op.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic_op.equate (Comonadic_op.of_const x) (Comonadic_op.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Comonadic_op.newvar () in Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Comonadic_op.newvar () in Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Comonadic_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic_op.Solver.linearity" ~product_values:values_comonadic_op ~field_values:values_linearity_op ~product_of_const:Comonadic_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Linearity_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Linearity_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic_op.proj_linearity ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Comonadic_op.min_with_linearity x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic_op.max_with_linearity x)) ~newvar:Comonadic_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Linearity_op.equate x (Linearity_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic_op.Const.linearity ~field_bot:Comonadic_op.Const.linearity_bot ~field_top:Comonadic_op.Const.linearity_top ~product_show:Comonadic_op.Const.show ~field_show:Linearity_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic_op.Solver.portability" ~product_values:values_comonadic_op ~field_values:values_portability_op ~product_of_const:Comonadic_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Portability_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Portability_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic_op.proj_portability ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Comonadic_op.min_with_portability x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic_op.max_with_portability x)) ~newvar:Comonadic_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Portability_op.equate x (Portability_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic_op.Const.portability ~field_bot:Comonadic_op.Const.portability_bot ~field_top:Comonadic_op.Const.portability_top ~product_show:Comonadic_op.Const.show ~field_show:Portability_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic_op.Solver.forkable" ~product_values:values_comonadic_op ~field_values:values_forkable_op ~product_of_const:Comonadic_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Forkable_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Forkable_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic_op.proj_forkable ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Comonadic_op.min_with_forkable x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic_op.max_with_forkable x)) ~newvar:Comonadic_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Forkable_op.equate x (Forkable_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic_op.Const.forkable ~field_bot:Comonadic_op.Const.forkable_bot ~field_top:Comonadic_op.Const.forkable_top ~product_show:Comonadic_op.Const.show ~field_show:Forkable_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic_op.Solver.yielding" ~product_values:values_comonadic_op ~field_values:values_yielding_op ~product_of_const:Comonadic_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Yielding_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Yielding_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic_op.proj_yielding ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Comonadic_op.min_with_yielding x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic_op.max_with_yielding x)) ~newvar:Comonadic_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Yielding_op.equate x (Yielding_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic_op.Const.yielding ~field_bot:Comonadic_op.Const.yielding_bot ~field_top:Comonadic_op.Const.yielding_top ~product_show:Comonadic_op.Const.show ~field_show:Yielding_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Comonadic_op.Solver.statefulness" ~product_values:values_comonadic_op ~field_values:values_statefulness_op ~product_of_const:Comonadic_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Statefulness_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Statefulness_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Comonadic_op.proj_statefulness ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Comonadic_op.min_with_statefulness x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Comonadic_op.max_with_statefulness x)) ~newvar:Comonadic_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Statefulness_op.equate x (Statefulness_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Comonadic_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Comonadic_op.Const.statefulness ~field_bot:Comonadic_op.Const.statefulness_bot ~field_top:Comonadic_op.Const.statefulness_top ~product_show:Comonadic_op.Const.show ~field_show:Statefulness_op.Const.show;
  check_product_roundtrip ~name:"Comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~view:Comonadic.Const.view ~of_view:Comonadic.Const.of_view ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  iter1 values_comonadic (fun value ->
    let made = Comonadic.Const.make ~linearity:(Comonadic.Const.linearity value) ~portability:(Comonadic.Const.portability value) ~forkable:(Comonadic.Const.forkable value) ~yielding:(Comonadic.Const.yielding value) ~statefulness:(Comonadic.Const.statefulness value) in
    check_valid ~name:"Comonadic" ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show made;
    ensure (made = value) "Comonadic: make/projection roundtrip failed");
  check_field_projection ~name:"Comonadic.linearity" ~product_values:values_comonadic ~field_values:values_linearity ~product_leq:Comonadic.Const.leq ~field_leq:Linearity.Const.leq ~field:Comonadic.Const.linearity ~with_field:Comonadic.Const.with_linearity ~field_bot:Comonadic.Const.linearity_bot ~field_top:Comonadic.Const.linearity_top ~product_to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Comonadic.Const.show ~field_to_int:Linearity.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Linearity.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Linearity.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic.proj_linearity" ~values:values_comonadic ~f:Comonadic.Const.proj_linearity ~g:Comonadic.Const.linearity ~to_int:Linearity.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Linearity.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Linearity.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic.min_with_linearity" ~values:values_linearity ~f:Comonadic.Const.min_with_linearity ~g:Comonadic.Const.linearity_bot ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic.max_with_linearity" ~values:values_linearity ~f:Comonadic.Const.max_with_linearity ~g:Comonadic.Const.linearity_top ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic.Const.proj.linearity" ~values:values_comonadic ~f:(Comonadic.Const.proj Comonadic.Axis.Linearity) ~g:Comonadic.Const.linearity ~to_int:Linearity.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Linearity.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Linearity.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic.Const.min_with.linearity" ~values:values_linearity ~f:(Comonadic.Const.min_with Comonadic.Axis.Linearity) ~g:Comonadic.Const.linearity_bot ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic.Const.max_with.linearity" ~values:values_linearity ~f:(Comonadic.Const.max_with Comonadic.Axis.Linearity) ~g:Comonadic.Const.linearity_top ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Comonadic.portability" ~product_values:values_comonadic ~field_values:values_portability ~product_leq:Comonadic.Const.leq ~field_leq:Portability.Const.leq ~field:Comonadic.Const.portability ~with_field:Comonadic.Const.with_portability ~field_bot:Comonadic.Const.portability_bot ~field_top:Comonadic.Const.portability_top ~product_to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Comonadic.Const.show ~field_to_int:Portability.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Portability.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Portability.Const.show;

  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic.min_with_portability" ~values:values_portability ~f:Comonadic.Const.min_with_portability ~g:Comonadic.Const.portability_bot ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;

  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic.Const.max_with.portability" ~values:values_portability ~f:(Comonadic.Const.max_with Comonadic.Axis.Portability) ~g:Comonadic.Const.portability_top ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Comonadic.forkable" ~product_values:values_comonadic ~field_values:values_forkable ~product_leq:Comonadic.Const.leq ~field_leq:Forkable.Const.leq ~field:Comonadic.Const.forkable ~with_field:Comonadic.Const.with_forkable ~field_bot:Comonadic.Const.forkable_bot ~field_top:Comonadic.Const.forkable_top ~product_to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Comonadic.Const.show ~field_to_int:Forkable.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Forkable.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Forkable.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic.proj_forkable" ~values:values_comonadic ~f:Comonadic.Const.proj_forkable ~g:Comonadic.Const.forkable ~to_int:Forkable.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Forkable.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Forkable.Const.show;
