  check_product_roundtrip ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality" ~values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~view:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.view ~of_view:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.of_view ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  iter1 values_comonadic_with_regionality (fun value ->
    let made = Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.make ~areality:(Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality value) ~comonadic:(Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic value) in
    check_valid ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality" ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show made;
    ensure (made = value) "Comonadic_with_regionality: make/projection roundtrip failed");
  check_field_projection ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.areality" ~product_values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~field_values:values_regionality ~product_leq:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.leq ~field_leq:Regionality.Const.leq ~field:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality ~with_field:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.with_areality ~field_bot:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality_bot ~field_top:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality_top ~product_to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show ~field_to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.proj_areality" ~values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~f:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.proj_areality ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality ~to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.min_with_areality" ~values:values_regionality ~f:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.min_with_areality ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality_bot ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.max_with_areality" ~values:values_regionality ~f:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.max_with_areality ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality_top ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.proj.areality" ~values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~f:(Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.proj Comonadic_with_regionality.Axis.Areality) ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality ~to_int:Regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.min_with.areality" ~values:values_regionality ~f:(Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.min_with Comonadic_with_regionality.Axis.Areality) ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality_bot ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.max_with.areality" ~values:values_regionality ~f:(Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.max_with Comonadic_with_regionality.Axis.Areality) ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.areality_top ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.comonadic" ~product_values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~field_values:values_comonadic ~product_leq:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.leq ~field_leq:Comonadic.Const.leq ~field:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic ~with_field:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.with_comonadic ~field_bot:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic_bot ~field_top:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic_top ~product_to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show ~field_to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.proj_comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~f:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.proj_comonadic ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.min_with_comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~f:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.min_with_comonadic ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic_bot ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.max_with_comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~f:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.max_with_comonadic ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic_top ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.proj.comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~f:(Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.proj Comonadic_with_regionality.Axis.Comonadic) ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic ~to_int:Comonadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.min_with.comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~f:(Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.min_with Comonadic_with_regionality.Axis.Comonadic) ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic_bot ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.max_with.comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic ~f:(Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.max_with Comonadic_with_regionality.Axis.Comonadic) ~g:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.comonadic_top ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  ()

let () =
  check_repr ~name:"Value" ~values:values_value ~mask:Value.Const.Repr.mask ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Value" ~values:values_value ~bottom:Value.Const.bottom ~top:Value.Const.top ~leq:Value.Const.leq ~join:Value.Const.join ~meet:Value.Const.meet ~sub:Value.Const.sub ~imply:Value.Const.imply ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Value_op" ~values:values_value_op ~bottom:Value_op.Const.bottom ~top:Value_op.Const.top ~leq:Value_op.Const.leq ~join:Value_op.Const.join ~meet:Value_op.Const.meet ~sub:Value_op.Const.sub ~imply:Value_op.Const.imply ~to_int:Value_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value_op.Const.show;
  check_duality ~name:"Value" ~values:values_value ~bottom:Value.Const.bottom ~top:Value.Const.top ~join:Value.Const.join ~meet:Value.Const.meet ~sub:Value.Const.sub ~imply:Value.Const.imply ~op_bottom:Value_op.Const.bottom ~op_top:Value_op.Const.top ~op_join:Value_op.Const.join ~op_meet:Value_op.Const.meet ~op_sub:Value_op.Const.sub ~op_imply:Value_op.Const.imply ~show:Value.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Value.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.bottom;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Value.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.top;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Value.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.leq xv.comonadic yv.comonadic
    && Monadic.Const.leq xv.monadic yv.monadic
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Value.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value.Const.view y in
    Value.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.join xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.join xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Value.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value.Const.view y in
    Value.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.meet xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.meet xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Value.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value.Const.view y in
    Value.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.sub xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.sub xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Value.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value.Const.view y in
    Value.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.imply xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.imply xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Value" ~values:values_value ~bottom:Value.Const.bottom ~top:Value.Const.top ~leq:Value.Const.leq ~join:Value.Const.join ~meet:Value.Const.meet ~sub:Value.Const.sub ~imply:Value.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Value" ~values:values_value ~bottom:Value.Const.bottom ~top:Value.Const.top ~leq:Value.Const.leq ~equal:Value.Const.equal ~solver_min:Value.min ~solver_max:Value.max ~of_const:Value.of_const ~to_const_exn:Value.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Value.newvar_above (Value.of_const value) in Value.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Value.newvar_below (Value.of_const value) in Value.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Value.submode (Value.of_const x) (Value.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Value.equate (Value.of_const x) (Value.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Value.newvar () in Value.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Value.newvar () in Value.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Value.Solver.comonadic" ~product_values:values_value ~field_values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~product_of_const:Value.of_const ~field_of_const:Comonadic_with_regionality.of_const ~field_to_const:Comonadic_with_regionality.to_const_exn ~proj:Value.proj_comonadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Value.zap_to_floor (Value.min_with_comonadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Value.zap_to_ceil (Value.max_with_comonadic x)) ~newvar:Value.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic_with_regionality.equate x (Comonadic_with_regionality.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Value.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Value.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Value.Const.comonadic ~field_bot:Value.Const.comonadic_bot ~field_top:Value.Const.comonadic_top ~product_show:Value.Const.show ~field_show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Value.Solver.monadic" ~product_values:values_value ~field_values:values_monadic ~product_of_const:Value.of_const ~field_of_const:Monadic.of_const ~field_to_const:Monadic.to_const_exn ~proj:Value.proj_monadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Value.zap_to_floor (Value.min_with_monadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Value.zap_to_ceil (Value.max_with_monadic x)) ~newvar:Value.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Monadic.equate x (Monadic.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Value.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Value.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Value.Const.monadic ~field_bot:Value.Const.monadic_bot ~field_top:Value.Const.monadic_top ~product_show:Value.Const.show ~field_show:Monadic.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Value_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Const.bottom;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Value_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Const.top;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Value_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value_op.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Const.leq xv.comonadic yv.comonadic
    && Monadic_op.Const.leq xv.monadic yv.monadic
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Value_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value_op.Const.view y in
    Value_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Const.join xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.join xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Value_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value_op.Const.view y in
    Value_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Const.meet xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.meet xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Value_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value_op.Const.view y in
    Value_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Const.sub xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.sub xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Value_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Value_op.Const.view y in
    Value_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Const.imply xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.imply xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Value_op" ~values:values_value_op ~bottom:Value_op.Const.bottom ~top:Value_op.Const.top ~leq:Value_op.Const.leq ~join:Value_op.Const.join ~meet:Value_op.Const.meet ~sub:Value_op.Const.sub ~imply:Value_op.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Value_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value_op.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Value_op" ~values:values_value_op ~bottom:Value_op.Const.bottom ~top:Value_op.Const.top ~leq:Value_op.Const.leq ~equal:Value_op.Const.equal ~solver_min:Value_op.min ~solver_max:Value_op.max ~of_const:Value_op.of_const ~to_const_exn:Value_op.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Value_op.newvar_above (Value_op.of_const value) in Value_op.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Value_op.newvar_below (Value_op.of_const value) in Value_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Value_op.submode (Value_op.of_const x) (Value_op.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Value_op.equate (Value_op.of_const x) (Value_op.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Value_op.newvar () in Value_op.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Value_op.newvar () in Value_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Value_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Value_op.Solver.comonadic" ~product_values:values_value_op ~field_values:values_comonadic_with_regionality_op ~product_of_const:Value_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Comonadic_with_regionality_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Comonadic_with_regionality_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Value_op.proj_comonadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Value_op.zap_to_floor (Value_op.min_with_comonadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Value_op.zap_to_ceil (Value_op.max_with_comonadic x)) ~newvar:Value_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic_with_regionality_op.equate x (Comonadic_with_regionality_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Value_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Value_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Value_op.Const.comonadic ~field_bot:Value_op.Const.comonadic_bot ~field_top:Value_op.Const.comonadic_top ~product_show:Value_op.Const.show ~field_show:Comonadic_with_regionality_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Value_op.Solver.monadic" ~product_values:values_value_op ~field_values:values_monadic_op ~product_of_const:Value_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Monadic_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Monadic_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Value_op.proj_monadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Value_op.zap_to_floor (Value_op.min_with_monadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Value_op.zap_to_ceil (Value_op.max_with_monadic x)) ~newvar:Value_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Monadic_op.equate x (Monadic_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Value_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Value_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Value_op.Const.monadic ~field_bot:Value_op.Const.monadic_bot ~field_top:Value_op.Const.monadic_top ~product_show:Value_op.Const.show ~field_show:Monadic_op.Const.show;
  check_product_roundtrip ~name:"Value" ~values:values_value ~view:Value.Const.view ~of_view:Value.Const.of_view ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  iter1 values_value (fun value ->
    let made = Value.Const.make ~comonadic:(Value.Const.comonadic value) ~monadic:(Value.Const.monadic value) in
    check_valid ~name:"Value" ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show made;
    ensure (made = value) "Value: make/projection roundtrip failed");
  check_field_projection ~name:"Value.comonadic" ~product_values:values_value ~field_values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~product_leq:Value.Const.leq ~field_leq:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.leq ~field:Value.Const.comonadic ~with_field:Value.Const.with_comonadic ~field_bot:Value.Const.comonadic_bot ~field_top:Value.Const.comonadic_top ~product_to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Value.Const.show ~field_to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.proj_comonadic" ~values:values_value ~f:Value.Const.proj_comonadic ~g:Value.Const.comonadic ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.min_with_comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~f:Value.Const.min_with_comonadic ~g:Value.Const.comonadic_bot ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.max_with_comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~f:Value.Const.max_with_comonadic ~g:Value.Const.comonadic_top ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.Const.proj.comonadic" ~values:values_value ~f:(Value.Const.proj Value.Axis.Comonadic) ~g:Value.Const.comonadic ~to_int:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_regionality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.Const.min_with.comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~f:(Value.Const.min_with Value.Axis.Comonadic) ~g:Value.Const.comonadic_bot ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.Const.max_with.comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_regionality ~f:(Value.Const.max_with Value.Axis.Comonadic) ~g:Value.Const.comonadic_top ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Value.monadic" ~product_values:values_value ~field_values:values_monadic ~product_leq:Value.Const.leq ~field_leq:Monadic.Const.leq ~field:Value.Const.monadic ~with_field:Value.Const.with_monadic ~field_bot:Value.Const.monadic_bot ~field_top:Value.Const.monadic_top ~product_to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Value.Const.show ~field_to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.proj_monadic" ~values:values_value ~f:Value.Const.proj_monadic ~g:Value.Const.monadic ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.min_with_monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~f:Value.Const.min_with_monadic ~g:Value.Const.monadic_bot ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.max_with_monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~f:Value.Const.max_with_monadic ~g:Value.Const.monadic_top ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.Const.proj.monadic" ~values:values_value ~f:(Value.Const.proj Value.Axis.Monadic) ~g:Value.Const.monadic ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.Const.min_with.monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~f:(Value.Const.min_with Value.Axis.Monadic) ~g:Value.Const.monadic_bot ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Value.Const.max_with.monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~f:(Value.Const.max_with Value.Axis.Monadic) ~g:Value.Const.monadic_top ~to_int:Value.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Value.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Value.Const.show;
  ()

let () =
  check_repr ~name:"Alloc" ~values:values_alloc ~mask:Alloc.Const.Repr.mask ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Alloc" ~values:values_alloc ~bottom:Alloc.Const.bottom ~top:Alloc.Const.top ~leq:Alloc.Const.leq ~join:Alloc.Const.join ~meet:Alloc.Const.meet ~sub:Alloc.Const.sub ~imply:Alloc.Const.imply ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Alloc_op" ~values:values_alloc_op ~bottom:Alloc_op.Const.bottom ~top:Alloc_op.Const.top ~leq:Alloc_op.Const.leq ~join:Alloc_op.Const.join ~meet:Alloc_op.Const.meet ~sub:Alloc_op.Const.sub ~imply:Alloc_op.Const.imply ~to_int:Alloc_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc_op.Const.show;
  check_duality ~name:"Alloc" ~values:values_alloc ~bottom:Alloc.Const.bottom ~top:Alloc.Const.top ~join:Alloc.Const.join ~meet:Alloc.Const.meet ~sub:Alloc.Const.sub ~imply:Alloc.Const.imply ~op_bottom:Alloc_op.Const.bottom ~op_top:Alloc_op.Const.top ~op_join:Alloc_op.Const.join ~op_meet:Alloc_op.Const.meet ~op_sub:Alloc_op.Const.sub ~op_imply:Alloc_op.Const.imply ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Alloc.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.bottom;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Alloc.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.top;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Alloc.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_with_locality.Const.leq xv.comonadic yv.comonadic
    && Monadic.Const.leq xv.monadic yv.monadic
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Alloc.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc.Const.view y in
    Alloc.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.join xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.join xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Alloc.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc.Const.view y in
    Alloc.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.meet xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.meet xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Alloc.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc.Const.view y in
    Alloc.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.sub xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.sub xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Alloc.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc.Const.view y in
    Alloc.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.imply xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.imply xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Alloc" ~values:values_alloc ~bottom:Alloc.Const.bottom ~top:Alloc.Const.top ~leq:Alloc.Const.leq ~join:Alloc.Const.join ~meet:Alloc.Const.meet ~sub:Alloc.Const.sub ~imply:Alloc.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Alloc" ~values:values_alloc ~bottom:Alloc.Const.bottom ~top:Alloc.Const.top ~leq:Alloc.Const.leq ~equal:Alloc.Const.equal ~solver_min:Alloc.min ~solver_max:Alloc.max ~of_const:Alloc.of_const ~to_const_exn:Alloc.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Alloc.newvar_above (Alloc.of_const value) in Alloc.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Alloc.newvar_below (Alloc.of_const value) in Alloc.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Alloc.submode (Alloc.of_const x) (Alloc.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Alloc.equate (Alloc.of_const x) (Alloc.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Alloc.newvar () in Alloc.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Alloc.newvar () in Alloc.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Alloc.Solver.comonadic" ~product_values:values_alloc ~field_values:values_comonadic_with_locality ~product_of_const:Alloc.of_const ~field_of_const:Comonadic_with_locality.of_const ~field_to_const:Comonadic_with_locality.to_const_exn ~proj:Alloc.proj_comonadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Alloc.zap_to_floor (Alloc.min_with_comonadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Alloc.zap_to_ceil (Alloc.max_with_comonadic x)) ~newvar:Alloc.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic_with_locality.equate x (Comonadic_with_locality.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Alloc.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Alloc.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Alloc.Const.comonadic ~field_bot:Alloc.Const.comonadic_bot ~field_top:Alloc.Const.comonadic_top ~product_show:Alloc.Const.show ~field_show:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Alloc.Solver.monadic" ~product_values:values_alloc ~field_values:values_monadic ~product_of_const:Alloc.of_const ~field_of_const:Monadic.of_const ~field_to_const:Monadic.to_const_exn ~proj:Alloc.proj_monadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Alloc.zap_to_floor (Alloc.min_with_monadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Alloc.zap_to_ceil (Alloc.max_with_monadic x)) ~newvar:Alloc.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Monadic.equate x (Monadic.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Alloc.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Alloc.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Alloc.Const.monadic ~field_bot:Alloc.Const.monadic_bot ~field_top:Alloc.Const.monadic_top ~product_show:Alloc.Const.show ~field_show:Monadic.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Alloc_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.bottom;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Alloc_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.top;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Alloc_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc_op.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.leq xv.comonadic yv.comonadic
    && Monadic_op.Const.leq xv.monadic yv.monadic
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Alloc_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc_op.Const.view y in
    Alloc_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.join xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.join xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Alloc_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc_op.Const.view y in
    Alloc_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.meet xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.meet xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Alloc_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc_op.Const.view y in
    Alloc_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.sub xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.sub xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Alloc_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Alloc_op.Const.view y in
    Alloc_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.imply xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.imply xv.monadic yv.monadic;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Alloc_op" ~values:values_alloc_op ~bottom:Alloc_op.Const.bottom ~top:Alloc_op.Const.top ~leq:Alloc_op.Const.leq ~join:Alloc_op.Const.join ~meet:Alloc_op.Const.meet ~sub:Alloc_op.Const.sub ~imply:Alloc_op.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Alloc_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc_op.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Alloc_op" ~values:values_alloc_op ~bottom:Alloc_op.Const.bottom ~top:Alloc_op.Const.top ~leq:Alloc_op.Const.leq ~equal:Alloc_op.Const.equal ~solver_min:Alloc_op.min ~solver_max:Alloc_op.max ~of_const:Alloc_op.of_const ~to_const_exn:Alloc_op.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Alloc_op.newvar_above (Alloc_op.of_const value) in Alloc_op.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Alloc_op.newvar_below (Alloc_op.of_const value) in Alloc_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Alloc_op.submode (Alloc_op.of_const x) (Alloc_op.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Alloc_op.equate (Alloc_op.of_const x) (Alloc_op.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Alloc_op.newvar () in Alloc_op.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Alloc_op.newvar () in Alloc_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Alloc_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Alloc_op.Solver.comonadic" ~product_values:values_alloc_op ~field_values:values_comonadic_with_locality_op ~product_of_const:Alloc_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Comonadic_with_locality_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Comonadic_with_locality_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Alloc_op.proj_comonadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Alloc_op.zap_to_floor (Alloc_op.min_with_comonadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Alloc_op.zap_to_ceil (Alloc_op.max_with_comonadic x)) ~newvar:Alloc_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic_with_locality_op.equate x (Comonadic_with_locality_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Alloc_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Alloc_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Alloc_op.Const.comonadic ~field_bot:Alloc_op.Const.comonadic_bot ~field_top:Alloc_op.Const.comonadic_top ~product_show:Alloc_op.Const.show ~field_show:Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Alloc_op.Solver.monadic" ~product_values:values_alloc_op ~field_values:values_monadic_op ~product_of_const:Alloc_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Monadic_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Monadic_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Alloc_op.proj_monadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Alloc_op.zap_to_floor (Alloc_op.min_with_monadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Alloc_op.zap_to_ceil (Alloc_op.max_with_monadic x)) ~newvar:Alloc_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Monadic_op.equate x (Monadic_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Alloc_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Alloc_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Alloc_op.Const.monadic ~field_bot:Alloc_op.Const.monadic_bot ~field_top:Alloc_op.Const.monadic_top ~product_show:Alloc_op.Const.show ~field_show:Monadic_op.Const.show;
  check_product_roundtrip ~name:"Alloc" ~values:values_alloc ~view:Alloc.Const.view ~of_view:Alloc.Const.of_view ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  iter1 values_alloc (fun value ->
    let made = Alloc.Const.make ~comonadic:(Alloc.Const.comonadic value) ~monadic:(Alloc.Const.monadic value) in
    check_valid ~name:"Alloc" ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show made;
    ensure (made = value) "Alloc: make/projection roundtrip failed");
  check_field_projection ~name:"Alloc.comonadic" ~product_values:values_alloc ~field_values:values_comonadic_with_locality ~product_leq:Alloc.Const.leq ~field_leq:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.leq ~field:Alloc.Const.comonadic ~with_field:Alloc.Const.with_comonadic ~field_bot:Alloc.Const.comonadic_bot ~field_top:Alloc.Const.comonadic_top ~product_to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Alloc.Const.show ~field_to_int:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.proj_comonadic" ~values:values_alloc ~f:Alloc.Const.proj_comonadic ~g:Alloc.Const.comonadic ~to_int:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.min_with_comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_locality ~f:Alloc.Const.min_with_comonadic ~g:Alloc.Const.comonadic_bot ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.max_with_comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_locality ~f:Alloc.Const.max_with_comonadic ~g:Alloc.Const.comonadic_top ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.Const.proj.comonadic" ~values:values_alloc ~f:(Alloc.Const.proj Alloc.Axis.Comonadic) ~g:Alloc.Const.comonadic ~to_int:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.Const.min_with.comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_locality ~f:(Alloc.Const.min_with Alloc.Axis.Comonadic) ~g:Alloc.Const.comonadic_bot ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.Const.max_with.comonadic" ~values:values_comonadic_with_locality ~f:(Alloc.Const.max_with Alloc.Axis.Comonadic) ~g:Alloc.Const.comonadic_top ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Alloc.monadic" ~product_values:values_alloc ~field_values:values_monadic ~product_leq:Alloc.Const.leq ~field_leq:Monadic.Const.leq ~field:Alloc.Const.monadic ~with_field:Alloc.Const.with_monadic ~field_bot:Alloc.Const.monadic_bot ~field_top:Alloc.Const.monadic_top ~product_to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Alloc.Const.show ~field_to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.proj_monadic" ~values:values_alloc ~f:Alloc.Const.proj_monadic ~g:Alloc.Const.monadic ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.min_with_monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~f:Alloc.Const.min_with_monadic ~g:Alloc.Const.monadic_bot ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.max_with_monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~f:Alloc.Const.max_with_monadic ~g:Alloc.Const.monadic_top ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.Const.proj.monadic" ~values:values_alloc ~f:(Alloc.Const.proj Alloc.Axis.Monadic) ~g:Alloc.Const.monadic ~to_int:Monadic.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Monadic.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Monadic.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.Const.min_with.monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~f:(Alloc.Const.min_with Alloc.Axis.Monadic) ~g:Alloc.Const.monadic_bot ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Alloc.Const.max_with.monadic" ~values:values_monadic ~f:(Alloc.Const.max_with Alloc.Axis.Monadic) ~g:Alloc.Const.monadic_top ~to_int:Alloc.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Alloc.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Alloc.Const.show;
  ()

let () =
  check_repr ~name:"Scannable_axes" ~values:values_scannable_axes ~mask:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.mask ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Scannable_axes" ~values:values_scannable_axes ~bottom:Scannable_axes.Const.bottom ~top:Scannable_axes.Const.top ~leq:Scannable_axes.Const.leq ~join:Scannable_axes.Const.join ~meet:Scannable_axes.Const.meet ~sub:Scannable_axes.Const.sub ~imply:Scannable_axes.Const.imply ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Scannable_axes_op" ~values:values_scannable_axes_op ~bottom:Scannable_axes_op.Const.bottom ~top:Scannable_axes_op.Const.top ~leq:Scannable_axes_op.Const.leq ~join:Scannable_axes_op.Const.join ~meet:Scannable_axes_op.Const.meet ~sub:Scannable_axes_op.Const.sub ~imply:Scannable_axes_op.Const.imply ~to_int:Scannable_axes_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes_op.Const.show;
  check_duality ~name:"Scannable_axes" ~values:values_scannable_axes ~bottom:Scannable_axes.Const.bottom ~top:Scannable_axes.Const.top ~join:Scannable_axes.Const.join ~meet:Scannable_axes.Const.meet ~sub:Scannable_axes.Const.sub ~imply:Scannable_axes.Const.imply ~op_bottom:Scannable_axes_op.Const.bottom ~op_top:Scannable_axes_op.Const.top ~op_join:Scannable_axes_op.Const.join ~op_meet:Scannable_axes_op.Const.meet ~op_sub:Scannable_axes_op.Const.sub ~op_imply:Scannable_axes_op.Const.imply ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Scannable_axes.Const.of_view
    {
      externality = Externality.Const.bottom;
      nullability = Nullability.Const.bottom;
      separability = Separability.Const.bottom;
      pointerness = Pointerness.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Scannable_axes.Const.of_view
    {
      externality = Externality.Const.top;
      nullability = Nullability.Const.top;
      separability = Separability.Const.top;
      pointerness = Pointerness.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Scannable_axes.Const.view x in
    let yv = Scannable_axes.Const.view y in
    Externality.Const.leq xv.externality yv.externality
    && Nullability.Const.leq xv.nullability yv.nullability
    && Separability.Const.leq xv.separability yv.separability
    && Pointerness.Const.leq xv.pointerness yv.pointerness
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Scannable_axes.Const.view x in
    let yv = Scannable_axes.Const.view y in
    Scannable_axes.Const.of_view
    {
      externality = Externality.Const.join xv.externality yv.externality;

  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.Const.max_with.nullability" ~values:values_nullability ~f:(Scannable_axes.Const.max_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Nullability) ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.nullability_top ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Scannable_axes.separability" ~product_values:values_scannable_axes ~field_values:values_separability ~product_leq:Scannable_axes.Const.leq ~field_leq:Separability.Const.leq ~field:Scannable_axes.Const.separability ~with_field:Scannable_axes.Const.with_separability ~field_bot:Scannable_axes.Const.separability_bot ~field_top:Scannable_axes.Const.separability_top ~product_to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Scannable_axes.Const.show ~field_to_int:Separability.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Separability.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Separability.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.proj_separability" ~values:values_scannable_axes ~f:Scannable_axes.Const.proj_separability ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.separability ~to_int:Separability.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Separability.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Separability.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.min_with_separability" ~values:values_separability ~f:Scannable_axes.Const.min_with_separability ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.separability_bot ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.max_with_separability" ~values:values_separability ~f:Scannable_axes.Const.max_with_separability ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.separability_top ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.Const.proj.separability" ~values:values_scannable_axes ~f:(Scannable_axes.Const.proj Scannable_axes.Axis.Separability) ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.separability ~to_int:Separability.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Separability.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Separability.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.Const.min_with.separability" ~values:values_separability ~f:(Scannable_axes.Const.min_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Separability) ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.separability_bot ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.Const.max_with.separability" ~values:values_separability ~f:(Scannable_axes.Const.max_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Separability) ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.separability_top ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  check_field_projection ~name:"Scannable_axes.pointerness" ~product_values:values_scannable_axes ~field_values:values_pointerness ~product_leq:Scannable_axes.Const.leq ~field_leq:Pointerness.Const.leq ~field:Scannable_axes.Const.pointerness ~with_field:Scannable_axes.Const.with_pointerness ~field_bot:Scannable_axes.Const.pointerness_bot ~field_top:Scannable_axes.Const.pointerness_top ~product_to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~product_of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~product_show:Scannable_axes.Const.show ~field_to_int:Pointerness.Const.Repr.to_int ~field_of_int_exn:Pointerness.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~field_show:Pointerness.Const.show;

  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.max_with_pointerness" ~values:values_pointerness ~f:Scannable_axes.Const.max_with_pointerness ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.pointerness_top ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.Const.proj.pointerness" ~values:values_scannable_axes ~f:(Scannable_axes.Const.proj Scannable_axes.Axis.Pointerness) ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.pointerness ~to_int:Pointerness.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Pointerness.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Pointerness.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.Const.min_with.pointerness" ~values:values_pointerness ~f:(Scannable_axes.Const.min_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Pointerness) ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.pointerness_bot ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  check_function_equality ~name:"Scannable_axes.Const.max_with.pointerness" ~values:values_pointerness ~f:(Scannable_axes.Const.max_with Scannable_axes.Axis.Pointerness) ~g:Scannable_axes.Const.pointerness_top ~to_int:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Scannable_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  ()

let () =
  check_repr ~name:"Kind_axes" ~values:values_kind_axes ~mask:Kind_axes.Const.Repr.mask ~to_int:Kind_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Kind_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Kind_axes.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Kind_axes" ~values:values_kind_axes ~bottom:Kind_axes.Const.bottom ~top:Kind_axes.Const.top ~leq:Kind_axes.Const.leq ~join:Kind_axes.Const.join ~meet:Kind_axes.Const.meet ~sub:Kind_axes.Const.sub ~imply:Kind_axes.Const.imply ~to_int:Kind_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Kind_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Kind_axes.Const.show;
  check_lattice ~name:"Kind_axes_op" ~values:values_kind_axes_op ~bottom:Kind_axes_op.Const.bottom ~top:Kind_axes_op.Const.top ~leq:Kind_axes_op.Const.leq ~join:Kind_axes_op.Const.join ~meet:Kind_axes_op.Const.meet ~sub:Kind_axes_op.Const.sub ~imply:Kind_axes_op.Const.imply ~to_int:Kind_axes_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Kind_axes_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Kind_axes_op.Const.show;
  check_duality ~name:"Kind_axes" ~values:values_kind_axes ~bottom:Kind_axes.Const.bottom ~top:Kind_axes.Const.top ~join:Kind_axes.Const.join ~meet:Kind_axes.Const.meet ~sub:Kind_axes.Const.sub ~imply:Kind_axes.Const.imply ~op_bottom:Kind_axes_op.Const.bottom ~op_top:Kind_axes_op.Const.top ~op_join:Kind_axes_op.Const.join ~op_meet:Kind_axes_op.Const.meet ~op_sub:Kind_axes_op.Const.sub ~op_imply:Kind_axes_op.Const.imply ~show:Kind_axes.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Kind_axes.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.bottom;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.bottom;
      scannable = Scannable_axes.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Kind_axes.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.top;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.top;
      scannable = Scannable_axes.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_with_locality.Const.leq xv.comonadic yv.comonadic
    && Monadic_op.Const.leq xv.monadic yv.monadic
    && Scannable_axes.Const.leq xv.scannable yv.scannable
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes.Const.view y in
    Kind_axes.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.join xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.join xv.monadic yv.monadic;
      scannable = Scannable_axes.Const.join xv.scannable yv.scannable;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes.Const.view y in
    Kind_axes.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.meet xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.meet xv.monadic yv.monadic;
      scannable = Scannable_axes.Const.meet xv.scannable yv.scannable;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes.Const.view y in
    Kind_axes.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.sub xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.sub xv.monadic yv.monadic;
      scannable = Scannable_axes.Const.sub xv.scannable yv.scannable;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes.Const.view y in
    Kind_axes.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality.Const.imply xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic_op.Const.imply xv.monadic yv.monadic;
      scannable = Scannable_axes.Const.imply xv.scannable yv.scannable;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Kind_axes" ~values:values_kind_axes ~bottom:Kind_axes.Const.bottom ~top:Kind_axes.Const.top ~leq:Kind_axes.Const.leq ~join:Kind_axes.Const.join ~meet:Kind_axes.Const.meet ~sub:Kind_axes.Const.sub ~imply:Kind_axes.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Kind_axes.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Kind_axes.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Kind_axes.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Kind_axes" ~values:values_kind_axes ~bottom:Kind_axes.Const.bottom ~top:Kind_axes.Const.top ~leq:Kind_axes.Const.leq ~equal:Kind_axes.Const.equal ~solver_min:Kind_axes.min ~solver_max:Kind_axes.max ~of_const:Kind_axes.of_const ~to_const_exn:Kind_axes.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Kind_axes.newvar_above (Kind_axes.of_const value) in Kind_axes.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Kind_axes.newvar_below (Kind_axes.of_const value) in Kind_axes.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Kind_axes.submode (Kind_axes.of_const x) (Kind_axes.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Kind_axes.equate (Kind_axes.of_const x) (Kind_axes.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Kind_axes.newvar () in Kind_axes.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Kind_axes.newvar () in Kind_axes.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Kind_axes.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Kind_axes.Solver.comonadic" ~product_values:values_kind_axes ~field_values:values_comonadic_with_locality ~product_of_const:Kind_axes.of_const ~field_of_const:Comonadic_with_locality.of_const ~field_to_const:Comonadic_with_locality.to_const_exn ~proj:Kind_axes.proj_comonadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Kind_axes.zap_to_floor (Kind_axes.min_with_comonadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Kind_axes.zap_to_ceil (Kind_axes.max_with_comonadic x)) ~newvar:Kind_axes.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic_with_locality.equate x (Comonadic_with_locality.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Kind_axes.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Kind_axes.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Kind_axes.Const.comonadic ~field_bot:Kind_axes.Const.comonadic_bot ~field_top:Kind_axes.Const.comonadic_top ~product_show:Kind_axes.Const.show ~field_show:Comonadic_with_locality.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Kind_axes.Solver.monadic" ~product_values:values_kind_axes ~field_values:values_monadic_op ~product_of_const:Kind_axes.of_const ~field_of_const:Monadic_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Monadic_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Kind_axes.proj_monadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Kind_axes.zap_to_floor (Kind_axes.min_with_monadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Kind_axes.zap_to_ceil (Kind_axes.max_with_monadic x)) ~newvar:Kind_axes.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Monadic_op.equate x (Monadic_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Kind_axes.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Kind_axes.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Kind_axes.Const.monadic ~field_bot:Kind_axes.Const.monadic_bot ~field_top:Kind_axes.Const.monadic_top ~product_show:Kind_axes.Const.show ~field_show:Monadic_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Kind_axes.Solver.scannable" ~product_values:values_kind_axes ~field_values:values_scannable_axes ~product_of_const:Kind_axes.of_const ~field_of_const:Scannable_axes.of_const ~field_to_const:Scannable_axes.to_const_exn ~proj:Kind_axes.proj_scannable ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Kind_axes.zap_to_floor (Kind_axes.min_with_scannable x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Kind_axes.zap_to_ceil (Kind_axes.max_with_scannable x)) ~newvar:Kind_axes.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Scannable_axes.equate x (Scannable_axes.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Kind_axes.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Kind_axes.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Kind_axes.Const.scannable ~field_bot:Kind_axes.Const.scannable_bot ~field_top:Kind_axes.Const.scannable_top ~product_show:Kind_axes.Const.show ~field_show:Scannable_axes.Const.show;
  let ref_bottom =
    Kind_axes_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.bottom;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.bottom;
      scannable = Scannable_axes_op.Const.bottom;
    }
  in
  let ref_top =
    Kind_axes_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.top;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.top;
      scannable = Scannable_axes_op.Const.top;
    }
  in
  let ref_leq x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view y in
    Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.leq xv.comonadic yv.comonadic
    && Monadic.Const.leq xv.monadic yv.monadic
    && Scannable_axes_op.Const.leq xv.scannable yv.scannable
  in
  let ref_join x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view y in
    Kind_axes_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.join xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.join xv.monadic yv.monadic;
      scannable = Scannable_axes_op.Const.join xv.scannable yv.scannable;
    }
  in
  let ref_meet x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view y in
    Kind_axes_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.meet xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.meet xv.monadic yv.monadic;
      scannable = Scannable_axes_op.Const.meet xv.scannable yv.scannable;
    }
  in
  let ref_sub x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view y in
    Kind_axes_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.sub xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.sub xv.monadic yv.monadic;
      scannable = Scannable_axes_op.Const.sub xv.scannable yv.scannable;
    }
  in
  let ref_imply x y =
    let xv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view x in
    let yv = Kind_axes_op.Const.view y in
    Kind_axes_op.Const.of_view
    {
      comonadic = Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.imply xv.comonadic yv.comonadic;
      monadic = Monadic.Const.imply xv.monadic yv.monadic;
      scannable = Scannable_axes_op.Const.imply xv.scannable yv.scannable;
    }
  in
  check_reference_equivalence ~name:"Kind_axes_op" ~values:values_kind_axes_op ~bottom:Kind_axes_op.Const.bottom ~top:Kind_axes_op.Const.top ~leq:Kind_axes_op.Const.leq ~join:Kind_axes_op.Const.join ~meet:Kind_axes_op.Const.meet ~sub:Kind_axes_op.Const.sub ~imply:Kind_axes_op.Const.imply ~ref_bottom ~ref_top ~ref_leq ~ref_join ~ref_meet ~ref_sub ~ref_imply ~to_int:Kind_axes_op.Const.Repr.to_int ~of_int_exn:Kind_axes_op.Const.Repr.of_int_exn ~show:Kind_axes_op.Const.show;
  check_solver ~name:"Kind_axes_op" ~values:values_kind_axes_op ~bottom:Kind_axes_op.Const.bottom ~top:Kind_axes_op.Const.top ~leq:Kind_axes_op.Const.leq ~equal:Kind_axes_op.Const.equal ~solver_min:Kind_axes_op.min ~solver_max:Kind_axes_op.max ~of_const:Kind_axes_op.of_const ~to_const_exn:Kind_axes_op.to_const_exn ~floor_of_above:(fun value -> let v, _ = Kind_axes_op.newvar_above (Kind_axes_op.of_const value) in Kind_axes_op.zap_to_floor v) ~ceil_of_below:(fun value -> let v, _ = Kind_axes_op.newvar_below (Kind_axes_op.of_const value) in Kind_axes_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~submode_const:(fun x y -> Kind_axes_op.submode (Kind_axes_op.of_const x) (Kind_axes_op.of_const y)) ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Kind_axes_op.equate (Kind_axes_op.of_const x) (Kind_axes_op.of_const y)) ~fresh_floor:(fun () -> let v = Kind_axes_op.newvar () in Kind_axes_op.zap_to_floor v) ~fresh_ceil:(fun () -> let v = Kind_axes_op.newvar () in Kind_axes_op.zap_to_ceil v) ~show:Kind_axes_op.Const.show;
  check_solver_projection ~name:"Kind_axes_op.Solver.comonadic" ~product_values:values_kind_axes_op ~field_values:values_comonadic_with_locality_op ~product_of_const:Kind_axes_op.of_const ~field_of_const:Comonadic_with_locality_op.of_const ~field_to_const:Comonadic_with_locality_op.to_const_exn ~proj:Kind_axes_op.proj_comonadic ~min_with_floor:(fun x -> Kind_axes_op.zap_to_floor (Kind_axes_op.min_with_comonadic x)) ~max_with_ceil:(fun x -> Kind_axes_op.zap_to_ceil (Kind_axes_op.max_with_comonadic x)) ~newvar:Kind_axes_op.newvar ~equate_const:(fun x y -> Comonadic_with_locality_op.equate x (Comonadic_with_locality_op.of_const y)) ~zap_to_floor:(fun v -> Kind_axes_op.zap_to_floor (Obj.magic v)) ~zap_to_ceil:(fun v -> Kind_axes_op.zap_to_ceil (Obj.magic v)) ~field:Kind_axes_op.Const.comonadic ~field_bot:Kind_axes_op.Const.comonadic_bot ~field_top:Kind_axes_op.Const.comonadic_top ~product_show:Kind_axes_op.Const.show ~field_show:Comonadic_with_locality_op.Const.show;
